Bayesian Optimization with Gaussian Processes to Accelerate Stationary Point Searches
Authors: Rohit Goswami
First: 2026-03-11T17:20:28+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-11T17:20:28+00:00
Comments: 57 pages, 22 figures. Invited article for ACS Physical Chemistry Au
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Accelerating the explorations of stationary points on potential energy surfaces building local surrogates spans decades of effort. Done correctly, surrogates reduce required evaluations by an order of magnitude while preserving the accuracy of the underlying theory. We present a unified Bayesian Optimization view of minimization, single point saddle searches, and double ended saddle searches through a unified six-step surrogate loop, differing only in the inner optimization target and acquisition criterion. The framework uses Gaussian process regression with derivative observations, inverse-distance kernels, and active learning. The Optimal Transport GP extensions of farthest point sampling with Earth mover's distance, MAP regularization via variance barrier and oscillation detection, and adaptive trust radius form concrete extensions of the same basic methodology, improving accuracy and efficiency. We also demonstrate random Fourier features decouple hyperparameter training from predictions enabling favorable scaling for high-dimensional systems. Accompanying pedagogical Rust code demonstrates that all applications use the exact same Bayesian optimization loop, bridging the gap between theoretical formulation and practical execution.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于高斯过程的贝叶斯优化加速势能面驻点搜索
通过构建局部代理模型加速势能面驻点探索已历经数十年研究。正确实施的代理模型能在保持底层理论精度的同时，将所需计算量降低一个数量级。本文提出统一的贝叶斯优化框架，通过六步代理循环统一处理极小值点搜索、单点鞍点搜索和双端鞍点搜索，仅在内层优化目标和采集准则上存在差异。该框架采用含导数观测的高斯过程回归、反距离核函数及主动学习技术。通过最远点采样与推土距离的最优传输GP扩展、基于方差屏障与振荡检测的MAP正则化、自适应信任半径等具体扩展方法，在保持基础方法论一致性的同时提升了精度与效率。随机傅里叶特征的应用实现超参数训练与预测解耦，为高维系统提供优越的扩展性。配套的Rust教学代码表明所有应用均采用完全相同的贝叶斯优化循环，弥合了理论构建与实际执行间的鸿沟。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the long-standing challenge of efficiently exploring stationary points on potential energy surfaces, this paper introduces a unified Bayesian Optimization framework using Gaussian processes to accelerate such searches. The method employs a six-step surrogate loop with Gaussian process regression incorporating derivative observations, inverse-distance kernels, and active learning, extended with techniques like Optimal Transport GP for sampling and adaptive trust radius. Experimental results demonstrate that the approach reduces required evaluations by an order of magnitude while maintaining accuracy, with random Fourier features enabling scalable performance in high-dimensional systems, as validated through pedagogical code implementations.
本文针对势能面上稳定点搜索效率低下的长期挑战，提出了一种基于高斯过程的统一贝叶斯优化框架以加速此类搜索。该方法采用包含导数观测、反距离核和主动学习的六步代理循环，并通过最优传输高斯过程扩展等技术进行增强。实验结果表明，该方法在保持精度的同时将所需评估次数减少了一个数量级，其中随机傅里叶特征技术实现了高维系统的良好扩展性，相关教学代码验证了该框架的实际可行性。
Learning What Reinforcement Learning Can't: Interleaved Online Fine-Tuning for Hardest Questions
Authors: Lu Ma, Hao Liang, Meiyi Qiang, Lexiang Tang, Xiaochen Ma, Zhen Hao Wong, Junbo Niu, Chengyu Shen, Runming He, Yanhao Li, Bin Cui, Wentao Zhang
Venue: ICLR 2026
First: 2025-06-09T08:11:20+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-11T17:08:49+00:00
Comments: 12 pages, 5 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Recent advances in large language model (LLM) reasoning have shown that sophisticated behaviors such as planning and self-reflection can emerge through reinforcement learning (RL). However, despite these successes, RL in its current form remains insufficient to induce capabilities that exceed the limitations of the base model, as it is primarily optimized based on existing knowledge of the model rather than facilitating the acquisition of new information. To address this limitation, we employ supervised fine-tuning (SFT) to learn what RL cannot, which enables the incorporation of new knowledge and reasoning patterns by leveraging high-quality demonstration data. We analyze the training dynamics of RL and SFT for LLM reasoning and find that RL excels at maintaining and improving performance on questions within the model's original capabilities, while SFT is more effective at enabling progress on questions beyond the current scope of the model. Motivated by the complementary strengths of RL and SFT, we introduce a novel training approach, \textbf{ReLIFT} (\textbf{Re}inforcement \textbf{L}earning \textbf{I}nterleaved with Online \textbf{F}ine-\textbf{T}uning). In ReLIFT, the model is primarily trained using RL, but when it encounters challenging questions, high-quality solutions are collected for fine-tuning, and the training process alternates between RL and fine-tuning to enhance the model's reasoning abilities. ReLIFT achieves an average improvement of over +5.2 points across five competition-level benchmarks and one out-of-distribution benchmark compared to other zero-RL models. Furthermore, we demonstrate that ReLIFT outperforms both RL and SFT while using only 13\% of the detailed demonstration data, highlighting its scalability. These results provide compelling evidence that ReLIFT overcomes the fundamental limitations of RL and underscores the significant potential.
中文标题/摘要
标题：学习强化学习无法掌握的内容：针对最难题目的交错在线微调
近期大语言模型推理能力的进展表明，规划与自我反思等复杂行为可通过强化学习自然涌现。然而，尽管强化学习取得了一定成功，其现有形式仍不足以突破基础模型的能力上限，因为它主要基于模型已有知识进行优化，而非促进新信息的获取。为克服这一局限，我们采用监督微调来学习强化学习无法掌握的内容，通过利用高质量示范数据来整合新知识与推理模式。我们分析了大语言模型推理中强化学习与监督微调的训练动态，发现强化学习擅长维持并提升模型原有能力范围内问题的表现，而监督微调更擅长推动模型解决当前能力范围外的问题。基于强化学习与监督微调的互补优势，我们提出一种新型训练方法——\textbf{ReLIFT}（\textbf{强}化学习与在线\textbf{微}调\textbf{交}错训练）。在ReLIFT中，模型主要使用强化学习训练，但当遇到难题时，会收集高质量解决方案进行微调，训练过程在强化学习与微调间交替进行以增强模型推理能力。与其他零强化学习模型相比，ReLIFT在五个竞赛级基准和一个分布外基准上平均提升超过5.2分。此外，我们证明ReLIFT仅需13%的详细示范数据即可超越纯强化学习与监督微调，凸显其可扩展性。这些结果为ReLIFT突破强化学习的根本局限提供了有力证据，并彰显了其巨大潜力。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the limitation of reinforcement learning (RL) in enabling large language models to acquire new knowledge beyond their base capabilities, as RL primarily optimizes existing knowledge rather than facilitating learning of novel information. To overcome this, the authors propose ReLIFT, a method that interleaves RL training with online supervised fine-tuning (SFT) on high-quality solutions for challenging questions, leveraging the complementary strengths of RL for maintaining performance on within-capability tasks and SFT for enabling progress on harder, out-of-scope problems. Experimental results show that ReLIFT achieves an average improvement of over +5.2 points across five competition-level benchmarks and one out-of-distribution benchmark compared to zero-RL models, while using only 13% of demonstration data, demonstrating its effectiveness and scalability in enhancing reasoning abilities.
本文针对强化学习（RL）在大语言模型中难以超越基础模型能力、无法有效获取新知识的局限性，提出了一种新方法ReLIFT，该方法通过交替进行RL训练和在线监督微调（SFT），利用RL在维持模型原有能力任务上的优势，以及SFT在处理超出当前能力范围的难题上的有效性，从而结合两者互补优势。实验结果表明，ReLIFT在五个竞赛级基准和一个分布外基准上平均提升了超过5.2分，且仅需13%的详细演示数据，显著优于纯RL和SFT方法，证明了其在提升推理能力方面的有效性和可扩展性。
Contact Coverage-Guided Exploration for General-Purpose Dexterous Manipulation
Authors: Zixuan Liu, Ruoyi Qiao, Chenrui Tie, Xuanwei Liu, Yunfan Lou, Chongkai Gao, Zhixuan Xu, Lin Shao
First: 2026-03-11T16:55:49+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-11T16:55:49+00:00
Comments: 16 pages
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Project1
Abstract
Deep Reinforcement learning (DRL) has achieved remarkable success in domains with well-defined reward structures, such as Atari games and locomotion. In contrast, dexterous manipulation lacks general-purpose reward formulations and typically depends on task-specific, handcrafted priors to guide hand-object interactions. We propose Contact Coverage-Guided Exploration (CCGE), a general exploration method designed for general-purpose dexterous manipulation tasks. CCGE represents contact state as the intersection between object surface points and predefined hand keypoints, encouraging dexterous hands to discover diverse and novel contact patterns, namely which fingers contact which object regions. It maintains a contact counter conditioned on discretized object states obtained via learned hash codes, capturing how frequently each finger interacts with different object regions. This counter is leveraged in two complementary ways: (1) to assign a count-based contact coverage reward that promotes exploration of novel contact patterns, and (2) an energy-based reaching reward that guides the agent toward under-explored contact regions. We evaluate CCGE on a diverse set of dexterous manipulation tasks, including cluttered object singulation, constrained object retrieval, in-hand reorientation, and bimanual manipulation. Experimental results show that CCGE substantially improves training efficiency and success rates over existing exploration methods, and that the contact patterns learned with CCGE transfer robustly to real-world robotic systems. Project page is https://contact-coverage-guided-exploration.github.io.
中文标题/摘要
标题：面向通用灵巧操作的接触覆盖引导探索
深度强化学习（DRL）在奖励结构明确的领域（如Atari游戏和运动控制）已取得显著成功。相比之下，灵巧操作缺乏通用的奖励设计框架，通常依赖针对特定任务手工设计的先验知识来引导手-物体交互。本文提出接触覆盖引导探索（CCGE），一种专为通用灵巧操作任务设计的探索方法。CCGE将接触状态表征为物体表面点与预定义手部关键点的交集，激励灵巧手发现多样新颖的接触模式（即不同手指与物体区域的接触关系）。该方法通过基于学习哈希码离散化的物体状态维护接触计数器，记录各手指与不同物体区域的交互频率。该计数器通过两种互补方式被利用：（1）生成基于计数的接触覆盖奖励，促进探索新接触模式；（2）设计基于能量的趋近奖励，引导智能体探索未充分接触的区域。我们在多种灵巧操作任务上评估CCGE，包括密集物体分离、受限物体抓取、手内重定向及双手操作。实验结果表明，CCGE相比现有探索方法显著提升了训练效率与成功率，且所学接触模式能有效迁移至真实机器人系统。项目页面：https://contact-coverage-guided-exploration.github.io。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for this work is that dexterous manipulation lacks general-purpose reward formulations and often relies on task-specific priors. The proposed method, Contact Coverage-Guided Exploration (CCGE), encourages exploration by representing contact states between hand keypoints and object surfaces, maintaining a counter of contact frequencies to guide learning via a coverage reward and an energy-based reaching reward. Main experimental results on tasks like object singulation and in-hand reorientation show that CCGE substantially improves training efficiency and success rates over existing methods and transfers robustly to real-world robots.
本研究的动机在于灵巧操作缺乏通用奖励公式，通常依赖任务特定的先验知识。所提出的方法——接触覆盖引导探索（CCGE）——通过表示手部关键点与物体表面的接触状态来鼓励探索，维护一个接触频率计数器，通过覆盖奖励和基于能量的接近奖励来引导学习。在物体分离、手中重定向等任务上的主要实验结果表明，CCGE相比现有方法显著提高了训练效率和成功率，并能鲁棒地迁移到现实世界的机器人系统。
Safe RLHF Beyond Expectation: Stochastic Dominance for Universal Spectral Risk Control
Authors: Yaswanth Chittepu, Ativ Joshi, Rajarshi Bhattacharjee, Scott Niekum
First: 2026-03-11T16:24:20+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-11T16:24:20+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Safe Reinforcement Learning from Human Feedback (RLHF) typically enforces safety through expected cost constraints, but the expectation captures only a single statistic of the cost distribution and fails to account for distributional uncertainty, particularly under heavy tails or rare catastrophic events. This limitation is problematic when robustness and risk sensitivity are critical. Stochastic dominance offers a principled alternative by comparing entire cost distributions rather than just their averages, enabling direct control over tail risks and potential out-of-distribution failures that expectation-based constraints may overlook. In this work, we propose Risk-sensitive Alignment via Dominance (RAD), a novel alignment framework that replaces scalar expected cost constraints with First-Order Stochastic Dominance (FSD) constraints. We operationalize this constraint by comparing the target policy's cost distribution to that of a reference policy within an Optimal Transport (OT) framework, using entropic regularization and Sinkhorn iterations to obtain a differentiable and computationally efficient objective for stable end-to-end optimization. Furthermore, we introduce quantile-weighted FSD constraints and show that weighted FSD universally controls a broad class of Spectral Risk Measures (SRMs), so that improvements under weighted dominance imply guaranteed improvements in the corresponding spectral risk. This provides a principled mechanism for tuning a model's risk profile via the quantile weighting function. Empirical results demonstrate that RAD improves harmlessness over baselines while remaining competitive in helpfulness, and exhibits greater robustness on out-of-distribution harmlessness evaluations.
中文标题/摘要
标题：超越期望的安全RLHF：基于随机占优的通用谱风险控制
基于人类反馈的安全强化学习（RLHF）通常通过期望成本约束来确保安全性，但期望仅捕捉成本分布的单一统计量，无法处理分布不确定性，尤其在重尾或罕见灾难性事件下。当鲁棒性和风险敏感性至关重要时，这一局限尤为突出。随机占优通过比较完整成本分布而非仅其均值，提供了一种原则性替代方案，能直接控制尾部风险及基于期望约束可能忽略的潜在分布外失效。本文提出风险敏感对齐占优（RAD），一种新颖的对齐框架，用一阶随机占优（FSD）约束替代标量期望成本约束。我们通过在最优化传输（OT）框架中比较目标策略与参考策略的成本分布来实现该约束，并采用熵正则化和Sinkhorn迭代获得可微分且计算高效的目标，以进行稳定的端到端优化。此外，我们引入分位数加权FSD约束，证明加权FSD可普遍控制一大类谱风险度量（SRM），从而在加权占优下的改进意味着相应谱风险的保证提升。这为通过分位数加权函数调整模型风险特征提供了原则性机制。实验结果表明，RAD在保持助益性竞争力的同时，较基线提升了无害性，并在分布外无害性评估中表现出更强的鲁棒性。
Summary / 总结
The paper is motivated by the limitation of standard safe RLHF, which uses expected cost constraints that only capture a single statistic and fail to control tail risks or distributional uncertainty, especially for rare catastrophic events. To address this, the authors propose Risk-sensitive Alignment via Dominance (RAD), a method that replaces expected constraints with First-Order Stochastic Dominance (FSD) constraints, operationalized via an Optimal Transport framework with entropic regularization and Sinkhorn iterations for efficient, differentiable optimization; they further introduce quantile-weighted FSD to universally control a broad class of Spectral Risk Measures, allowing tunable risk profiles. Experimentally, RAD improves harmlessness over baselines while maintaining competitive helpfulness and shows greater robustness in out-of-distribution harmlessness evaluations.
本文的动机在于标准安全RLHF使用期望成本约束的局限性，该约束仅捕捉单一统计量，无法控制尾部风险或分布不确定性，特别是在罕见灾难性事件中。为此，作者提出了风险敏感对齐通过随机占优（RAD）方法，用一阶随机占优（FSD）约束替代期望约束，并通过最优传输框架结合熵正则化和Sinkhorn迭代实现高效、可微的优化；进一步引入分位数加权FSD来普遍控制一类谱风险度量，从而允许可调的风险轮廓。实验结果表明，RAD在无害性上优于基线方法，同时保持有帮助性的竞争力，并在分布外无害性评估中表现出更强的鲁棒性。
Offline Dynamic Inventory and Pricing Strategy: Addressing Censored and Dependent Demand
Authors: Korel Gundem, Zhengling Qi
First: 2025-04-14T02:57:51+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-11T16:18:36+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
In this paper, we study the offline sequential feature-based pricing and inventory control problem where the current demand depends on the past demand levels and any demand exceeding the available inventory is lost. Our goal is to leverage the offline dataset, consisting of past prices, ordering quantities, inventory levels, covariates, and censored sales levels, to estimate the optimal pricing and inventory control policy that maximizes long-term profit. While the underlying dynamic without censoring can be modeled by Markov decision process (MDP), the primary obstacle arises from the observed process where demand censoring is present, resulting in missing profit information, the failure of the Markov property, and a non-stationary optimal policy. To overcome these challenges, we first approximate the optimal policy by solving a high-order MDP characterized by the number of consecutive censoring instances, which ultimately boils down to solving a specialized Bellman equation tailored for this problem. Inspired by offline reinforcement learning and survival analysis, we propose two novel data-driven algorithms for solving these Bellman equations and, thus, estimate the optimal policy. Furthermore, we establish finite-sample regret bounds to validate the effectiveness of these algorithms. Finally, we conduct numerical experiments to demonstrate the efficacy of our algorithms in estimating the optimal policy. To the best of our knowledge, this is the first data-driven approach to learning optimal pricing and inventory control policies in a sequential decision-making environment characterized by censored and dependent demand. The implementations of the proposed algorithms are available at https://github.com/gundemkorel/Inventory_Pricing_Control
中文标题/摘要
标题：离线动态库存与定价策略：应对截尾与相依需求
本文研究了基于特征的离线序贯定价与库存控制问题，其中当前需求依赖于历史需求水平，且超出可用库存的需求将流失。我们的目标是利用离线数据集（包含历史价格、订购量、库存水平、协变量及截尾销售水平）来估计最大化长期利润的最优定价与库存控制策略。尽管无截尾情况下的底层动态可通过马尔可夫决策过程建模，但主要障碍源于观测过程中存在的需求截尾，这导致利润信息缺失、马尔可夫性质失效以及最优策略的非平稳性。为应对这些挑战，我们首先通过求解以连续截尾次数为特征的高阶MDP来近似最优策略，最终归结为求解针对该问题定制的特殊贝尔曼方程。受离线强化学习与生存分析的启发，我们提出了两种新颖的数据驱动算法来求解这些贝尔曼方程，从而估计最优策略。此外，我们建立了有限样本遗憾界以验证算法的有效性。最后，通过数值实验展示了算法在估计最优策略方面的效能。据我们所知，这是在以截尾与相依需求为特征的序贯决策环境中，首个学习最优定价与库存控制策略的数据驱动方法。所提算法的实现代码可在 https://github.com/gundemkorel/Inventory_Pricing_Control 获取。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need to optimize long-term profit in sequential inventory and pricing decisions where demand is both dependent on past levels and censored when exceeding stock, this paper develops a data-driven approach to estimate optimal policies from offline historical data. The method addresses the challenges of missing profit information and non-stationarity by approximating the problem as a high-order Markov decision process and solving specialized Bellman equations, drawing on offline reinforcement learning and survival analysis to propose two novel algorithms with theoretical regret bounds. Experimental results from numerical simulations confirm the efficacy of these algorithms in learning effective policies, marking the first such approach for censored and dependent demand environments.
本文针对库存与定价顺序决策中需求依赖于历史水平且超出库存时被截尾的问题，旨在利用离线历史数据优化长期利润，提出了一种数据驱动的方法来估计最优策略。该方法通过将问题近似为高阶马尔可夫决策过程并求解定制化的贝尔曼方程，结合离线强化学习和生存分析，设计了两种新算法，并建立了有限样本遗憾界以验证其理论有效性。数值实验结果表明，这些算法能有效学习最优策略，这是首次在需求截尾且依赖的序列决策环境中实现此类数据驱动方法。
Panda: A pretrained forecast model for chaotic dynamics
Authors: Jeffrey Lai, Anthony Bao, William Gilpin
First: 2025-05-19T21:59:19+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-11T15:51:45+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Chaotic systems are intrinsically sensitive to small errors, challenging efforts to construct predictive data-driven models of real-world dynamical systems such as fluid flows or neuronal activity. Prior efforts comprise either specialized models trained on individual time series, or foundation models trained on vast time series databases with little underlying dynamical structure. Motivated by dynamical systems theory, we present Panda, Patched Attention for Nonlinear DynAmics. We train Panda on a novel synthetic, extensible dataset of $2 \times 10^4$ chaotic dynamical systems that we discover using an evolutionary algorithm. Trained purely on simulated data, Panda exhibits emergent properties: zero-shot forecasting of unseen chaotic systems preserving both short-term accuracy and distributional measures, nonlinear resonance patterns in attention heads, and effective prediction of real-world experimental time series. Despite having been trained only on low-dimensional ordinary differential equations, Panda spontaneously develops the ability to predict partial differential equations without retraining. We also demonstrate a neural scaling law for differential equations, underscoring the potential of pre-trained models for probing abstract mathematical domains like nonlinear dynamics.
中文标题/摘要
标题：Panda：面向混沌动力学的预训练预测模型
混沌系统对小误差具有内在敏感性，这对构建现实世界动力系统（如流体流动或神经元活动）的数据驱动预测模型提出了挑战。先前研究主要包括针对单个时间序列训练的专业模型，或在缺乏基础动力学结构的大规模时间序列数据库上训练的基础模型。受动力系统理论启发，我们提出Panda（非线性动力学的分块注意力模型）。我们在通过进化算法发现的2×10^4个混沌动力系统构成的新型可扩展合成数据集上训练Panda。该模型仅基于模拟数据训练即展现出涌现特性：对未见混沌系统进行零样本预测时能同时保持短期精度与分布度量、注意力头中的非线性共振模式，以及对真实世界实验时间序列的有效预测。尽管仅基于低维常微分方程训练，Panda能自发预测偏微分方程而无需重新训练。我们还证明了微分方程的神经缩放定律，凸显了预训练模型在探索非线性动力学等抽象数学领域的潜力。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the challenge of predicting chaotic systems, which are highly sensitive to initial conditions, this paper introduces Panda, a pretrained model for chaotic dynamics. The method involves training Panda on a novel, synthetically generated dataset of 20,000 chaotic systems discovered via an evolutionary algorithm, using a patched attention architecture. Key experimental results show that Panda achieves zero-shot forecasting of unseen chaotic systems, preserving both short-term accuracy and long-term statistical properties, exhibits emergent nonlinear resonance patterns in its attention mechanisms, and successfully predicts real-world experimental time series and partial differential equations despite being trained only on low-dimensional ordinary differential equations, also demonstrating a neural scaling law for such systems.
本文针对混沌系统对初始条件高度敏感、难以预测的挑战，提出了名为Panda的预训练模型。该方法通过进化算法发现并构建了一个包含2万个混沌系统的合成数据集，并采用分块注意力架构对Panda进行训练。主要实验结果表明，Panda能够对未见过的混沌系统进行零样本预测，在保持短期精度的同时准确反映长期统计特性；其注意力头中出现了非线性共振模式；尽管仅基于低维常微分方程训练，该模型能有效预测真实世界实验时间序列甚至偏微分方程，同时还展示了微分方程领域的神经缩放定律。
Ergodicity in reinforcement learning
Authors: Dominik Baumann, Erfaun Noorani, Arsenii Mustafin, Xinyi Sheng, Bert Verbruggen, Arne Vanhoyweghen, Vincent Ginis, Thomas B. Schön
First: 2026-03-11T15:42:49+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-11T15:42:49+00:00
Comments: Accepted article to appear in Philosophical Transactions of the Royal Society A: Mathematical, Physical and Engineering Sciences
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
In reinforcement learning, we typically aim to optimize the expected value of the sum of rewards an agent collects over a trajectory. However, if the process generating these rewards is non-ergodic, the expected value, i.e., the average over infinitely many trajectories with a given policy, is uninformative for the average over a single, but infinitely long trajectory. Thus, if we care about how the individual agent performs during deployment, the expected value is not a good optimization objective. In this paper, we discuss the impact of non-ergodic reward processes on reinforcement learning agents through an instructive example, relate the notion of ergodic reward processes to more widely used notions of ergodic Markov chains, and present existing solutions that optimize long-term performance of individual trajectories under non-ergodic reward dynamics.
中文标题/摘要
标题：强化学习中的遍历性
在强化学习中，我们通常旨在优化智能体在轨迹上收集的奖励总和的期望值。然而，如果生成这些奖励的过程是非遍历的，那么期望值（即给定策略下无限多条轨迹的平均值）对于单条无限长轨迹的平均值而言是无意义的。因此，如果我们关心单个智能体在部署过程中的表现，期望值就不是一个良好的优化目标。本文通过一个示例性案例，讨论了非遍历奖励过程对强化学习智能体的影响，将遍历奖励过程的概念与更广泛使用的遍历马尔可夫链概念联系起来，并介绍了在非遍历奖励动态下优化单条轨迹长期性能的现有解决方案。
Summary / 总结
The paper is motivated by the inadequacy of the standard expected return objective in reinforcement learning when reward processes are non-ergodic, as this expectation fails to predict the long-term performance of an individual deployed agent. The method involves analyzing the problem through an instructive example, formally relating ergodic reward processes to the more common concept of ergodic Markov chains, and reviewing existing algorithmic solutions designed for non-ergodic dynamics. The main experimental or analytical result is the demonstration that optimizing for individual trajectory performance under non-ergodic conditions requires alternative approaches, which the paper catalogs and discusses.
本文的动机在于，当强化学习中的奖励过程是非遍历时，标准的期望回报目标存在缺陷，因为它无法预测单个智能体在长期部署中的实际表现。研究方法是通过一个示例进行分析，将遍历性奖励过程与更常见的遍历马尔可夫链概念建立形式化联系，并综述了针对非遍历动态设计的现有算法解决方案。主要结果是指出并讨论了在非遍历条件下优化个体轨迹性能需要替代方法，并对这些现有方案进行了梳理。
Dynamics-Predictive Sampling for Active RL Finetuning of Large Reasoning Models
Authors: Yixiu Mao, Yun Qu, Qi Wang, Heming Zou, Xiangyang Ji
Venue: ICLR 2026
First: 2026-03-11T15:31:14+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-11T15:31:14+00:00
Comments: Accepted to ICLR 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement learning (RL) finetuning has become a key technique for enhancing the reasoning abilities of large language models (LLMs). However, its effectiveness critically depends on the selection of training data. Recent advances underscore the importance of online prompt selection methods, which typically concentrate training on partially solved or moderately challenging examples under the current policy, thereby yielding more effective model updates. While significantly accelerating RL finetuning in terms of training steps, they also incur substantial computational overhead by requiring extensive LLM rollouts over large candidate batches to identify informative samples, an expense that can outweigh the finetuning process itself. To address this challenge, this work proposes Dynamics-Predictive Sampling (DPS), which online predicts and selects informative prompts by inferring their learning dynamics prior to costly rollouts. Specifically, we introduce a new perspective by modeling each prompt's solving progress during RL finetuning as a dynamical system, where the extent of solving is represented as the state and the transition is characterized by a hidden Markov model. Using historical rollout reward signals, we perform online Bayesian inference to estimate evolving state distributions, and the inference outcome provides a predictive prior for efficient prompt selection without rollout-intensive filtering. Empirical results across diverse reasoning tasks, including mathematics, planning, and visual geometry, demonstrate that DPS substantially reduces redundant rollouts, accelerates the training process, and achieves superior reasoning performance.
中文标题/摘要
标题：面向大型推理模型主动强化学习微调的动态预测采样方法
强化学习微调已成为提升大语言模型推理能力的关键技术，但其效果高度依赖于训练数据的选择。近期研究强调在线提示选择方法的重要性，这类方法通常将训练集中在当前策略下部分解决或中等难度的样本上，从而产生更有效的模型更新。虽然能显著加速强化学习微调的训练步数，但这类方法需要在大规模候选批次上进行大量大语言模型推演以筛选信息样本，产生了可能超过微调过程本身的计算开销。为应对这一挑战，本研究提出动态预测采样方法，通过在昂贵推演前推断学习动态，在线预测并选择信息性提示。具体而言，我们引入新视角：将强化学习微调中每个提示的解决进度建模为动态系统，其中解决程度表示为状态，状态转移由隐马尔可夫模型刻画。利用历史推演奖励信号，我们执行在线贝叶斯推断以估计演化状态分布，推断结果为无需推演密集型筛选的高效提示选择提供预测先验。在数学、规划和视觉几何等多样化推理任务上的实验结果表明，该方法能显著减少冗余推演、加速训练过程，并获得更优的推理性能。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the computational inefficiency of online prompt selection in RL finetuning for large reasoning models, which traditionally requires extensive and costly LLM rollouts to identify informative training samples. The proposed method, Dynamics-Predictive Sampling (DPS), models each prompt's solving progress as a dynamical system using a hidden Markov model and performs online Bayesian inference on historical reward signals to predict learning dynamics, thereby enabling efficient prompt selection without rollout-intensive filtering. Experimental results across mathematics, planning, and visual geometry tasks show that DPS significantly reduces redundant rollouts, accelerates training, and achieves superior reasoning performance compared to prior methods.
本文针对大型推理模型强化学习微调中在线提示选择的计算低效问题，传统方法需通过大量耗时的模型展开来筛选信息样本。提出的动态预测采样方法将每个提示的求解进度建模为动态系统，利用隐马尔可夫模型并通过历史奖励信号进行在线贝叶斯推断，从而预测学习动态，实现无需展开密集型过滤的高效提示选择。在数学、规划和视觉几何等多样化推理任务上的实验结果表明，该方法显著减少了冗余展开，加速了训练过程，并获得了更优的推理性能。
Toward Closed-loop Molecular Discovery via Language Model, Property Alignment and Strategic Search
Authors: Junkai Ji, Zhangfan Yang, Dong Xu, Ruibin Bai, Jianqiang Li, Tingjun Hou, Zexuan Zhu
First: 2025-12-10T11:59:42+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-11T15:30:03+00:00
Comments: 30 pages, 7 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Drug discovery is a time-consuming and expensive process, with traditional high-throughput and docking-based virtual screening hampered by low success rates and limited scalability. Recent advances in generative modelling, including autoregressive, diffusion, and flow-based approaches, have enabled de novo ligand design beyond the limits of enumerative screening. Yet these models often suffer from inadequate generalization, limited interpretability, and an overemphasis on binding affinity at the expense of key pharmacological properties, thereby restricting their translational utility. Here we present Trio, a molecular generation framework integrating fragment-based molecular language modeling, reinforcement learning, and Monte Carlo tree search, for effective and interpretable closed-loop targeted molecular design. Through the three key components, Trio enables context-aware fragment assembly, enforces physicochemical and synthetic feasibility, and guides a balanced search between the exploration of novel chemotypes and the exploitation of promising intermediates within protein binding pockets. Experimental results show that Trio reliably achieves chemically valid and pharmacologically enhanced ligands, outperforming state-of-the-art approaches with improved binding affinity (+7.85%), drug-likeness (+11.10%) and synthetic accessibility (+12.05%), while expanding molecular diversity more than fourfold. By combining generalization, plausibility, and interpretability, Trio establishes a closed-loop generative paradigm that redefines how chemical space can be navigated, offering a transformative foundation for the next era of AI-driven drug discovery.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于语言模型、性质对齐与策略搜索的闭环分子发现研究
药物发现过程耗时且昂贵，传统的高通量筛选和基于对接的虚拟筛选受限于低成功率和有限的可扩展性。近年来，包括自回归、扩散和流模型在内的生成建模技术已能实现超越枚举筛选范围的全新配体设计。然而，这些模型常存在泛化能力不足、可解释性有限，以及过度强调结合亲和力而忽视关键药理学性质的问题，从而限制了其实际应用。本文提出Trio框架，该框架整合了基于片段的分子语言建模、强化学习和蒙特卡洛树搜索，以实现高效且可解释的闭环靶向分子设计。通过三大核心组件，Trio实现了上下文感知的片段组装，强化了物理化学与合成可行性，并在探索新型化学类型与利用蛋白质结合口袋中有前景的中间体之间引导平衡搜索。实验结果表明，Trio能稳定生成化学有效且药理学增强的配体，在结合亲和力（+7.85%）、类药性（+11.10%）和合成可及性（+12.05%）上优于现有先进方法，同时将分子多样性扩展四倍以上。通过结合泛化性、合理性与可解释性，Trio建立了一种闭环生成范式，重新定义了化学空间的探索方式，为人工智能驱动的药物发现新时代提供了变革性基础。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the inefficiency and limited scalability of traditional drug discovery methods, this paper introduces Trio, a molecular generation framework that integrates fragment-based language modeling, reinforcement learning, and Monte Carlo tree search for closed-loop targeted design. The method enables context-aware fragment assembly while enforcing physicochemical and synthetic feasibility, balancing exploration of novel chemotypes with exploitation of promising intermediates. Experimental results demonstrate that Trio reliably produces valid, pharmacologically enhanced ligands, outperforming state-of-the-art approaches with improvements in binding affinity (+7.85%), drug-likeness (+11.10%), and synthetic accessibility (+12.05%), while significantly expanding molecular diversity.
针对传统药物发现方法效率低下且可扩展性有限的问题，本文提出了Trio框架，它整合了基于片段的语言建模、强化学习和蒙特卡洛树搜索，用于闭环靶向分子设计。该方法实现了上下文感知的片段组装，同时确保物理化学和合成可行性，平衡了对新型化学型的探索与有前景中间体的利用。实验结果表明，Trio能可靠地生成有效且药理学增强的配体，在结合亲和力（+7.85%）、类药性（+11.10%）和合成可及性（+12.05%）上优于现有先进方法，并显著扩展了分子多样性。
Partially Equivariant Reinforcement Learning in Symmetry-Breaking Environments
Authors: Junwoo Chang, Minwoo Park, Joohwan Seo, Roberto Horowitz, Jongmin Lee, Jongeun Choi
Venue: ICLR 2026
First: 2025-11-30T14:41:08+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-11T15:19:35+00:00
Comments: ICLR 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Project1
Abstract
Group symmetries provide a powerful inductive bias for reinforcement learning (RL), enabling efficient generalization across symmetric states and actions via group-invariant Markov Decision Processes (MDPs). However, real-world environments almost never realize fully group-invariant MDPs; dynamics, actuation limits, and reward design usually break symmetries, often only locally. Under group-invariant Bellman backups for such cases, local symmetry-breaking introduces errors that propagate across the entire state-action space, resulting in global value estimation errors. To address this, we introduce Partially group-Invariant MDP (PI-MDP), which selectively applies group-invariant or standard Bellman backups depending on where symmetry holds. This framework mitigates error propagation from locally broken symmetries while maintaining the benefits of equivariance, thereby enhancing sample efficiency and generalizability. Building on this framework, we present practical RL algorithms -- Partially Equivariant (PE)-DQN for discrete control and PE-SAC for continuous control -- that combine the benefits of equivariance with robustness to symmetry-breaking. Experiments across Grid-World, locomotion, and manipulation benchmarks demonstrate that PE-DQN and PE-SAC significantly outperform baselines, highlighting the importance of selective symmetry exploitation for robust and sample-efficient RL. Project page: https://pranaboy72.github.io/perl_page/
中文标题/摘要
标题：对称性破缺环境中的部分等变强化学习
群对称性为强化学习提供了强大的归纳偏置，通过群不变马尔可夫决策过程，能够在对称状态与动作间实现高效泛化。然而，现实环境几乎从不实现完全的群不变MDP；动力学、执行器限制及奖励设计通常会破坏对称性，且往往仅局部破坏。对此类情况采用群不变贝尔曼备份时，局部对称性破缺会引入误差，并传播至整个状态-动作空间，导致全局价值估计误差。为解决此问题，我们提出部分群不变MDP框架，根据对称性保持区域选择性应用群不变或标准贝尔曼备份。该框架在保持等变性优势的同时，缓解了局部对称性破缺导致的误差传播，从而提升了样本效率与泛化能力。基于此框架，我们提出了实用RL算法——面向离散控制的PE-DQN与面向连续控制的PE-SAC，它们融合了等变性的优势与对对称性破缺的鲁棒性。在Grid-World、运动控制与操作任务基准上的实验表明，PE-DQN与PE-SAC显著优于基线方法，凸显了选择性利用对称性对实现鲁棒且高效的强化学习的重要性。项目页面：https://pranaboy72.github.io/perl_page/
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the challenge of applying group symmetries in reinforcement learning (RL) to real-world environments where perfect symmetries are often broken locally by dynamics or rewards. The authors introduce the Partially group-Invariant Markov Decision Process (PI-MDP) framework, which selectively applies group-invariant or standard Bellman backups depending on whether symmetry holds in a given state-action region, thereby preventing local symmetry-breaking errors from propagating globally. They develop practical algorithms, PE-DQN for discrete control and PE-SAC for continuous control, which experimentally outperform baselines in Grid-World, locomotion, and manipulation tasks, demonstrating improved sample efficiency and robustness through selective symmetry exploitation.
本文针对强化学习中群对称性应用于现实环境时，常因动力学或奖励设计导致局部对称性被破坏的问题展开研究。作者提出了部分群不变马尔可夫决策过程（PI-MDP）框架，该框架根据状态-动作区域中对称性是否成立，选择性应用群不变或标准贝尔曼备份，从而防止局部对称性破坏误差全局传播。基于此框架，他们开发了适用于离散控制的PE-DQN算法和连续控制的PE-SAC算法。在网格世界、运动控制和操作任务上的实验表明，这些算法显著优于基线方法，验证了选择性利用对称性可提升样本效率和鲁棒性。
$V_{0.5}$: Generalist Value Model as a Prior for Sparse RL Rollouts
Authors: Yi-Kai Zhang, Yueqing Sun, Hongyan Hao, Qi Gu, Xunliang Cai, De-Chuan Zhan, Han-Jia Ye
First: 2026-03-11T14:57:41+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-11T14:57:41+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
In Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR), constructing a robust advantage baseline is critical for policy gradients, effectively guiding the policy model to reinforce desired behaviors. Recent research has introduced Generalist Value Models (such as $V_0$), which achieve pre-trained value estimation by explicitly encoding model capabilities in-context, eliminating the need to synchronously update the value model alongside the policy model. In this paper, we propose $V_{0.5}$, which adaptively fuses the baseline predicted by such value model (acting as a prior) with the empirical mean derived from sparse rollouts. This constructs a robust baseline that balances computational efficiency with extremely low variance. Specifically, we introduce a real-time statistical testing and dynamic budget allocation. This balances the high variance caused by sparse sampling against the systematic bias (or hallucinations) inherent in the value model's prior. By constructing a hypothesis test to evaluate the prior's reliability in real-time, the system dynamically allocates additional rollout budget on demand. This mechanism minimizes the baseline estimator's Mean Squared Error (MSE), guaranteeing stable policy gradients, even under extreme sparsity with a group size of 4. Extensive evaluations across six mathematical reasoning benchmarks demonstrate that $V_{0.5}$ significantly outperforms GRPO and DAPO, achieving faster convergence and over some 10% performance improvement.
中文标题/摘要
标题：$V_{0.5}$：作为稀疏强化学习推演先验的通用价值模型
在可验证奖励的强化学习中，构建稳健的优势基线对策略梯度至关重要，能有效引导策略模型强化期望行为。近期研究提出的通用价值模型通过显式编码模型上下文能力实现预训练价值估计，无需与策略模型同步更新。本文提出$V_{0.5}$模型，自适应融合此类价值模型预测的基线先验与稀疏推演的经验均值，构建出平衡计算效率与极低方差的稳健基线。具体引入实时统计检验与动态预算分配机制，权衡稀疏采样导致的高方差与价值模型先验固有的系统偏差。通过假设检验实时评估先验可靠性，系统按需动态分配额外推演预算，最小化基线估计器的均方误差，确保即使在组规模为4的极端稀疏条件下仍能保持稳定的策略梯度。在六个数学推理基准上的广泛评估表明，$V_{0.5}$显著优于GRPO和DAPO方法，实现更快收敛与约10%的性能提升。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the challenge of constructing a low-variance advantage baseline for policy gradients in Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR), where sparse rollouts can lead to high variance. The proposed method, $V_{0.5}$, adaptively fuses a prior from a pre-trained Generalist Value Model with the empirical mean from sparse rollouts, using real-time statistical testing and dynamic budget allocation to balance bias and variance. Experimental results across six mathematical reasoning benchmarks show that $V_{0.5}$ significantly outperforms GRPO and DAPO, achieving faster convergence and over 10% performance improvement even with extreme sparsity.
本文针对可验证奖励强化学习（RLVR）中策略梯度所需低方差优势基线的构建难题，旨在解决稀疏模拟导致的高方差问题。方法上提出了$V_{0.5}$，它自适应地融合了预训练通用价值模型提供的先验与稀疏模拟的经验均值，通过实时统计检验和动态预算分配来权衡偏差与方差。在六个数学推理基准上的实验结果表明，$V_{0.5}$显著优于GRPO和DAPO，即使在极端稀疏条件下也能实现更快收敛和超过10%的性能提升。
Towards Cold-Start Drafting and Continual Refining: A Value-Driven Memory Approach with Application to NPU Kernel Synthesis
Authors: Yujie Zheng, Zhuo Li, Shengtao Zhang, Hanjing Wang, Junjie Sheng, Jiaqian Wang, Junchi Yan, Weinan Zhang, Ying Wen, Bo Tang, Muning Wen
First: 2026-03-11T14:57:06+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-11T14:57:06+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Deploying Large Language Models to data-scarce programming domains poses significant challenges, particularly for kernel synthesis on emerging Domain-Specific Architectures where a "Data Wall" limits available training data. While models excel on data-rich platforms like CUDA, they suffer catastrophic performance drops on data-scarce ecosystems such as NPU programming. To overcome this cold-start barrier without expensive fine-tuning, we introduce EvoKernel, a self-evolving agentic framework that automates the lifecycle of kernel synthesis from initial drafting to continual refining. EvoKernel addresses this by formulating the synthesis process as a memory-based reinforcement learning task. Through a novel value-driven retrieval mechanism, it learns stage-specific Q-values that prioritize experiences based on their contribution to the current objective, whether bootstrapping a feasible draft or iteratively refining latency. Furthermore, by enabling cross-task memory sharing, the agent generalizes insights from simple to complex operators. By building an NPU variant of KernelBench and evaluating on it, EvoKernel improves frontier models' correctness from 11.0% to 83.0% and achieves a median speedup of 3.60x over initial drafts through iterative refinement. This demonstrates that value-guided experience accumulation allows general-purpose models to master the kernel synthesis task on niche hardware ecosystems. Our official page is available at https://evokernel.zhuo.li.

标题：面向冷启动草拟与持续优化：一种基于价值驱动记忆的方法及其在NPU内核合成中的应用
将大语言模型部署至数据稀缺的编程领域面临重大挑战，尤其在面向新兴领域专用架构的内核合成中，'数据壁垒'限制了可用训练数据。尽管模型在CUDA等数据丰富的平台上表现优异，但在NPU编程等数据稀缺生态系统中性能会急剧下降。为在不依赖昂贵微调的情况下突破冷启动障碍，我们提出了EvoKernel——一个自进化的智能体框架，实现了从初始草拟到持续优化的内核合成全生命周期自动化。该框架通过将合成过程构建为基于记忆的强化学习任务来解决此问题。借助新颖的价值驱动检索机制，系统学习阶段特定的Q值，根据经验对当前目标（无论是引导可行草拟还是迭代优化延迟）的贡献度进行优先级排序。此外，通过跨任务记忆共享机制，智能体能够将简单算子的洞察泛化至复杂算子。通过构建KernelBench的NPU变体并开展评估，EvoKernel将前沿模型的正确率从11.0%提升至83.0%，并通过迭代优化使中位加速比达到初始草拟的3.60倍。这表明价值引导的经验积累能使通用模型掌握小众硬件生态系统的内核合成任务。项目主页：https://evokernel.zhuo.li。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the challenge of deploying Large Language Models for kernel synthesis on emerging Domain-Specific Architectures like NPUs, where scarce training data leads to poor performance, unlike in data-rich environments such as CUDA. To overcome this cold-start problem without costly fine-tuning, the authors propose EvoKernel, a self-evolving agentic framework that treats kernel synthesis as a memory-based reinforcement learning task, utilizing a value-driven retrieval mechanism to prioritize experiences for drafting or refining kernels and enabling cross-task memory sharing for generalization. Experimental results on an NPU variant of KernelBench show that EvoKernel boosts model correctness from 11.0% to 83.0% and achieves a median speedup of 3.60x over initial drafts through iterative refinement, demonstrating that value-guided experience accumulation allows general-purpose models to master kernel synthesis on niche hardware.

LexiSafe: Offline Safe Reinforcement Learning with Lexicographic Safety-Reward Hierarchy
Authors: Hsin-Jung Yang, Zhanhong Jiang, Prajwal Koirala, Qisai Liu, Cody Fleming, Soumik Sarkar
First: 2026-02-19T12:22:50+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-11T14:41:41+00:00
Comments: 17th ACM/IEEE International Conference on Cyber-Physical Systems
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Offline safe reinforcement learning (RL) is increasingly important for cyber-physical systems (CPS), where safety violations during training are unacceptable and only pre-collected data are available. Existing offline safe RL methods typically balance reward-safety tradeoffs through constraint relaxation or joint optimization, but they often lack structural mechanisms to prevent safety drift. We propose LexiSafe, a lexicographic offline RL framework designed to preserve safety-aligned behavior. We first develop LexiSafe-SC, a single-cost formulation for standard offline safe RL, and derive safety-violation and performance-suboptimality bounds that together yield sample-complexity guarantees. We then extend the framework to hierarchical safety requirements with LexiSafe-MC, which supports multiple safety costs and admits its own sample-complexity analysis. Empirically, LexiSafe demonstrates reduced safety violations and improved task performance compared to constrained offline baselines. By unifying lexicographic prioritization with structural bias, LexiSafe offers a practical and theoretically grounded approach for safety-critical CPS decision-making.
中文标题/摘要
标题：LexiSafe：基于词典序安全-奖励层级的离线安全强化学习
离线安全强化学习对信息物理系统日益重要，因其训练过程不允许出现安全违规且仅能使用预收集数据。现有方法通常通过约束松弛或联合优化平衡奖励与安全，但缺乏防止安全漂移的结构机制。本文提出词典序离线强化学习框架LexiSafe以保持安全对齐行为：首先构建单成本模型LexiSafe-SC，推导出安全违规与性能次优性边界，共同形成样本复杂度保证；随后扩展为多安全成本框架LexiSafe-MC以支持层级安全需求，并提供相应样本复杂度分析。实验表明，相比约束离线基线方法，LexiSafe能减少安全违规并提升任务性能。该框架通过词典序优先级与结构偏差的统一，为安全关键信息物理系统决策提供兼具理论依据与实践价值的新途径。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the challenge of offline safe reinforcement learning for cyber-physical systems, where safety violations during training are unacceptable and only pre-collected data can be used. Existing methods often lack structural mechanisms to prevent safety drift, so the authors propose LexiSafe, a lexicographic framework that prioritizes safety through a hierarchical approach. The method includes LexiSafe-SC for single safety costs with theoretical sample-complexity guarantees, and LexiSafe-MC for multiple safety costs. Experimental results show that LexiSafe reduces safety violations and improves task performance compared to constrained offline baselines, offering a practical and theoretically grounded solution for safety-critical decision-making.
本文针对信息物理系统的离线安全强化学习问题，旨在避免训练中的安全违规，且仅能使用预收集数据。现有方法常缺乏防止安全漂移的结构机制，因此作者提出了LexiSafe，一种基于词典序的框架，通过层次化方法优先保障安全。该方法包括针对单一安全成本的LexiSafe-SC，具有理论样本复杂度保证，以及支持多安全成本的LexiSafe-MC。实验结果表明，与受限离线基线方法相比，LexiSafe减少了安全违规并提升了任务性能，为安全关键决策提供了实用且理论扎实的解决方案。
ReTabSyn: Realistic Tabular Data Synthesis via Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Xiaofeng Lin, Seungbae Kim, Zhuoya Li, Zachary DeSoto, Charles Fleming, Guang Cheng
First: 2026-03-11T14:31:07+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-11T14:31:07+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Deep generative models can help with data scarcity and privacy by producing synthetic training data, but they struggle in low-data, imbalanced tabular settings to fully learn the complex data distribution. We argue that striving for the full joint distribution could be overkill; for greater data efficiency, models should prioritize learning the conditional distribution $P(y\mid \bm{X})$, as suggested by recent theoretical analysis. Therefore, we overcome this limitation with \textbf{ReTabSyn}, a \textbf{Re}inforced \textbf{Tab}ular \textbf{Syn}thesis pipeline that provides direct feedback on feature correlation preservation during synthesizer training. This objective encourages the generator to prioritize the most useful predictive signals when training data is limited, thereby strengthening downstream model utility. We empirically fine-tune a language model-based generator using this approach, and across benchmarks with small sample sizes, class imbalance, and distribution shift, ReTabSyn consistently outperforms state-of-the-art baselines. Moreover, our approach can be readily extended to control various aspects of synthetic tabular data, such as applying expert-specified constraints on generated observations.
中文标题/摘要
标题：ReTabSyn：基于强化学习的真实表格数据合成
深度生成模型可通过生成合成训练数据缓解数据稀缺与隐私问题，但在低数据量、不平衡的表格场景中难以完整学习复杂数据分布。我们认为追求完整联合分布可能过度；为提高数据效率，模型应优先学习条件分布 $P(y\mid \bm{X})$（近期理论分析支持此观点）。为此，我们提出 \textbf{ReTabSyn}——一种基于\textbf{强化学习}的\textbf{表格数据合成}流程，能在合成器训练期间直接反馈特征相关性保持情况。该目标促使生成器在训练数据有限时优先学习最具预测价值的信号，从而增强下游模型效用。我们采用此方法对基于语言模型的生成器进行实证微调，在小样本、类别不平衡及分布偏移的基准测试中，ReTabSyn 均持续优于前沿基线模型。此外，该方法可轻松扩展至控制合成表格数据的多维度属性，例如对生成样本施加专家指定的约束条件。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the limitations of deep generative models in low-data, imbalanced tabular settings, where learning the full joint distribution is inefficient, this paper proposes ReTabSyn, a reinforced tabular synthesis pipeline that prioritizes learning the conditional distribution P(y|X) to enhance data efficiency. The method employs reinforcement learning to provide direct feedback on feature correlation preservation during generator training, encouraging the model to focus on the most useful predictive signals. Experimental results on benchmarks with small sample sizes, class imbalance, and distribution shift show that ReTabSyn consistently outperforms state-of-the-art baselines in downstream utility, and it can be extended to incorporate expert constraints on synthetic data.
针对深度生成模型在低数据、不平衡表格数据中难以学习完整联合分布的问题，本文提出ReTabSyn，一种基于强化学习的表格数据合成框架，旨在通过优先学习条件分布P(y|X)来提高数据效率。该方法在生成器训练过程中利用强化学习提供特征相关性保持的直接反馈，促使模型专注于最有用的预测信号。在小型样本、类别不平衡和分布偏移的基准测试中，ReTabSyn在提升下游模型性能方面持续优于现有先进方法，并且能够扩展以融入专家对生成数据的约束控制。
Mindstorms in Natural Language-Based Societies of Mind
Authors: Mingchen Zhuge, Haozhe Liu, Francesco Faccio, Dylan R. Ashley, Róbert Csordás, Anand Gopalakrishnan, Abdullah Hamdi, Hasan Abed Al Kader Hammoud, Vincent Herrmann, Kazuki Irie, Louis Kirsch, Bing Li, Guohao Li, Shuming Liu, Jinjie Mai, Piotr Piękos, Aditya Ramesh, Imanol Schlag, Weimin Shi, Aleksandar Stanić, Wenyi Wang, Yuhui Wang, Mengmeng Xu, Deng-Ping Fan, Bernard Ghanem, Jürgen Schmidhuber
Venue: (2025). Computational Visual Media, 11(1), 29-81
First: 2023-05-26T16:21:25+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-11T13:43:31+00:00
Comments: published in Computational Visual Media Journal (CVMJ); 9 pages in main text + 7 pages of references + 38 pages of appendices, 14 figures in main text + 13 in appendices, 7 tables in appendices
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Both Minsky's "society of mind" and Schmidhuber's "learning to think" inspire diverse societies of large multimodal neural networks (NNs) that solve problems by interviewing each other in a "mindstorm." Recent implementations of NN-based societies of minds consist of large language models (LLMs) and other NN-based experts communicating through a natural language interface. In doing so, they overcome the limitations of single LLMs, improving multimodal zero-shot reasoning. In these natural language-based societies of mind (NLSOMs), new agents -- all communicating through the same universal symbolic language -- are easily added in a modular fashion. To demonstrate the power of NLSOMs, we assemble and experiment with several of them (having up to 129 members), leveraging mindstorms in them to solve some practical AI tasks: visual question answering, image captioning, text-to-image synthesis, 3D generation, egocentric retrieval, embodied AI, and general language-based task solving. We view this as a starting point towards much larger NLSOMs with billions of agents-some of which may be humans. And with this emergence of great societies of heterogeneous minds, many new research questions have suddenly become paramount to the future of artificial intelligence. What should be the social structure of an NLSOM? What would be the (dis)advantages of having a monarchical rather than a democratic structure? How can principles of NN economies be used to maximize the total reward of a reinforcement learning NLSOM? In this work, we identify, discuss, and try to answer some of these questions.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于自然语言的思维社会中的思维风暴

The method involves assembling modular societies of up to 129 agents that engage in collaborative "mindstorms" through a universal language interface. RetroAgent: From Solving to Evolving via Retrospective Dual Intrinsic Feedback
Authors: Xiaoying Zhang, Zichen Liu, Yipeng Zhang, Xia Hu, Wenqi Shao
First: 2026-03-09T16:23:33+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-11T12:33:30+00:00
Comments: 45 pages, update the results for Llama3.1-8B-instruct
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large language model (LLM)-based agents trained with reinforcement learning (RL) have shown strong potential on complex interactive tasks. However, standard RL paradigms favor static problem-solving over continuous adaptation: agents often converge to suboptimal strategies due to insufficient exploration, while learned knowledge remains implicit within parameters rather than explicitly retrievable, limiting effective experiential learning. To address these limitations, we introduce RetroAgent, an online RL framework that empowers agents to master complex interactive environments not just by solving, but by evolving. Concretely, RetroAgent features a hindsight self-reflection mechanism that produces dual intrinsic feedback: (1) intrinsic numerical feedback that that tracks incremental subtask completion relative to prior attempts, rewarding promising explorations, and (2) intrinsic language feedback that distills reusable lessons into a memory buffer, retrieved via our proposed Similarity & Utility-Aware Upper Confidence Bound (SimUtil-UCB) strategy balancing relevance, utility, and exploration to effectively leverage past experiences. Extensive experiments on two model families across four challenging agentic tasks demonstrate that RetroAgent significantly outperforms existing methods, achieving state-of-the-art results -- e.g., surpassing Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO)-trained agents by +18.3% on ALFWorld, +15.4% on WebShop, +27.1% on Sokoban, and +8.9% on MineSweeper -- while exhibiting strong test-time adaptation and generalization to out-of-distribution scenarios.
中文标题/摘要
标题：RetroAgent：通过回顾式双重内在反馈实现从求解到进化的跨越
基于大语言模型（LLM）并通过强化学习（RL）训练的智能体在复杂交互任务中展现出巨大潜力。然而，标准RL范式偏向静态问题求解而非持续适应：智能体常因探索不足而收敛至次优策略，且习得知识隐式存储于参数中而非显式可检索，限制了有效的经验学习。为应对这些局限，我们提出RetroAgent——一种在线RL框架，使智能体不仅能通过求解，更能通过进化来掌握复杂交互环境。具体而言，RetroAgent具备事后自省机制，可生成双重内在反馈：（1）追踪相对于先前尝试的子任务完成进度的内在数值反馈，以奖励有前景的探索；（2）将可复用经验提炼至记忆缓冲区的内在语言反馈，通过我们提出的相似性与效用感知上置信界（SimUtil-UCB）策略进行检索，该策略平衡相关性、效用与探索性，从而有效利用过往经验。在两个模型族、四项挑战性智能体任务上的大量实验表明，RetroAgent显著优于现有方法，取得最先进成果——例如在ALFWorld超越GRPO训练智能体18.3%、WebShop提升15.4%、Sokoban提高27.1%、MineSweeper增加8.9%——同时展现出强大的测试时适应能力及对分布外场景的泛化性能。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the limitations of standard reinforcement learning paradigms for LLM-based agents, which often lead to suboptimal strategies and implicit knowledge that hinders continuous adaptation, this paper introduces RetroAgent, an online RL framework featuring a hindsight self-reflection mechanism. The method generates dual intrinsic feedback: numerical feedback that rewards incremental subtask completion and language feedback that distills reusable lessons into a memory buffer, retrieved via a novel Similarity & Utility-Aware Upper Confidence Bound strategy to balance relevance, utility, and exploration. Experimental results across four challenging tasks, including ALFWorld and WebShop, show that RetroAgent significantly outperforms existing methods, achieving state-of-the-art performance gains of up to +27.1% and demonstrating strong test-time adaptation and generalization to out-of-distribution scenarios.
本文的动机是解决标准强化学习范式在基于大语言模型的智能体上的局限性，这些范式常导致次优策略和隐含知识，阻碍了持续适应能力。为此，研究提出了RetroAgent这一在线强化学习框架，其核心是事后自我反思机制，能生成双重内在反馈：一是追踪相对于先前尝试的增量子任务完成度的数值反馈以奖励有前景的探索，二是将可重用经验提炼到记忆缓冲区的语言反馈，并通过提出的相似性与效用感知上置信界策略来检索，以平衡相关性、效用和探索。在四个挑战性任务上的广泛实验表明，RetroAgent显著优于现有方法，例如在ALFWorld上超过GRPO训练智能体18.3%，在WebShop上超过15.4%，并展现出强大的测试时适应和分布外泛化能力。
To Mix or To Merge: Toward Multi-Domain Reinforcement Learning for Large Language Models
Authors: Haoqing Wang, Xiang Long, Ziheng Li, Yilong Xu, Tingguang Li, Yehui Tang
First: 2026-02-13T03:25:13+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-11T12:27:33+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) plays a key role in stimulating the explicit reasoning capability of Large Language Models (LLMs). We can achieve expert-level performance in some specific domains via RLVR, such as coding or math. When a general multi-domain expert-level model is required, we need to carefully consider the collaboration of RLVR across different domains. The current state-of-the-art models mainly employ two different training paradigms for multi-domain RLVR: mixed multi-task RLVR and separate RLVR followed by model merging. However, most of the works did not provide a detailed comparison and analysis about these paradigms. To this end, we choose multiple commonly used high-level tasks (e.g., math, coding, science, instruction following, and agent) as our target domains and design extensive qualitative and quantitative experiments using open-source datasets. We find the RLVR across domains exhibits few mutual interferences, and reasoning-intensive domains demonstrate mutually synergistic effects. Furthermore, we analyze the internal mechanisms of mutual gains from the perspectives of weight space geometry, information constraints, model prediction behavior and self-verification. This project is named as M2RL that means Mixed multi-task training or separate training followed by model Merging for Reinforcement Learning, and the homepage is at https://github.com/Mosi-AI/M2RL.
中文标题/摘要
标题：混合还是合并：迈向大语言模型的多领域强化学习
可验证奖励强化学习（RLVR）在激发大语言模型（LLMs）的显式推理能力方面起着关键作用。通过RLVR，我们能在特定领域（如编程或数学）实现专家级性能。当需要通用的多领域专家级模型时，需审慎考虑RLVR在不同领域间的协同机制。当前最先进的模型主要采用两种多领域RLVR训练范式：混合多任务RLVR，以及独立RLVR后模型合并。然而，现有研究大多未对这些范式进行系统比较分析。为此，我们选取多个常用高级任务（如数学、编程、科学、指令遵循、智能体）作为目标领域，基于开源数据集设计大量定性与定量实验。研究发现：跨领域RLVR存在较少相互干扰，推理密集型领域呈现相互协同效应。进一步从权重空间几何、信息约束、模型预测行为及自我验证等视角，深入解析了跨领域增益的内在机制。本项目命名为M2RL（意为“混合多任务训练或独立训练后模型合并的强化学习”），项目主页位于https://github.com/Mosi-AI/M2RL。
Summary / 总结
This paper investigates training paradigms for achieving multi-domain expertise in large language models via reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR), motivated by the need to understand whether mixed multi-task training or separate training followed by model merging is more effective. The method involves extensive experiments across domains like math, coding, and science using open-source datasets, analyzing mutual interference and synergy. The main experimental results reveal that RLVR across domains shows minimal mutual interference, with reasoning-intensive domains even exhibiting synergistic gains, and the analysis explores underlying mechanisms through weight space geometry and model behavior.
本文研究通过可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR）实现大型语言模型多领域专业化的训练范式，动机在于需要理解混合多任务训练与分别训练后模型合并哪种更有效。方法包括使用开源数据集在数学、编程和科学等领域进行广泛实验，分析相互干扰与协同效应。主要实验结果表明，跨领域的RLVR相互干扰很小，推理密集型领域甚至表现出协同增益，并通过权重空间几何和模型行为分析了其内在机制。
Position: Beyond Model-Centric Prediction -- Agentic Time Series Forecasting
Authors: Mingyue Cheng, Xiaoyu Tao, Qi Liu, Ze Guo, Enhong Chen
First: 2026-02-02T08:01:11+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-11T11:27:36+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Time series forecasting has traditionally been formulated as a model-centric, static, and single-pass prediction problem that maps historical observations to future values. While this paradigm has driven substantial progress, it proves insufficient in adaptive and multi-turn settings where forecasting requires informative feature extraction, reasoning-driven inference, iterative refinement, and continual adaptation over time. In this paper, we argue for agentic time series forecasting (ATSF), which reframes forecasting as an agentic process composed of perception, planning, action, reflection, and memory. Rather than focusing solely on predictive models, ATSF emphasizes organizing forecasting as an agentic workflow that can interact with tools, incorporate feedback from outcomes, and evolve through experience accumulation. We outline three representative implementation paradigms -- workflow-based design, agentic reinforcement learning, and a hybrid agentic workflow paradigm -- and discuss the opportunities and challenges that arise when shifting from model-centric prediction to agentic forecasting. Together, this position aims to establish agentic forecasting as a foundation for future research at the intersection of time series forecasting.
中文标题/摘要
标题：观点：超越模型中心预测——智能体时间序列预测
时间序列预测传统上被构建为一个模型中心、静态且单次执行的预测问题，即将历史观测值映射为未来值。尽管这一范式推动了显著进展，但在需要信息特征提取、推理驱动推断、迭代优化以及持续时域适应的自适应多轮场景中，其局限性日益凸显。本文提出智能体时间序列预测（ATSF）框架，将预测重构为由感知、规划、行动、反思与记忆构成的智能体过程。ATSF不仅关注预测模型，更强调将预测组织为可与工具交互、整合结果反馈、通过经验积累进化的智能体工作流。我们概述了三种典型实现范式——基于工作流的设计、智能体强化学习及混合智能体工作流范式，并探讨了从模型中心预测转向智能体预测所面临的机遇与挑战。本观点旨在将智能体预测确立为时间序列预测交叉领域未来研究的基础。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the limitations of traditional model-centric, single-pass approaches in adaptive and multi-turn forecasting scenarios, this position paper advocates for agentic time series forecasting (ATSF), which reframes forecasting as an agentic process involving perception, planning, action, reflection, and memory. The proposed method emphasizes organizing forecasting as an interactive workflow that can utilize tools, incorporate feedback, and evolve through experience, outlining three implementation paradigms: workflow-based design, agentic reinforcement learning, and a hybrid agentic workflow. The main experimental results are not detailed as this is a conceptual position paper, but it establishes ATSF as a foundational direction for future research, highlighting the opportunities and challenges in shifting from static prediction to dynamic, agent-driven forecasting.
本文的动机在于传统以模型为中心、单次预测的方法在自适应和多轮预测场景中的不足，因此主张将时间序列预测重构为一种智能体过程，即智能体时间序列预测（ATSF），该过程包含感知、规划、行动、反思和记忆。方法上强调将预测组织为一种可交互的工作流程，能够利用工具、整合反馈并通过经验积累不断演进，概述了三种实现范式：基于工作流的设计、智能体强化学习以及混合智能体工作流。由于这是一篇概念性立场论文，未详述具体实验结果，但其确立了ATSF作为未来研究的基础方向，重点探讨了从静态预测转向动态、智能体驱动预测所带来的机遇与挑战。
CARE: Towards Clinical Accountability in Multi-Modal Medical Reasoning with an Evidence-Grounded Agentic Framework
Authors: Yuexi Du, Jinglu Wang, Shujie Liu, Nicha C. Dvornek, Yan Lu
Venue: ICLR 2026
First: 2026-03-02T08:38:37+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-11T10:41:44+00:00
Comments: Accepted by ICLR 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Project1
Abstract
Large visual language models (VLMs) have shown strong multi-modal medical reasoning ability, but most operate as end-to-end black boxes, diverging from clinicians' evidence-based, staged workflows and hindering clinical accountability. Complementarily, expert visual grounding models can accurately localize regions of interest (ROIs), providing explicit, reliable evidence that improves both reasoning accuracy and trust. In this paper, we introduce CARE, advancing Clinical Accountability in multi-modal medical Reasoning with an Evidence-grounded agentic framework. Unlike existing approaches that couple grounding and reasoning within a single generalist model, CARE decomposes the task into coordinated sub-modules to reduce shortcut learning and hallucination: a compact VLM proposes relevant medical entities; an expert entity-referring segmentation model produces pixel-level ROI evidence; and a grounded VLM reasons over the full image augmented by ROI hints. The VLMs are optimized with reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards to align answers with supporting evidence. Furthermore, a VLM coordinator plans tool invocation and reviews evidence-answer consistency, providing agentic control and final verification. Evaluated on standard medical VQA benchmarks, our CARE-Flow (coordinator-free) improves average accuracy by 10.9% over the same size (10B) state-of-the-art (SOTA). With dynamic planning and answer review, our CARE-Coord yields a further gain, outperforming the heavily pre-trained SOTA by 5.2%. Our experiments demonstrate that an agentic framework that emulates clinical workflows, incorporating decoupled specialized models and explicit evidence, yields more accurate and accountable medical AI. Project page: https://xypb.github.io/CARE-Project-Page/
中文标题/摘要
标题：CARE：基于证据驱动的智能体框架实现多模态医学推理的临床可问责性
大规模视觉语言模型（VLMs）已展现出强大的多模态医学推理能力，但多数模型作为端到端黑箱运行，与临床医生基于证据的分阶段工作流程相悖，且阻碍临床可问责性。互补性地，专家级视觉定位模型能精准定位感兴趣区域（ROIs），提供显式可靠的证据以提升推理准确性与可信度。本文提出CARE框架，通过证据驱动的智能体架构推进多模态医学推理的临床可问责性。与现有将定位与推理耦合于单一通用模型的方法不同，CARE将任务分解为协同子模块以减少捷径学习与幻觉：紧凑型VLM提议相关医学实体；专家级实体参照分割模型生成像素级ROI证据；基于证据的VLM结合ROI提示对完整图像进行推理。VLMs通过可验证奖励的强化学习进行优化，使答案与支持证据对齐。此外，VLM协调器规划工具调用并核查证据-答案一致性，提供智能体控制与最终验证。在标准医学VQA基准测试中，CARE-Flow（无协调器版本）较同规模（100亿参数）的先进模型平均准确率提升10.9%；结合动态规划与答案审查的CARE-Coord进一步获得增益，超越强预训练先进模型5.2%。实验表明，模拟临床工作流程、融合解耦专用模型与显式证据的智能体框架能产生更精准、可问责的医学人工智能。项目页面：https://xypb.github.io/CARE-Project-Page/
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the lack of clinical accountability in existing large visual language models (VLMs) for medical reasoning, which operate as black boxes unlike clinicians' evidence-based workflows. The proposed method, CARE, introduces an agentic framework that decomposes the task into coordinated sub-modules: a compact VLM proposes medical entities, an expert segmentation model provides pixel-level region-of-interest evidence, and a grounded VLM reasons over the image augmented with this evidence, all optimized with reinforcement learning using verifiable rewards. Experimental results on medical VQA benchmarks show that CARE-Flow improves average accuracy by 10.9% over a same-size state-of-the-art model, and CARE-Coord with dynamic planning further outperforms heavily pre-trained SOTA by 5.2%, demonstrating that emulating clinical workflows with explicit evidence enhances accuracy and accountability.

Reinforcement Learning with Conditional Expectation Reward
Authors: Changyi Xiao, Caijun Xu, Yixin Cao
First: 2026-03-11T10:36:27+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-11T10:36:27+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) has proven effective in enhancing the reasoning capabilities of large language models, particularly in domains such as mathematics where reliable rule-based verifiers can be constructed. However, the reliance on handcrafted, domain-specific verification rules substantially limits the applicability of RLVR to general reasoning domains with free-form answers, where valid answers often exhibit significant variability, making it difficult to establish complete and accurate rules. To address this limitation, we propose Conditional Expectation Reward (CER), which leverages the large language model itself as an implicit verifier, and is therefore applicable to general domains and eliminates the need for external verifiers or auxiliary models. CER is defined as the expected likelihood of generating the reference answer conditioned on the generated answer. In contrast to rule-based verifiers that yield binary feedback, CER provides a soft, graded reward signal that reflects varying degrees of correctness, making it better suited to tasks where answers vary in correctness. Experimental results demonstrate that CER is effective across a wide range of reasoning tasks, spanning both mathematical and general domains, indicating that CER serves as a flexible and general verification mechanism. The code is available at https://github.com/changyi7231/CER.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于条件期望奖励的强化学习
可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR）已被证明能有效提升大语言模型的推理能力，尤其在数学等可构建可靠规则验证器的领域。然而，依赖手工构建的领域特定验证规则极大限制了RLVR在自由形式答案的通用推理领域的适用性，因为有效答案通常存在显著差异，难以建立完整准确的规则。为解决这一局限，我们提出条件期望奖励（CER），其利用大语言模型自身作为隐式验证器，从而适用于通用领域，无需外部验证器或辅助模型。CER定义为在生成答案条件下生成参考答案的期望似然。与产生二元反馈的规则验证器不同，CER提供反映不同程度正确性的软性分级奖励信号，更适用于答案正确性存在差异的任务。实验结果表明，CER在数学和通用领域的广泛推理任务中均有效，表明CER是一种灵活通用的验证机制。代码发布于https://github.com/changyi7231/CER。

The paper addresses the limitation of Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR), which relies on handcrafted, domain-specific verification rules that restrict its applicability to general reasoning domains with free-form answers. To overcome this, the authors propose Conditional Expectation Reward (CER), a method that uses the large language model itself as an implicit verifier, eliminating the need for external tools by defining the reward as the expected likelihood of generating a reference answer conditioned on the generated answer, providing a soft, graded signal rather than binary feedback. Experimental results show that CER is effective across a wide range of reasoning tasks, including both mathematical and general domains, demonstrating its flexibility as a general verification mechanism.
本文针对可验证奖励强化学习（RLVR）的局限性展开研究，该方法依赖手工构建的领域特定验证规则，限制了其在具有自由形式答案的通用推理领域的适用性。为解决这一问题，作者提出了条件期望奖励（CER）方法，该方法利用大语言模型自身作为隐式验证器，通过将奖励定义为基于生成答案条件下生成参考答案的期望似然，从而无需外部工具，并提供软性、分级的反馈信号而非二元判断。实验结果表明，CER在包括数学和通用领域在内的多种推理任务中均有效，证明了其作为一种灵活通用验证机制的能力。
Does LLM Alignment Really Need Diversity? An Empirical Study of Adapting RLVR Methods for Moral Reasoning
Authors: Zhaowei Zhang, Xiaohan Liu, Xuekai Zhu, Junchao Huang, Ceyao Zhang, Zhiyuan Feng, Yaodong Yang, Xiaoyuan Yi, Xing Xie
First: 2026-03-11T09:45:30+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-11T09:45:30+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement learning with verifiable rewards (RLVR) has achieved remarkable success in logical reasoning tasks, yet whether large language model (LLM) alignment requires fundamentally different approaches remains unclear. Given the apparent tolerance for multiple valid responses in moral reasoning, a natural hypothesis is that alignment tasks inherently require diversity-seeking distribution-matching algorithms rather than reward-maximizing policy-based methods. We conduct the first comprehensive empirical study comparing both paradigms on MoReBench. To enable stable RLVR training, we build a rubric-grounded reward pipeline by training a Qwen3-1.7B judge model. Contrary to our hypothesis, we find that distribution-matching approaches do not demonstrate significant advantages over reward-maximizing methods as expected on alignment tasks. Through semantic visualization mapping high-reward responses to semantic space, we demonstrate that moral reasoning exhibits more concentrated high-reward distributions than mathematical reasoning, where diverse solution strategies yield similarly high rewards. This counter-intuitive finding explains why mode-seeking optimization proves equally or more effective for alignment tasks. Our results suggest that alignment tasks do not inherently require diversity-preserving algorithms, and standard reward-maximizing RLVR methods can effectively transfer to moral reasoning without explicit diversity mechanisms.

标题：LLM对齐真的需要多样性吗？一项关于将RLVR方法应用于道德推理的实证研究
可验证奖励强化学习（RLVR）在逻辑推理任务中取得了显著成功，但大型语言模型（LLM）对齐是否需要根本不同的方法仍不明确。鉴于道德推理对多种有效回答的明显包容性，一个自然假设是对齐任务本质上需要寻求多样性的分布匹配算法，而非基于奖励最大化的策略方法。我们在MoReBench上首次进行了全面实证研究，比较这两种范式。为实现稳定的RLVR训练，我们通过训练Qwen3-1.7B评判模型构建了基于量规的奖励管道。与假设相反，我们发现分布匹配方法在对齐任务中并未如预期般展现出显著优于奖励最大化方法的优势。通过将高奖励回答映射到语义空间的语义可视化，我们证明道德推理的高奖励分布比数学推理更为集中，而后者中多样化的解决策略能产生相似的高奖励。这一反直觉的发现解释了为何寻求模态的优化在对齐任务中同样或更为有效。我们的结果表明，对齐任务并不固有地需要保持多样性的算法，标准的奖励最大化RLVR方法无需显式多样性机制即可有效迁移至道德推理。

Adaptive RAN Slicing Control via Reward-Free Self-Finetuning Agents
Authors: Yuanhao Li, Haozhe Wang, Geyong Min, Nektarios Georgalas, Wang Miao
First: 2026-03-11T09:14:56+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-11T09:14:56+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
The integration of Generative AI models into AI-native network systems offers a transformative path toward achieving autonomous and adaptive control. However, the application of such models to continuous control tasks is impeded by intrinsic architectural limitations, including finite context windows, the lack of explicit reward signals, and the degradation of the long context. This paper posits that the key to unlocking robust continuous control is enabling agents to internalize experience by distilling it into their parameters, rather than relying on prompt-based memory. To this end, we propose a novel self-finetuning framework that enables agentic systems to learn continuously through direct interaction with the environment, bypassing the need for handcrafted rewards. Our framework implements a bi-perspective reflection mechanism that generates autonomous linguistic feedback to construct preference datasets from interaction history. A subsequent preference-based fine-tuning process distills long-horizon experiences into the model's parameters. We evaluate our approach on a dynamic Radio Access Network (RAN) slicing task, a challenging multi-objective control problem that requires the resolution of acute trade-offs between spectrum efficiency, service quality, and reconfiguration stability under volatile network conditions. Experimental results show that our framework outperforms standard Reinforcement Learning (RL) baselines and existing Large Language Model (LLM)-based agents in sample efficiency, stability, and multi-metric optimization. These findings demonstrate the potential of self-improving generative agents for continuous control tasks, paving the way for future AI-native network infrastructure.

TikArt: Stabilizing Aperture-Guided Fine-Grained Visual Reasoning with Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Hao Ding, Zhichuan Yang, Weijie Ge, Ziqin Gao, Chaoyi Lu, Lei Zhao
First: 2026-02-16T05:46:47+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-11T08:57:18+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Fine-grained visual reasoning in multimodal large language models (MLLMs) is bottlenecked by single-pass global image encoding: key evidence often lies in tiny objects, cluttered regions, subtle markings, or dense charts. We present \textbf{TikArt} (\textbf{T}h\textbf{i}n\textbf{k}ing \textbf{A}pe\textbf{rt}ure), an aperture-guided agent that formulates multimodal reasoning as sequential evidence acquisition over regions of interest. TikArt follows a Think--Aperture--Observe (TAO) loop that interleaves language reasoning with two aperture actions: Zoom, which extracts rectangular crops, and Segment, which invokes an off-the-shelf segmenter to produce object-centric mask-based views for irregular targets. A mandatory Observation step after every aperture action writes local evidence back into text, yielding interpretable aperture trajectories and persistent linguistic memory. Built on Qwen3-VL-8B, TikArt is trained with GRPO-style reinforcement learning under a two-stage curriculum. To stabilize long-horizon tool-integrated learning, we introduce Relative Uncertainty Reduction (RUR), a dense reward computed by a frozen evaluator that favors evidence-building trajectories and mitigates degenerate tool use. Experiments on high-resolution reasoning, general multimodal understanding, and both referring and reasoning-oriented segmentation show consistent gains over the backbone, demonstrating that aperture-guided observation improves fine-grained visual reasoning and transfers naturally to pixel-level grounding.
中文标题/摘要
标题：TikArt：基于强化学习的孔径引导细粒度视觉推理稳定化方法
多模态大语言模型（MLLMs）中的细粒度视觉推理受限于单次全局图像编码：关键证据常存在于微小物体、杂乱区域、细微标记或密集图表中。本文提出\textbf{TikArt}（\textbf{T}h\textbf{i}n\textbf{k}ing \textbf{A}pe\textbf{rt}ure），一种孔径引导智能体，将多模态推理建模为对感兴趣区域的序列化证据采集过程。TikArt遵循“思考-孔径-观察”（TAO）循环，交替进行语言推理与两种孔径操作：提取矩形裁剪的“缩放”操作，以及调用现成分割器生成面向不规则目标的掩码视图的“分割”操作。每次孔径操作后强制执行的观察步骤会将局部证据写回文本，形成可解释的孔径轨迹与持久性语言记忆。 基于Qwen3-VL-8B构建的TikArt采用两阶段课程学习，通过GRPO风格强化学习进行训练。为稳定长时程工具集成学习，我们提出相对不确定性降低（RUR）奖励机制——由冻结评估器计算的稠密奖励，该机制鼓励证据积累轨迹并抑制工具滥用。在高分辨率推理、通用多模态理解、指代与推理导向分割任务上的实验表明，该方法在基线上取得持续提升，证明孔径引导观察能有效改进细粒度视觉推理，并可自然迁移至像素级定位任务。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for TikArt stems from the limitations of single-pass global image encoding in multimodal large language models (MLLMs), which often fails to capture fine-grained details crucial for visual reasoning. The method introduces an aperture-guided agent that performs sequential evidence acquisition through a Think-Aperture-Observe loop, utilizing Zoom and Segment actions to extract detailed region-specific information and integrating observations into a persistent linguistic memory. Main experimental results demonstrate that TikArt, trained with reinforcement learning and a novel Relative Uncertainty Reduction reward, consistently outperforms its backbone model on high-resolution reasoning, general multimodal understanding, and segmentation tasks, showing improved fine-grained visual reasoning and pixel-level grounding.
TikArt的提出源于多模态大语言模型（MLLMs）中单次全局图像编码的局限性，该方式常无法捕捉对视觉推理至关重要的细粒度细节。该方法引入了一种孔径引导的智能体，通过“思考-孔径-观察”循环进行序列化证据采集，利用缩放和分割动作提取特定区域的详细信息，并将观察结果整合到持久的语言记忆中。主要实验结果表明，通过强化学习和新颖的相对不确定性降低奖励进行训练的TikArt，在高分辨率推理、通用多模态理解以及分割任务上均持续优于其基础模型，显示出在细粒度视觉推理和像素级定位方面的提升。
Learning to Score: Tuning Cluster Schedulers through Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Martin Asenov, Qiwen Deng, Gingfung Yeung, Adam Barker
First: 2026-03-11T08:54:30+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-11T08:54:30+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Efficiently allocating incoming jobs to nodes in large-scale clusters can lead to substantial improvements in both cluster utilization and job performance. In order to allocate incoming jobs, cluster schedulers usually rely on a set of scoring functions to rank feasible nodes. Results from individual scoring functions are usually weighted equally, which could lead to sub-optimal deployments as the one-size-fits-all solution does not take into account the characteristics of each workload. Tuning the weights of scoring functions, however, requires expert knowledge and is computationally expensive. This paper proposes a reinforcement learning approach for learning the weights in scheduler scoring algorithms with the overall objective of improving the end-to-end performance of jobs for a given cluster. Our approach is based on percentage improvement reward, frame-stacking, and limiting domain information. We propose a percentage improvement reward to address the objective of multi-step parameter tuning. The inclusion of frame-stacking allows for carrying information across an optimization experiment. Limiting domain information prevents overfitting and improves performance in unseen clusters and workloads. The policy is trained on different combinations of workloads and cluster setups. We demonstrate the proposed approach improves performance on average by 33\% compared to fixed weights and 12\% compared to the best-performing baseline in a lab-based serverless scenario.
中文标题/摘要
标题：学习评分：通过强化学习优化集群调度器
在大规模集群中高效分配任务至节点可显著提升集群利用率和任务性能。集群调度器通常依赖一组评分函数对可行节点排序，但各评分函数的结果常被等权重处理，这种通用方案未考虑各工作负载特性，可能导致次优部署。调整评分函数权重需专业知识且计算成本高昂。本文提出一种强化学习方法，以提升特定集群任务端到端性能为目标，学习调度器评分算法中的权重。该方法基于百分比改进奖励、帧堆叠和领域信息限制：百分比改进奖励用于多步参数调优；帧堆叠可在优化实验中传递信息；限制领域信息防止过拟合并提升在未知集群与工作负载中的性能。策略通过不同工作负载与集群配置组合训练，实验表明，在实验室无服务器场景中，该方法相比固定权重平均性能提升33%，较最佳基线提升12%。
Summary / 总结
The paper is motivated by the need to improve cluster utilization and job performance by moving beyond the sub-optimal, equal weighting of scoring functions in cluster schedulers, which fails to account for workload characteristics and is difficult to tune manually. The method introduces a reinforcement learning framework that learns optimal weights for scheduler scoring algorithms, employing techniques like a percentage improvement reward for multi-step tuning, frame-stacking to retain information across experiments, and limiting domain information to enhance generalization. Experimental results demonstrate that this approach yields substantial performance gains, improving job performance by an average of 33% over fixed-weight schedulers and 12% over the best baseline in a lab-based serverless environment.
本文的动机在于，集群调度器中评分函数的等权重分配无法考虑工作负载特性且难以手动调整，导致次优部署，因此需要提升集群利用率和作业性能。方法上，提出了一种强化学习框架来学习调度器评分算法的最优权重，采用了针对多步调优的百分比改进奖励、跨实验保留信息的帧堆叠技术，以及限制领域信息以提升泛化能力。主要实验结果表明，该方法在实验室无服务器场景中，相比固定权重调度器平均提升了33%的性能，相比最佳基线方法提升了12%。
DeepEyesV2: Toward Agentic Multimodal Model
Authors: Jack Hong, Chenxiao Zhao, ChengLin Zhu, Weiheng Lu, Guohai Xu, Xing Yu
First: 2025-11-07T14:31:20+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-11T08:46:41+00:00
Comments: Accepted to ICLR2026. Homepage: https://visual-agent.github.io/
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Project1
Abstract
Agentic multimodal models should not only comprehend text and images, but also actively invoke external tools, such as code execution environments and web search, and integrate these operations into reasoning. In this work, we introduce DeepEyesV2 and explore how to build an agentic multimodal model from the perspectives of data construction, training methods, and model evaluation. We observe that direct reinforcement learning alone fails to induce robust tool-use behavior. This phenomenon motivates a two-stage training pipeline: a cold-start stage to establish tool-use patterns, and reinforcement learning stage to further refine tool invocation. We curate a diverse, moderately challenging training dataset, specifically including examples where tool use is beneficial. We further introduce RealX-Bench, a comprehensive benchmark designed to evaluate real-world multimodal reasoning, which inherently requires the integration of multiple capabilities, including perception, search, and reasoning. We evaluate DeepEyesV2 on RealX-Bench and other representative benchmarks, demonstrating its effectiveness across real-world understanding, mathematical reasoning, and search-intensive tasks. Moreover, DeepEyesV2 exhibits task-adaptive tool invocation, tending to use image operations for perception tasks and numerical computations for reasoning tasks. Reinforcement learning further enables complex tool combinations and allows model to selectively invoke tools based on context. We hope our study can provide guidance for community in developing agentic multimodal models.
中文标题/摘要
标题：DeepEyesV2：迈向具身化多模态智能体模型
具身化多模态模型不仅需要理解文本与图像，还应能主动调用外部工具（如代码执行环境与网络搜索），并将这些操作整合至推理流程中。本研究提出DeepEyesV2，从数据构建、训练方法与模型评估三个维度探索如何构建具身化多模态模型。我们发现仅依靠直接强化学习难以形成稳健的工具使用行为，因此设计了两阶段训练流程：通过冷启动阶段建立工具使用范式，再经强化学习阶段优化工具调用机制。我们构建了多样化、适度挑战性的训练数据集，特别纳入工具使用具有显著增益的示例。同时提出RealX-Bench综合评估基准，专门检验需融合感知、搜索与推理能力的真实场景多模态推理。在RealX-Bench及其他代表性基准测试中，DeepEyesV2在真实场景理解、数学推理与搜索密集型任务上均表现优异。该模型还展现出任务自适应的工具调用特性：感知任务倾向调用图像操作，推理任务偏好数值计算。强化学习进一步支持复杂工具组合调用，并能依据上下文选择性启用工具。本研究旨在为具身化多模态模型的开发提供方法论参考。

For evaluation, the authors introduce RealX-Bench, a comprehensive benchmark for real-world multimodal reasoning.
