Tackling Length Inflation Without Trade-offs: Group Relative Reward Rescaling for Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Zichao Li, Jie Lou, Fangchen Dong, Zhiyuan Fan, Mengjie Ren, Hongyu Lin, Xianpei Han, Debing Zhang, Le Sun, Yaojie Lu, Xing Yu
First: 2026-03-11T08:41:34+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-11T08:41:34+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement learning significantly enhances LLM capabilities but suffers from a critical issue: length inflation, where models adopt verbosity or inefficient reasoning to maximize rewards. Prior approaches struggle to address this challenge in a general and lossless manner, primarily because additive penalties introduce a compensatory effect that creates optimization shortcuts, while heuristic gating strategies lack generality beyond binary feedback. To bridge this gap, we present Group Relative Reward Rescaling (GR$^3$), which reframes length control as a multiplicative rescaling paradigm, effectively establishing a generalized, continuous, and reward-dependent gating mechanism. To further ensure lossless optimization, we incorporate group-relative regularization and advantage-aware calibration, which dynamically adapt length budgets to instance difficulty and preserve the advantage signal of high-quality trajectories. Empirically, across both RLHF and RLVR settings, GR$^3$~maintains training dynamics and downstream performance comparable to standard GRPO while significantly mitigating length inflation, outperforming state-of-the-art length-regularized baselines.
中文标题/摘要
标题：无权衡应对长度膨胀：强化学习的组相对奖励重标度方法
强化学习显著提升了大型语言模型的能力，但存在一个关键问题：长度膨胀，即模型为最大化奖励而采用冗长表达或低效推理。先前方法难以以通用且无损的方式解决这一挑战，主要因为加法惩罚会引入补偿效应从而产生优化捷径，而启发式门控策略在二元反馈之外缺乏普适性。为填补这一空白，我们提出组相对奖励重标度方法（GR$^3$），将长度控制重构为乘法重标度范式，有效建立了广义、连续且依赖奖励的门控机制。为进一步确保无损优化，我们引入组相对正则化与优势感知校准，动态调整长度预算以适应实例难度，并保留高质量轨迹的优势信号。实验表明，在RLHF和RLVR两种设置下，GR$^3$在保持与标准GRPO相当的训练动态和下游性能的同时，显著缓解了长度膨胀问题，其表现优于当前最先进的长度正则化基线方法。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the problem of length inflation in reinforcement learning for large language models, where models become verbose to maximize rewards, and prior methods either introduce optimization shortcuts with additive penalties or lack generality. The authors propose Group Relative Reward Rescaling (GR^3), a method that reframes length control as multiplicative rescaling with group-relative regularization and advantage-aware calibration to dynamically adapt length budgets based on instance difficulty while preserving high-quality trajectory signals. Experimental results in RLHF and RLVR settings show that GR^3 effectively mitigates length inflation without compromising training dynamics or downstream performance, outperforming existing length-regularized baselines.
本文针对强化学习在大语言模型中导致的长度膨胀问题展开研究，即模型为最大化奖励而变得冗长，先前方法因引入加性惩罚造成优化捷径或缺乏普适性。作者提出了组相对奖励重缩放方法，将长度控制重构为乘性重缩放范式，结合组相对正则化和优势感知校准，根据实例难度动态调整长度预算并保留高质量轨迹的优势信号。在RLHF和RLVR设置下的实验结果表明，该方法能显著缓解长度膨胀，同时保持与标准GRPO相当的训练动态和下游性能，优于现有长度正则化基线。
UAV-MARL: Multi-Agent Reinforcement Learning for Time-Critical and Dynamic Medical Supply Delivery
Authors: Islam Guven, Mehmet Parlak
First: 2026-03-11T08:31:52+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-11T08:31:52+00:00
Comments: 7 pages, 4 figures, 2 tables, conference
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Unmanned aerial vehicles (UAVs) are increasingly used to support time-critical medical supply delivery, providing rapid and flexible logistics during emergencies and resource shortages. However, effective deployment of UAV fleets requires coordination mechanisms capable of prioritizing medical requests, allocating limited aerial resources, and adapting delivery schedules under uncertain operational conditions. This paper presents a multi-agent reinforcement learning (MARL) framework for coordinating UAV fleets in stochastic medical delivery scenarios where requests vary in urgency, location, and delivery deadlines. The problem is formulated as a partially observable Markov decision process (POMDP) in which UAV agents maintain awareness of medical delivery demands while having limited visibility of other agents due to communication and localization constraints. The proposed framework employs Proximal Policy Optimization (PPO) as the primary learning algorithm and evaluates several variants, including asynchronous extensions, classical actor--critic methods, and architectural modifications to analyze scalability and performance trade-offs. The model is evaluated using real-world geographic data from selected clinics and hospitals extracted from the OpenStreetMap dataset. The framework provides a decision-support layer that prioritizes medical tasks, reallocates UAV resources in real time, and assists healthcare personnel in managing urgent logistics. Experimental results show that classical PPO achieves superior coordination performance compared to asynchronous and sequential learning strategies, highlighting the potential of reinforcement learning for adaptive and scalable UAV-assisted healthcare logistics.
中文标题/摘要
标题：UAV-MARL：面向时效性与动态医疗物资配送的多智能体强化学习
无人机正日益用于支持时效性医疗物资配送，在紧急情况和资源短缺时提供快速灵活的物流支持。然而，无人机编队的有效部署需要协调机制，能够优先处理医疗请求、分配有限的空中资源，并在不确定的操作条件下调整配送计划。本文提出一种多智能体强化学习框架，用于在随机医疗配送场景中协调无人机编队，其中请求的紧急程度、位置和配送截止时间各不相同。该问题被建模为部分可观测马尔可夫决策过程，无人机智能体需保持对医疗配送需求的感知，同时因通信和定位限制对其他智能体的可见性有限。所提框架采用近端策略优化作为主要学习算法，并评估了多种变体，包括异步扩展、经典演员-评论家方法及架构修改，以分析可扩展性与性能权衡。模型使用从OpenStreetMap数据集提取的选定诊所和医院真实地理数据进行评估。该框架提供决策支持层，可优先处理医疗任务、实时重新分配无人机资源，并协助医护人员管理紧急物流。实验结果表明，经典PPO相比异步和顺序学习策略实现了更优的协调性能，凸显了强化学习在自适应、可扩展无人机辅助医疗物流中的潜力。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need for rapid and flexible medical logistics during emergencies, this paper proposes a multi-agent reinforcement learning (MARL) framework to coordinate UAV fleets for time-critical medical supply delivery under stochastic demand and operational uncertainty. The method formulates the problem as a partially observable Markov decision process (POMDP) and employs Proximal Policy Optimization (PPO) as the core learning algorithm, evaluating variants including asynchronous extensions and architectural modifications for scalability. Experimental results using real-world geographic data from OpenStreetMap show that classical PPO achieves superior coordination performance compared to asynchronous and sequential strategies, demonstrating its potential for adaptive, real-time resource allocation in healthcare logistics.
本文针对紧急情况下对快速灵活医疗物流的需求，提出了一种多智能体强化学习框架，用于在随机需求和不确定操作条件下协调无人机机队进行时效性医疗物资配送。该方法将问题建模为部分可观测马尔可夫决策过程，并采用近端策略优化作为核心学习算法，评估了包括异步扩展和架构修改在内的多种变体以分析可扩展性。基于OpenStreetMap真实地理数据的实验结果表明，经典PPO相比异步和顺序学习策略实现了更优的协调性能，凸显了强化学习在自适应、实时医疗物流资源分配中的潜力。
IH-Challenge: A Training Dataset to Improve Instruction Hierarchy on Frontier LLMs
Authors: Chuan Guo, Juan Felipe Ceron Uribe, Sicheng Zhu, Christopher A. Choquette-Choo, Steph Lin, Nikhil Kandpal, Milad Nasr, Rai, Sam Toyer, Miles Wang, Yaodong Yu, Alex Beutel, Kai Xiao
First: 2026-03-11T08:27:09+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-11T08:27:09+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Instruction hierarchy (IH) defines how LLMs prioritize system, developer, user, and tool instructions under conflict, providing a concrete, trust-ordered policy for resolving instruction conflicts. IH is key to defending against jailbreaks, system prompt extractions, and agentic prompt injections. However, robust IH behavior is difficult to train: IH failures can be confounded with instruction-following failures, conflicts can be nuanced, and models can learn shortcuts such as overrefusing. We introduce IH-Challenge, a reinforcement learning training dataset, to address these difficulties. Fine-tuning GPT-5-Mini on IH-Challenge with online adversarial example generation improves IH robustness by +10.0% on average across 16 in-distribution, out-of-distribution, and human red-teaming benchmarks (84.1% to 94.1%), reduces unsafe behavior from 6.6% to 0.7% while improving helpfulness on general safety evaluations, and saturates an internal static agentic prompt injection evaluation, with minimal capability regression. We release the IH-Challenge dataset (https://huggingface.co/datasets/openai/ih-challenge) to support future research on robust instruction hierarchy.
中文标题/摘要
标题：IH-Challenge：提升前沿大语言模型指令层级理解的训练数据集
指令层级定义了大型语言模型在指令冲突时如何优先处理系统、开发者、用户和工具指令，为解决指令冲突提供了具体且可信度排序的策略框架。指令层级是防御越狱攻击、系统提示提取和智能体提示注入的关键能力。然而，稳健的指令层级行为难以训练：其失效可能与指令遵循失败相混淆，冲突可能具有细微差别，且模型可能习得过度拒绝等捷径策略。为此，我们推出强化学习训练数据集IH-Challenge以应对这些挑战。通过在线对抗样本生成对GPT-5-Mini进行IH-Challenge微调后，在16个分布内、分布外及人工红队评估基准上平均提升指令层级稳健性10.0%（84.1%→94.1%），将不安全行为从6.6%降至0.7%的同时提升通用安全评估中的助益性，并在内部静态智能体提示注入评估中达到饱和性能，且能力衰退极小。我们公开IH-Challenge数据集（https://huggingface.co/datasets/openai/ih-challenge）以支持未来关于稳健指令层级的研究。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for this work is to improve the robustness of large language models (LLMs) in handling conflicting instructions from different sources, a capability termed instruction hierarchy (IH), which is crucial for defending against security threats like jailbreaks and prompt injections. The method involves creating and releasing the IH-Challenge dataset, a reinforcement learning training resource designed to address the difficulties of training robust IH, such as nuanced conflicts and model shortcuts like overrefusal; the researchers fine-tuned GPT-5-Mini on this dataset with online adversarial example generation. The main experimental results show that this approach significantly enhances IH robustness, with an average improvement of +10.0% across 16 benchmarks, reduces unsafe behavior from 6.6% to 0.7% while maintaining helpfulness, and effectively mitigates agentic prompt injections with minimal regression in general capabilities.
本研究的动机是提升大语言模型在处理来自不同来源的冲突指令时的鲁棒性，这种能力称为指令层级，对于防御越狱和提示注入等安全威胁至关重要。方法上，研究团队创建并发布了IH-Challenge数据集，这是一个旨在解决训练鲁棒指令层级难点的强化学习训练资源，例如细微的冲突和模型捷径问题；研究人员基于该数据集，通过在线对抗样本生成对GPT-5-Mini进行了微调。主要实验结果表明，该方法显著增强了指令层级的鲁棒性，在16个基准测试中平均提升了10.0%，将不安全行为从6.6%降至0.7%同时保持了帮助性，并有效缓解了代理提示注入问题，且对模型整体能力影响最小。
Exploratory Optimal Stopping: A Singular Control Formulation
Authors: Jodi Dianetti, Giorgio Ferrari, Renyuan Xu
First: 2024-08-18T02:31:55+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-11T07:17:41+00:00
Comments: 49 pages, 3 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
This paper explores continuous-time and state-space optimal stopping problems from a reinforcement learning perspective. We begin by formulating the stopping problem using randomized stopping times, where the decision maker's control is represented by the probability of stopping within a given time-specifically, a bounded, non-decreasing, càdlàg control process. To encourage exploration and facilitate learning, we introduce a regularized version of the problem by penalizing the performance criterion with the cumulative residual entropy of the randomized stopping time. The regularized problem takes the form of an (n+1)-dimensional degenerate singular stochastic control with finite-fuel, where the regularized free boundary becomes the graph of a function mapping the state variable of the original stopping problem into the probability of stopping. We address this singular control problem through the dynamic programming principle, which enables us to identify the unique optimal exploratory strategy. Finally, we propose both model-based and model-free reinforcement learning algorithms tailored for exploratory optimal stopping problems. We establish policy improvement guarantees for the proposed algorithms. Moreover, the model-free method is of actor-critic type and it is scalable in high-dimensions under neural network parameterization.
中文标题/摘要
标题：探索性最优停止：奇异控制建模
本文从强化学习视角研究连续时间与状态空间的最优停止问题。首先通过随机化停止时间建立停止问题的数学模型，其中决策者的控制表现为给定时间内停止的概率——具体而言，是一个有界、非降的右连左极控制过程。为促进探索与学习，我们引入该问题的正则化版本，通过随机停止时间的累积残差熵对性能准则进行惩罚。正则化问题呈现为具有有限燃料的(n+1)维退化奇异随机控制形式，其正则化自由边界成为将原停止问题状态变量映射至停止概率的函数图像。我们通过动态规划原理处理该奇异控制问题，从而识别出唯一的最优探索策略。最后，我们提出分别适用于模型驱动与无模型场景的强化学习算法，专门针对探索性最优停止问题设计。我们为所提算法建立了策略改进保证。此外，无模型方法采用演员-评论家架构，在神经网络参数化下具备高维可扩展性。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need to incorporate exploration into continuous-time optimal stopping problems for reinforcement learning, this paper formulates the problem using randomized stopping times, where the control is a bounded, non-decreasing process representing the probability of stopping. The method introduces a regularization term based on cumulative residual entropy to encourage exploration, transforming the problem into a finite-fuel singular stochastic control problem, which is solved via the dynamic programming principle to derive a unique optimal exploratory strategy. Experimentally, the authors propose both model-based and model-free reinforcement learning algorithms, with the model-free actor-critic approach proving scalable in high-dimensional settings under neural network parameterization, and they establish policy improvement guarantees for these algorithms.
本文的动机是将探索机制引入连续时间最优停止问题以适用于强化学习，其方法采用随机化停止时间，将控制表示为停止概率的有界非递减过程。通过引入基于累积残差熵的正则化项来鼓励探索，将问题转化为有限燃料的奇异随机控制问题，并利用动态规划原理求解，从而得到唯一的最优探索策略。在实验结果方面，作者提出了基于模型和无模型的强化学习算法，其中无模型的演员-评论家方法在神经网络参数化下能适应高维场景，并证明了这些算法的策略改进保证。
Revisiting Value Iteration: Unified Analysis of Discounted and Average-Reward Cases
Authors: Arsenii Mustafin, Xinyi Sheng, Dominik Baumann
First: 2025-10-27T22:42:53+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-11T07:14:56+00:00
Comments: 22 pages, 2 figure
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
While Value Iteration (VI) is one of the most fundamental algorithms in Reinforcement Learning, its theoretical convergence guarantees still exhibit a persistent mismatch with empirical behavior. In the discounted-reward case, classical theory guarantees geometric convergence with rate $γ$, while in the average-reward case recent work suggests that only sublinear convergence can be expected. In practice, however, VI is often observed to converge significantly faster. In this work, we show through a unified geometry-based analysis that, under an assumption of a unique and unichain optimal policy, (i) convergence is geometric in both the discounted- and average-reward settings and (ii) the convergence rate is faster than previous analyses suggest.
中文标题/摘要
标题：重访价值迭代：折扣与平均奖励情形的统一分析
价值迭代（VI）是强化学习中最基础的算法之一，但其理论收敛保证与实证行为之间仍存在持续的不匹配。在折扣奖励情形中，经典理论保证以速率$γ$几何收敛；而在平均奖励情形中，近期研究表明仅能预期次线性收敛。然而，实践中常观察到VI收敛速度显著更快。本文通过基于几何的统一分析证明，在假设存在唯一且单链最优策略的条件下：（i）折扣奖励与平均奖励情形下均呈几何收敛；（ii）收敛速率快于先前分析所预测。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the persistent mismatch between theoretical convergence guarantees and empirical performance of Value Iteration (VI) in reinforcement learning, where classical theory predicts slower geometric or sublinear rates than typically observed in practice. The authors propose a unified geometry-based analysis, assuming a unique and unichain optimal policy, to demonstrate that VI actually achieves geometric convergence in both discounted- and average-reward settings. Their main experimental results confirm that the convergence rate is faster than previously suggested by earlier analyses, bridging the gap between theory and practical observations.
本文针对强化学习中值迭代算法的理论收敛保证与实证性能之间的持续不匹配问题展开研究，经典理论预测的收敛速度通常慢于实际观察到的速度。作者提出了一种基于几何的统一分析方法，在假设存在唯一且单链最优策略的条件下，证明了值迭代在折扣奖励和平均奖励两种设置下均能达到几何收敛。主要实验结果表明，其收敛速度比先前分析所暗示的要更快，从而弥合了理论与实际观察之间的差距。
Muscle Synergy Priors Enhance Biomechanical Fidelity in Predictive Musculoskeletal Locomotion Simulation
Authors: Ilseung Park, Eunsik Choi, Jangwhan Ahn, Jooeun Ahn
First: 2026-03-11T06:48:15+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-11T06:48:15+00:00
Comments: 12 pages, 5 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Human locomotion emerges from high-dimensional neuromuscular control, making predictive musculoskeletal simulation challenging. We present a physiology-informed reinforcement-learning framework that constrains control using muscle synergies. We extracted a low-dimensional synergy basis from inverse musculoskeletal analyses of a small set of overground walking trials and used it as the action space for a muscle-driven three-dimensional model trained across variable speeds, slopes and uneven terrain. The resulting controller generated stable gait from 0.7-1.8 m/s and on $\pm$ 6$^{\circ}$ grades and reproduced condition-dependent modulation of joint angles, joint moments and ground reaction forces. Compared with an unconstrained controller, synergy-constrained control reduced non-physiological knee kinematics and kept knee moment profiles within the experimental envelope. Across conditions, simulated vertical ground reaction forces correlated strongly with human measurements, and muscle-activation timing largely fell within inter-subject variability. These results show that embedding neurophysiological structure into reinforcement learning can improve biomechanical fidelity and generalization in predictive human locomotion simulation with limited experimental data.
中文标题/摘要
标题：肌肉协同先验增强预测性肌肉骨骼运动模拟的生物力学保真度

Summary / 总结
The study addresses the challenge of simulating human locomotion by integrating neurophysiological priors into a reinforcement learning framework to enhance biomechanical realism. The method involves extracting low-dimensional muscle synergies from experimental walking data and using them as constraints in a muscle-driven 3D model trained across diverse conditions like speed, slope, and terrain. Experimental results show that the synergy-constrained controller generated stable gait across a range of speeds and slopes, improved knee kinematics and moments compared to an unconstrained approach, and produced ground reaction forces and muscle activations that closely matched human experimental data, demonstrating better generalization with limited data.
该研究针对人体运动模拟的挑战，通过将神经生理学先验知识融入强化学习框架，以提高生物力学保真度。方法是从少量实验步行数据中提取低维肌肉协同作用，并将其作为约束应用于肌肉驱动的三维模型，在多种速度、坡度和不平坦地形条件下进行训练。实验结果表明，协同约束控制器在多种条件下生成了稳定的步态，与非约束控制器相比，改善了膝关节运动学和力矩，模拟的垂直地面反作用力与人类测量数据高度相关，肌肉激活时序也基本落在受试者间变异范围内，证明了在有限实验数据下具有更好的泛化能力。
MemOCR: Layout-Aware Visual Memory for Efficient Long-Horizon Reasoning
Authors: Yaorui Shi, Shugui Liu, Yu Yang, Wenyu Mao, Yuxin Chen, Qi GU, Hui Su, Xunliang Cai, Xiang Wang, An Zhang
First: 2026-01-29T09:47:17+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-11T06:10:35+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Long-horizon agentic reasoning necessitates effectively compressing growing interaction histories into a limited context window. Most existing memory systems serialize history as text, where token-level cost is uniform and scales linearly with length, often spending scarce budget on low-value details. To this end, we introduce MemOCR, a multimodal memory agent that improves long-horizon reasoning under tight context budgets by allocating memory space with adaptive information density through visual layout. Concretely, MemOCR maintains a structured rich-text memory (e.g., headings, highlights) and renders it into an image that the agent consults for memory access, visually prioritizing crucial evidence while aggressively compressing auxiliary details. To ensure robustness across varying memory budgets, we train MemOCR with reinforcement learning under budget-aware objectives that expose the agent to diverse compression levels. Across long-context multi-hop and single-hop question-answering benchmarks, MemOCR outperforms strong text-based baselines and achieves more effective context utilization under extreme budgets.
中文标题/摘要
标题：MemOCR：面向高效长程推理的布局感知视觉记忆系统
长程智能体推理需将不断增长的交互历史有效压缩至有限上下文窗口。现有记忆系统多将历史序列化为文本，其词元级成本固定且随长度线性增长，常将稀缺资源消耗于低价值细节。为此，我们提出MemOCR——一种多模态记忆智能体，通过视觉布局实现自适应信息密度的记忆空间分配，从而提升严格上下文预算下的长程推理能力。具体而言，MemOCR维护结构化富文本记忆（如标题、高亮内容），并将其渲染为智能体查询记忆的图像，在视觉层面突出关键证据的同时对辅助细节进行激进压缩。为确保不同记忆预算下的鲁棒性，我们采用预算感知的强化学习目标训练MemOCR，使智能体适应多级压缩场景。在长上下文多跳与单跳问答基准测试中，MemOCR优于强文本基线，并在极端预算下实现更高效的上下文利用。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the challenge of efficiently compressing long interaction histories for agentic reasoning within limited context windows, noting that existing text-based memory systems allocate token budgets uniformly and thus waste capacity on low-value details. To overcome this, the authors propose MemOCR, a multimodal memory agent that uses visual layout to adaptively allocate memory space with varying information density, structuring rich-text memory into rendered images that visually prioritize crucial evidence while compressing auxiliary details. Through reinforcement learning trained with budget-aware objectives across diverse compression levels, MemOCR demonstrates superior performance over text-based baselines on long-context multi-hop and single-hop QA benchmarks, achieving more effective context utilization under extreme budget constraints.
本文针对智能体在有限上下文窗口内高效压缩长交互历史的挑战，指出现有基于文本的记忆系统均匀分配令牌预算，导致在低价值细节上浪费容量。为此，作者提出MemOCR，一种多模态记忆代理，利用视觉布局自适应分配具有不同信息密度的内存空间，将结构化富文本记忆渲染为图像，从而视觉上优先呈现关键证据并压缩辅助细节。通过基于预算感知目标的强化学习训练，MemOCR在不同压缩级别下表现出色，在长上下文多跳和单跳问答基准测试中优于强文本基线，并在极端预算条件下实现了更有效的上下文利用。
GTR-Turbo: Merged Checkpoint is Secretly a Free Teacher for Agentic VLM Training
Authors: Tong Wei, Yijun Yang, Changhao Zhang, Junliang Xing, Yuanchun Shi, Zongqing Lu, Deheng Ye
Venue: CVPR 2026
First: 2025-12-15T07:11:56+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-11T05:58:08+00:00
Comments: Accepted by CVPR 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Multi-turn reinforcement learning (RL) for multi-modal agents built upon vision-language models (VLMs) is hampered by sparse rewards and long-horizon credit assignment. Recent methods densify the reward by querying a teacher that provides step-level feedback, e.g., Guided Thought Reinforcement (GTR) and On-Policy Distillation, but rely on costly, often privileged models as the teacher, limiting practicality and reproducibility. We introduce GTR-Turbo, a highly efficient upgrade to GTR that matches its performance without training on or querying an expensive teacher model. Specifically, GTR-Turbo merges the weights of checkpoints produced during ongoing RL training and then uses the resulting merged model as a "free" teacher to guide subsequent RL via supervised fine-tuning or soft logit distillation. This design removes dependence on privileged VLMs (e.g., GPT or Gemini), mitigates the "entropy collapse" observed in prior work, and maintains stable training. Across diverse visual agentic tasks, GTR-Turbo improves the accuracy of the baseline model by 10-30% while reducing wall-clock training time by 50% and compute cost by 60% relative to GTR.
中文标题/摘要
标题：GTR-Turbo：合并检查点在智能体化视觉语言模型训练中实为免费教师
基于视觉语言模型（VLM）构建的多模态智能体在多轮强化学习（RL）中面临奖励稀疏与长程信用分配的挑战。现有方法通过查询提供步骤级反馈的教师模型（如引导思维强化GTR与同策略蒸馏）来稠化奖励，但依赖昂贵且通常具有特权访问权限的教师模型，限制了实用性与可复现性。本文提出GTR-Turbo——一种对GTR的高效升级方案，在不训练或查询昂贵教师模型的情况下达到同等性能。具体而言，GTR-Turbo合并持续RL训练过程中产生的检查点权重，将所得合并模型作为“免费”教师，通过监督微调或软逻辑蒸馏指导后续RL训练。该设计消除了对特权VLM（如GPT或Gemini）的依赖，缓解了先前工作中观察到的“熵崩溃”现象，并保持训练稳定性。在多样化视觉智能体任务中，相较于GTR，GTR-Turbo将基线模型准确率提升10-30%，同时减少50%的挂钟训练时间与60%的计算成本。

The motivation for this work is to overcome the limitations of multi-turn reinforcement learning for vision-language agents, which suffers from sparse rewards and requires costly privileged teacher models for step-level feedback. The method introduces GTR-Turbo, which merges the weights of checkpoints generated during ongoing RL training and uses this merged model as a free teacher to guide subsequent training via supervised fine-tuning or soft logit distillation. Experimental results show that across diverse visual agentic tasks, GTR-Turbo improves baseline model accuracy by 10-30% while reducing wall-clock training time by 50% and compute cost by 60% compared to prior methods, all without requiring expensive external teacher models.
本研究旨在解决视觉语言智能体在多轮强化学习中面临的奖励稀疏和依赖昂贵特权教师模型的问题。该方法提出了GTR-Turbo，通过合并持续强化学习训练中产生的检查点权重，并将合并后的模型作为免费教师，通过监督微调或软对数蒸馏来指导后续训练。实验结果表明，在多种视觉智能体任务中，GTR-Turbo将基线模型的准确率提升了10-30%，同时相比先前方法减少了50%的训练时间和60%的计算成本，且无需依赖昂贵的外部教师模型。
ToolRLA: Multiplicative Reward Decomposition for Tool-Integrated Agents
Authors: Pengbo Liu
First: 2026-03-02T08:52:14+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-11T05:50:54+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Tool-integrated agents that interleave reasoning with API calls are promising for complex tasks, yet aligning them for high-stakes, domain-specific deployment remains challenging: existing reinforcement learning approaches rely on coarse binary rewards that cannot distinguish tool selection errors from malformed parameters. We present ToolRLA, a three-stage post-training pipeline (SFT -> GRPO -> DPO) for domain-specific tool agents. The core contribution is a fine-grained reward function with multiplicative correctness decomposition spanning four dimensions -- format validity, tool selection, parameter accuracy, and regulatory compliance -- that encodes domain priority orderings as inductive biases in the reward landscape. Deployed on a financial advisory copilot (80+ advisors, 1,200+ daily queries), ToolRLA achieves over three months: a 47% improvement in task completion rate (62%->91%), a 63% reduction in tool invocation errors (38%->14%), and a 93% reduction in regulatory violations (12%->0.8%), within sub-2-second latency. Ablation studies show the multiplicative reward design accounts for 7 percentage points of improvement over additive alternatives. Generalization is further validated on ToolBench and API-Bank.
中文标题/摘要
标题：ToolRLA：面向工具集成智能体的乘性奖励分解框架
融合推理与API调用的工具集成智能体在复杂任务中前景广阔，但针对高风险领域特定场景的对齐部署仍具挑战：现有强化学习方法依赖粗粒度二元奖励，无法区分工具选择错误与参数格式错误。本文提出ToolRLA——面向领域特定工具智能体的三阶段后训练流程（监督微调→分组相对策略优化→直接偏好优化），其核心贡献在于构建了跨四维度的细粒度乘性奖励函数：格式有效性、工具选择、参数准确性、合规性检查，通过将领域优先级编码为奖励空间的归纳偏置实现精细优化。在金融顾问协理系统（覆盖80+顾问，日均1200+查询）的部署中，ToolRLA在三个月内实现：任务完成率提升47%（62%→91%），工具调用错误减少63%（38%→14%），违规操作降低93%（12%→0.8%），且响应延迟低于2秒。消融实验表明乘性奖励设计较加性方案额外贡献7个百分点的性能提升，在ToolBench与API-Bank基准上的实验进一步验证了框架的泛化能力。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the challenge of aligning tool-integrated agents for high-stakes, domain-specific tasks, where existing reinforcement learning methods suffer from coarse binary rewards that fail to differentiate between types of errors like tool selection and parameter malformation. The authors propose ToolRLA, a three-stage post-training pipeline involving supervised fine-tuning, group relative policy optimization, and direct preference optimization, with a core innovation being a fine-grained multiplicative reward function that decomposes correctness into four dimensions—format validity, tool selection, parameter accuracy, and regulatory compliance—to encode domain priorities as inductive biases. Experimental results from deployment on a financial advisory copilot show significant improvements over three months: a 47% increase in task completion rate (from 62% to 91%), a 63% reduction in tool invocation errors (from 38% to 14%), and a 93% reduction in regulatory violations (from 12% to 0.8%), all while maintaining sub-2-second latency, with ablation studies confirming the superiority of the multiplicative reward design over additive alternatives and generalization validated on additional benchmarks.
本文针对高风险、特定领域任务中工具集成智能体的对齐挑战，现有强化学习方法依赖粗糙的二元奖励，无法区分工具选择错误与参数格式错误等问题。作者提出了ToolRLA，这是一个包含监督微调、组相对策略优化和直接偏好优化的三阶段后训练流程，其核心贡献在于细粒度的乘法奖励函数，将正确性分解为四个维度——格式有效性、工具选择、参数准确性和法规遵从性——以领域优先级作为归纳偏置编码到奖励景观中。在金融顾问助手上的部署实验显示，三个月内任务完成率提升了47%（从62%至91%），工具调用错误减少了63%（从38%至14%），违规行为降低了93%（从12%至0.8%），同时保持亚2秒延迟，消融研究表明乘法奖励设计比加法替代方案带来7个百分点的改进，并在其他基准上验证了泛化能力。
SPAARS: Safer RL Policy Alignment through Abstract Exploration and Refined Exploitation of Action Space
Authors: Swaminathan S K, Aritra Hazra
First: 2026-03-10T08:52:15+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-11T05:45:21+00:00
Comments: 9 pages
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Offline-to-online reinforcement learning (RL) offers a promising paradigm for robotics by pre-training policies on safe, offline demonstrations and fine-tuning them via online interaction. However, a fundamental challenge remains: how to safely explore online without deviating from the behavioral support of the offline data? While recent methods leverage conditional variational autoencoders (CVAEs) to bound exploration within a latent space, they inherently suffer from an exploitation gap -- a performance ceiling imposed by the decoder's reconstruction loss. We introduce SPAARS, a curriculum learning framework that initially constrains exploration to the low-dimensional latent manifold for sample-efficient, safe behavioral improvement, then seamlessly transfers control to the raw action space, bypassing the decoder bottleneck. SPAARS has two instantiations: the CVAE-based variant requires only unordered (s,a) pairs and no trajectory segmentation; SPAARS-SUPE pairs SPAARS with OPAL temporal skill pretraining for stronger exploration structure at the cost of requiring trajectory chunks. We prove an upper bound on the exploitation gap using the Performance Difference Lemma, establish that latent-space policy gradients achieve provable variance reduction over raw-space exploration, and show that concurrent behavioral cloning during the latent phase directly controls curriculum transition stability. Empirically, SPAARS-SUPE achieves 0.825 normalized return on kitchen-mixed-v0 versus 0.75 for SUPE, with 5x better sample efficiency; standalone SPAARS achieves 92.7 and 102.9 normalized return on hopper-medium-v2 and walker2d-medium-v2 respectively, surpassing IQL baselines of 66.3 and 78.3 respectively, confirming the utility of the unordered-pair CVAE instantiation.
中文标题/摘要
标题：SPAARS：通过抽象探索与精细化动作空间利用实现更安全的强化学习策略对齐
离线到在线强化学习（RL）通过离线安全演示预训练策略并在线交互微调，为机器人学提供了前景广阔的研究范式。然而，核心挑战依然存在：如何在不偏离离线数据行为支持的前提下安全进行在线探索？现有方法虽利用条件变分自编码器（CVAE）将探索限制在潜在空间，却因解码器重构损失导致固有的利用缺口——即性能上限瓶颈。本文提出SPAARS课程学习框架：初期将探索约束在低维潜在流形以实现样本高效的安全行为改进，随后无缝切换至原始动作空间以规避解码器瓶颈。SPAARS具有两种实现形式：基于CVAE的变体仅需无序状态-动作对且无需轨迹分割；SPAARS-SUPE将SPAARS与OPAL时序技能预训练结合，以轨迹片段为代价获得更强的探索结构。我们通过性能差异引理证明了利用缺口的上界，论证了潜在空间策略梯度相比原始空间探索可实现可证明的方差缩减，并表明潜在阶段并行的行为克隆能直接控制课程转换稳定性。实验表明：在kitchen-mixed-v0任务中，SPAARS-SUPE获得0.825标准化回报（SUPE为0.75）且样本效率提升5倍；独立SPAARS在hopper-medium-v2和walker2d-medium-v2任务中分别获得92.7和102.9标准化回报，显著超越IQL基线的66.3和78.3，验证了无序对CVAE实现的有效性。

The paper introduces SPAARS, a curriculum learning framework for safer offline-to-online reinforcement learning in robotics, motivated by the challenge of safely exploring online without deviating from offline data support while overcoming the performance ceiling imposed by prior latent-space methods. The method initially constrains exploration to a low-dimensional latent manifold for safe, sample-efficient improvement and then transfers control to the raw action space to bypass decoder bottlenecks, with two instantiations: a CVAE-based variant using unordered state-action pairs and SPAARS-SUPE, which incorporates temporal skill pretraining for stronger exploration. Adaptive Active Learning for Regression via Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Simon D. Nguyen, Troy Russo, Kentaro Hoffman, Tyler H. McCormick
First: 2026-03-11T05:33:07+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-11T05:33:07+00:00
Comments: 33 pages, 103 figures. Main paper (8 pages, 4 figures) plus appendix with proofs and supplemental experimental results. Submitted to UAI2026. Codebase available at https://github.com/thatswhatsimonsaid/WeightedGreedySampling
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Active learning for regression reduces labeling costs by selecting the most informative samples. Improved Greedy Sampling is a prominent method that balances feature-space diversity and output-space uncertainty using a static, multiplicative rule. We propose Weighted improved Greedy Sampling (WiGS), which replaces this framework with a dynamic, additive criterion. We formulate weight selection as a reinforcement learning problem, enabling an agent to adapt the exploration-investigation balance throughout learning. Experiments on 18 benchmark datasets and a synthetic environment show WiGS outperforms iGS and other baseline methods in both accuracy and labeling efficiency, particularly in domains with irregular data density where the baseline's multiplicative rule ignores high-error samples in dense regions.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于强化学习的回归自适应主动学习
回归主动学习通过选择信息量最大的样本来降低标注成本。改进型贪婪采样是一种主流方法，采用静态乘法规则平衡特征空间多样性与输出空间不确定性。本文提出加权改进型贪婪采样，以动态加法准则替代原有框架，并将权重选择构建为强化学习问题，使智能体能在学习过程中自适应调整探索与利用的平衡。在18个基准数据集和合成环境上的实验表明，WiGS在准确率和标注效率上均优于iGS及其他基线方法，尤其在数据密度分布不均的场景中，基线方法的乘法规则会忽略密集区域的高误差样本。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the need for more efficient active learning in regression tasks by improving upon the Improved Greedy Sampling (iGS) method, which uses a static multiplicative rule to balance diversity and uncertainty. The authors propose Weighted improved Greedy Sampling (WiGS), which introduces a dynamic additive criterion where weight selection is formulated as a reinforcement learning problem, allowing adaptive tuning of the exploration-investigation trade-off. Experimental results on 18 benchmark datasets and a synthetic environment demonstrate that WiGS outperforms iGS and other baselines in accuracy and labeling efficiency, especially in scenarios with irregular data density where traditional methods may overlook high-error samples in dense regions.

Scalable Multi-Task Learning through Spiking Neural Networks with Adaptive Task-Switching Policy for Intelligent Autonomous Agents
Authors: Rachmad Vidya Wicaksana Putra, Avaneesh Devkota, Muhammad Shafique
First: 2025-04-18T08:12:59+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-11T04:56:38+00:00
Comments: Accepted at the 63rd ACM/IEEE Design Automation Conference (DAC), July 26-29, 2026 in Long Beach, CA, USA Codes: https://github.com/rachmadvwp/SwitchMT
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Training resource-constrained autonomous agents on multiple tasks simultaneously is crucial for adapting to diverse real-world environments. Recent works employ reinforcement learning (RL) approach, but they still suffer from sub-optimal multi-task performance due to task interference. State-of-the-art works employ Spiking Neural Networks (SNNs) to improve RL-based multi-task learning and enable low-power/energy operations through network enhancements and spike-driven data stream processing. However, they rely on fixed task-switching intervals during its training, thus limiting its performance and scalability. To address this, we propose SwitchMT, a novel methodology that employs adaptive task-switching for effective, scalable, and simultaneous multi-task learning. SwitchMT employs the following key ideas: (1) leveraging a Deep Spiking Q-Network with active dendrites and dueling structure, that utilizes task-specific context signals to create specialized sub-networks; and (2) devising an adaptive task-switching policy that leverages both rewards and internal dynamics of the network parameters. Experimental results demonstrate that SwitchMT achieves competitive scores in multiple Atari games (i.e., Pong: -8.8, Breakout: 5.6, and Enduro: 355.2) and longer game episodes as compared to the state-of-the-art. These results also highlight the effectiveness of SwitchMT methodology in addressing task interference without increasing the network complexity, enabling intelligent autonomous agents with scalable multi-task learning capabilities.
中文标题/摘要
标题：面向智能自主体的可扩展多任务学习：基于脉冲神经网络与自适应任务切换策略
在资源受限的自主智能体上同时训练多任务对于适应多样化现实环境至关重要。现有研究多采用强化学习方法，但仍受任务干扰影响导致多任务性能欠佳。前沿工作通过脉冲神经网络改进基于强化学习的多任务学习，并借助网络增强与脉冲驱动数据流处理实现低功耗/低能耗运行。然而，这些方法在训练期间依赖固定任务切换间隔，限制了性能与可扩展性。为此，我们提出SwitchMT——一种采用自适应任务切换策略的新型方法，可实现高效、可扩展的同步多任务学习。SwitchMT的核心创新包括：（1）采用具有活跃树突与竞争结构的深度脉冲Q网络，利用任务特定上下文信号构建专用子网络；（2）设计融合奖励信号与网络参数内部动态的自适应任务切换策略。实验结果表明，相较于现有最优方法，SwitchMT在多个Atari游戏（Pong: -8.8分，Breakout: 5.6分，Enduro: 355.2分）中取得竞争优势，并能维持更长的游戏回合。这些结果凸显了SwitchMT在不增加网络复杂度的前提下有效解决任务干扰的能力，为智能自主体赋予了可扩展的多任务学习能力。

Experimental results on multiple Atari games show that SwitchMT achieves competitive scores, such as -8.8 in Pong, 5.6 in Breakout, and 355.2 in Enduro, and supports longer game episodes compared to state-of-the-art methods, effectively mitigating task interference without increasing network complexity.
本文针对资源受限的自主智能体在多任务强化学习中存在的任务干扰问题，该问题限制了其性能与可扩展性。所提出的SwitchMT方法在脉冲神经网络框架内引入了一种自适应任务切换策略，具体采用具有主动树突和竞争结构的深度脉冲Q网络，利用任务特定的上下文信号创建专用子网络。在多个Atari游戏上的实验结果表明，SwitchMT取得了有竞争力的分数，如在Pong中为-8.8、Breakout中为5.6、Enduro中为355.2，并且相比现有先进方法能支持更长的游戏回合，有效缓解了任务干扰且未增加网络复杂度。
Graph-GRPO: Training Graph Flow Models with Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Baoheng Zhu, Deyu Bo, Delvin Ce Zhang, Xiao Wang
First: 2026-03-11T04:20:45+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-11T04:20:45+00:00
Comments: Under Review
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Graph generation is a fundamental task with broad applications, such as drug discovery. Recently, discrete flow matching-based graph generation, \aka, graph flow model (GFM), has emerged due to its superior performance and flexible sampling. However, effectively aligning GFMs with complex human preferences or task-specific objectives remains a significant challenge. In this paper, we propose Graph-GRPO, an online reinforcement learning (RL) framework for training GFMs under verifiable rewards. Our method makes two key contributions: (1) We derive an analytical expression for the transition probability of GFMs, replacing the Monte Carlo sampling and enabling fully differentiable rollouts for RL training; (2) We propose a refinement strategy that randomly perturbs specific nodes and edges in a graph, and regenerates them, allowing for localized exploration and self-improvement of generation quality. Extensive experiments on both synthetic and real datasets demonstrate the effectiveness of Graph-GRPO. With only 50 denoising steps, our method achieves 95.0\% and 97.5\% Valid-Unique-Novelty scores on the planar and tree datasets, respectively. Moreover, Graph-GRPO achieves state-of-the-art performance on the molecular optimization tasks, outperforming graph-based and fragment-based RL methods as well as classic genetic algorithms.
中文标题/摘要
标题：Graph-GRPO：基于强化学习的图流模型训练
图生成是药物发现等广泛应用中的基础任务。近期，基于离散流匹配的图生成方法（即图流模型，GFM）因其优越性能和灵活采样而兴起，但如何有效使GFM与复杂的人类偏好或任务特定目标对齐仍是一大挑战。本文提出Graph-GRPO，一种在可验证奖励下训练GFM的在线强化学习框架。主要贡献包括：（1）推导出GFM转移概率的解析表达式，替代蒙特卡洛采样，实现完全可微分的强化学习训练过程；（2）提出一种优化策略，通过随机扰动图中特定节点与边并重新生成，实现局部探索与生成质量的自我提升。在合成与真实数据集上的大量实验验证了Graph-GRPO的有效性：仅用50步去噪，该方法在平面图和树图数据集上分别达到95.0%和97.5%的有效-唯一-新颖性评分；在分子优化任务中，其性能优于基于图、基于片段的强化学习方法及经典遗传算法，达到当前最优水平。

Latent Poincaré Shaping for Agentic Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Hanchen Xia, Baoyou Chen, Zelin Zang, Yutang Ge, Guojiang Zhao, Siyu Zhu
First: 2026-02-10T03:35:52+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-11T03:30:29+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We propose LaPha, a method for training AlphaZero-like LLM agents in a Poincaré latent space. Under LaPha, the search process can be visualized as a tree rooted at the prompt and growing outward from the origin toward the boundary of the Poincaré ball, where negative curvature provides exponentially increasing capacity with radius. Using hyperbolic geodesic distance to rule-verified correctness, we define a node potential and assign dense process rewards by potential differences. We further attach a lightweight value head on the same shared latent space, enabling self-guided test-time scaling with almost no additional overhead. On MATH-500, LaPha improves Qwen2.5-Math-1.5B from 66.0% to 88.2%. With value-head-guided search, LaPha-1.5B reaches 56.7% accuracy on AIME'24, and LaPha-7B further achieves 60.0% on AIME'24 and 53.3% on AIME'25.
中文标题/摘要
标题：面向智能体强化学习的潜在庞加莱塑形方法
我们提出LaPha方法，用于在庞加莱潜在空间中训练类AlphaZero的大型语言模型智能体。该方法将搜索过程可视化为以提示为根、从原点向庞加莱球边界生长的树结构，其负曲率特性使模型容量随半径呈指数增长。通过双曲测地线距离与规则验证正确性的结合，我们定义了节点势能函数，并依据势能差分配密集过程奖励。我们在共享潜在空间上附加轻量级价值头，实现几乎零额外开销的自引导测试时扩展。在MATH-500基准测试中，LaPha将Qwen2.5-Math-1.5B模型准确率从66.0%提升至88.2%。通过价值头引导搜索，LaPha-1.5B在AIME'24达到56.7%准确率，LaPha-7B进一步在AIME'24和AIME'25分别取得60.0%和53.3%的准确率。
Summary / 总结
The paper introduces LaPha, a method motivated by the need to enhance the reasoning capabilities of AlphaZero-like large language model agents by training them in a Poincaré latent space, which leverages hyperbolic geometry to provide exponentially increasing representational capacity. The method visualizes the search process as a tree growing in this space, using hyperbolic geodesic distance to measure correctness and define node potentials for dense process rewards, and incorporates a lightweight value head on the shared latent space to enable efficient self-guided scaling during testing. Utility Function is All You Need: LLM-based Congestion Control
Authors: Neta Rozen-Schiff, Liron Schiff, Stefan Schmid
First: 2026-03-11T03:11:36+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-11T03:11:36+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Congestion is a critical and challenging problem in communication networks. Congestion control protocols allow network applications to tune their sending rate in a way that optimizes their performance and the network utilization. In the common distributed setting, the applications cannot collaborate with each other directly but instead obtain similar estimations about the state of the network using latency and loss measurements. These measurements can be fed into analytical functions, referred to by utility functions, whose gradients help each and all distributed senders to converge to a desired state. The above process becomes extremely complicated when each application has different optimization goals and requirements. Crafting these utilization functions has been a research subject for over a decade, with small incremental changes requiring rigorous mathematical analysis as well as real-world experiments. In this work, we present GenCC, a framework leveraging the code generation capabilities of large language models (LLMs) coupled with realistic network testbed, to design congestion control utility functions. Using GenCC, we analyze the impact of different guidance strategies on the performance of the generated protocols, considering application-specific requirements and network capacity. Our results show that LLMs, guided by either a generative code evolution strategy or mathematical chain-of-thought (CoT), can obtain close to optimal results, improving state-of-the-art congestion control protocols by 37%-142%, depending on the scenario.
中文标题/摘要
标题：效用函数即一切：基于大语言模型的拥塞控制
拥塞是通信网络中一个关键且具有挑战性的问题。拥塞控制协议使网络应用能够调整其发送速率，以优化自身性能和网络利用率。在常见的分布式环境中，应用之间无法直接协作，而是通过延迟和丢包测量获得对网络状态的相似估计。这些测量值可输入到被称为效用函数的解析函数中，其梯度帮助每个分布式发送方共同收敛到期望状态。当每个应用具有不同的优化目标和需求时，上述过程变得极为复杂。设计这些效用函数已成为十多年的研究课题，即使是微小的增量改进也需要严格的数学分析和实际实验。本研究提出GenCC框架，利用大语言模型的代码生成能力结合真实网络测试平台，设计拥塞控制效用函数。通过GenCC，我们分析了不同引导策略对生成协议性能的影响，并考虑了应用特定需求和网络容量。结果表明，在生成式代码进化策略或数学思维链引导下，大语言模型可获得接近最优的结果，将最先进的拥塞控制协议性能提升37%-142%，具体取决于场景。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the complexity of designing congestion control utility functions for diverse application requirements, this paper introduces GenCC, a framework that leverages large language models (LLMs) to generate these functions through code generation, guided by strategies like generative code evolution or mathematical chain-of-thought. The method integrates LLMs with a realistic network testbed to tailor protocols to specific needs and network conditions. Experimental results demonstrate that LLM-generated protocols achieve close-to-optimal performance, improving state-of-the-art congestion control by 37% to 142% across various scenarios.
针对不同应用需求下拥塞控制效用函数设计复杂的问题，本文提出了GenCC框架，利用大型语言模型（LLMs）的代码生成能力，通过生成式代码进化或数学思维链等引导策略来生成这些函数。该方法将LLMs与真实网络测试平台结合，以根据特定需求和网络条件定制协议。实验结果表明，LLM生成的协议实现了接近最优的性能，在不同场景下将最先进的拥塞控制协议提升了37%至142%。
PlayWorld: Learning Robot World Models from Autonomous Play
Authors: Tenny Yin, Zhiting Mei, Zhonghe Zheng, Miyu Yamane, David Wang, Jade Sceats, Samuel M. Bateman, Lihan Zha, Apurva Badithela, Ola Shorinwa, Anirudha Majumdar
First: 2026-03-09T23:58:07+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-11T01:39:15+00:00
Comments: https://robot-playworld.github.io/
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Project1
Abstract
Action-conditioned video models offer a promising path to building general-purpose robot simulators that can improve directly from data. Yet, despite training on large-scale robot datasets, current state-of-the-art video models still struggle to predict physically consistent robot-object interactions that are crucial in robotic manipulation. To close this gap, we present PlayWorld, a simple, scalable, and fully autonomous pipeline for training high-fidelity video world simulators from interaction experience. In contrast to prior approaches that rely on success-biased human demonstrations, PlayWorld is the first system capable of learning entirely from unsupervised robot self-play, enabling naturally scalable data collection while capturing complex, long-tailed physical interactions essential for modeling realistic object dynamics. Experiments across diverse manipulation tasks show that PlayWorld generates high-quality, physically consistent predictions for contact-rich interactions that are not captured by world models trained on human-collected data. We further demonstrate the versatility of PlayWorld in enabling fine-grained failure prediction and policy evaluation, with up to 40% improvements over human-collected data. Finally, we demonstrate how PlayWorld enables reinforcement learning in the world model, improving policy performance by 65% in success rates when deployed in the real world.
中文标题/摘要
标题：PlayWorld：通过自主游戏学习机器人世界模型
动作条件视频模型为构建能直接从数据中改进的通用机器人模拟器提供了可行路径。然而，尽管基于大规模机器人数据集进行训练，当前最先进的视频模型仍难以预测对机器人操作至关重要的物理一致性机器人-物体交互。为弥补这一差距，我们提出PlayWorld——一个简单、可扩展且完全自主的流程，用于从交互经验中训练高保真视频世界模拟器。与以往依赖偏向成功的人类演示方法不同，PlayWorld是首个能够完全从无监督机器人自主游戏中学习的系统，在捕捉复杂长尾物理交互（对建模真实物体动力学至关重要）的同时，实现了自然可扩展的数据收集。跨多种操作任务的实验表明，PlayWorld能对密集接触交互生成高质量、物理一致的预测，这是基于人类收集数据训练的世界模型所无法实现的。我们进一步展示了PlayWorld在细粒度故障预测与策略评估方面的通用性，相比人类收集数据最高可提升40%的性能。最后，我们演示了PlayWorld如何支持在世界模型中进行强化学习，在真实世界部署时将策略成功率提升了65%。
Summary / 总结
The motivation behind PlayWorld is to address the limitations of current action-conditioned video models in predicting physically consistent robot-object interactions, which are crucial for robotic manipulation but often poorly captured by models trained on success-biased human demonstrations. The method involves a simple, scalable, and fully autonomous pipeline that learns high-fidelity video world simulators from unsupervised robot self-play, enabling data collection that naturally scales and captures complex, long-tailed physical interactions. Experimental results across diverse manipulation tasks show that PlayWorld generates high-quality, physically consistent predictions for contact-rich interactions, outperforming models trained on human-collected data by up to 40% in fine-grained failure prediction and policy evaluation, and it enables reinforcement learning in the world model, improving real-world policy success rates by 65%.
PlayWorld的动机是解决当前基于动作的视频模型在预测物理一致的机器人-物体交互方面的局限性，这对于机器人操作至关重要，但基于人类演示训练的模型往往难以捕捉。该方法采用了一个简单、可扩展且完全自主的流程，通过无监督的机器人自主游戏学习高保真视频世界模拟器，实现了自然可扩展的数据收集，并能捕捉复杂的长尾物理交互。实验结果表明，在多种操作任务中，PlayWorld能生成高质量的、物理一致的接触丰富交互预测，在细粒度故障预测和策略评估上比基于人类收集数据训练的模型提升高达40%，并且支持在世界模型中进行强化学习，将真实世界中的策略成功率提高了65%。
PvP: Data-Efficient Humanoid Robot Learning with Proprioceptive-Privileged Contrastive Representations
Authors: Mingqi Yuan, Tao Yu, Haolin Song, Bo Li, Xin Jin, Hua Chen, Wenjun Zeng
Venue: CVPR
First: 2025-12-15T08:50:20+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-11T01:31:17+00:00
Comments: 15 pages, 17 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Achieving efficient and robust whole-body control (WBC) is essential for enabling humanoid robots to perform complex tasks in dynamic environments. Despite the success of reinforcement learning (RL) in this domain, its sample inefficiency remains a significant challenge due to the intricate dynamics and partial observability of humanoid robots. To address this limitation, we propose PvP, a Proprioceptive-Privileged contrastive learning framework that leverages the intrinsic complementarity between proprioceptive and privileged states. PvP learns compact and task-relevant latent representations without requiring hand-crafted data augmentations, enabling faster and more stable policy learning. To support systematic evaluation, we develop SRL4Humanoid, the first unified and modular framework that provides high-quality implementations of representative state representation learning (SRL) methods for humanoid robot learning. Extensive experiments on the LimX Oli robot across velocity tracking and motion imitation tasks demonstrate that PvP significantly improves sample efficiency and final performance compared to baseline SRL methods. Our study further provides practical insights into integrating SRL with RL for humanoid WBC, offering valuable guidance for data-efficient humanoid robot learning.
中文标题/摘要
标题：PvP：基于本体感知-特权对比表征的数据高效人形机器人学习
实现高效稳健的全身控制对于人形机器人在动态环境中执行复杂任务至关重要。尽管强化学习在该领域已取得成果，但由于人形机器人复杂的动力学特性和部分可观测性，其样本效率低仍是重大挑战。为突破此限制，我们提出PvP——一种利用本体感知状态与特权状态内在互补性的对比学习框架。该框架无需人工设计数据增强即可学习紧凑且任务相关的潜在表征，从而实现更快速稳定的策略学习。为支持系统化评估，我们开发了首个面向人形机器人学习的统一模块化框架SRL4Humanoid，其高质量实现了代表性状态表征学习方法。在LimX Oli机器人上进行的速度跟踪与运动模仿实验表明，相较于基线SRL方法，PvP显著提升了样本效率与最终性能。本研究进一步为SRL与RL在人形机器人全身控制中的融合提供了实践洞见，为数据高效的人形机器人学习提供了重要指导。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the sample inefficiency of reinforcement learning for humanoid whole-body control by proposing PvP, a contrastive learning framework that leverages the complementarity between proprioceptive and privileged states to learn compact, task-relevant latent representations without hand-crafted augmentations. The method is evaluated using a newly developed unified framework, SRL4Humanoid, and experiments on a LimX Oli robot show that PvP significantly improves sample efficiency and final performance in velocity tracking and motion imitation tasks compared to baseline state representation learning methods.
该论文针对人形机器人全身控制中强化学习样本效率低的问题，提出了PvP对比学习框架，利用本体感知与特权状态之间的互补性来学习紧凑且与任务相关的潜在表示，无需手工数据增强。该方法通过新开发的统一框架SRL4Humanoid进行评估，在LimX Oli机器人上的实验表明，在速度跟踪和运动模仿任务中，PvP相比基线状态表示学习方法显著提高了样本效率和最终性能。
Quantum entanglement provides a competitive advantage in adversarial games
Authors: Peiyong Wang, Kieran Hymas, James Quach
First: 2026-03-11T00:15:56+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-11T00:15:56+00:00
Comments: 22 pages, 5 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Whether uniquely quantum resources confer advantages in fully classical, competitive environments remains an open question. Competitive zero-sum reinforcement learning is particularly challenging, as success requires modelling dynamic interactions between opposing agents rather than static state-action mappings. Here, we conduct a controlled study isolating the role of quantum entanglement in a quantum-classical hybrid agent trained on Pong, a competitive Markov game. An 8-qubit parameterised quantum circuit serves as a feature extractor within a proximal policy optimisation framework, allowing direct comparison between separable circuits and architectures incorporating fixed (CZ) or trainable (IsingZZ) entangling gates. Entangled circuits consistently outperform separable counterparts with comparable parameter counts and, in low-capacity regimes, match or exceed classical multilayer perceptron baselines. Representation similarity analysis further shows that entangled circuits learn structurally distinct features, consistent with improved modelling of interacting state variables. These findings establish entanglement as a function resource for representation learning in competitive reinforcement learning.
中文标题/摘要
标题：量子纠缠在对抗性游戏中提供竞争优势
量子资源能否在完全经典的竞争环境中提供优势仍是一个开放性问题。竞争性零和强化学习尤其具有挑战性，因为成功需要建模对抗智能体之间的动态交互，而非静态的状态-动作映射。本研究通过控制实验，在训练于对抗性马尔可夫游戏《Pong》的量子-经典混合智能体中，分离出量子纠缠的作用。一个8量子比特参数化量子电路在近端策略优化框架中作为特征提取器，使可分离电路与采用固定纠缠门（CZ）或可训练纠缠门（IsingZZ）的架构能够直接比较。在参数量相当的情况下，纠缠电路始终优于可分离电路；在低容量机制中，其性能达到或超越经典多层感知机基线。表征相似性分析进一步表明，纠缠电路能学习结构独特的特征，这与交互状态变量建模能力的提升相一致。这些发现确立了纠缠作为竞争性强化学习中表征学习的功能性资源。

This study investigates whether quantum entanglement offers a competitive edge in classical adversarial environments, specifically in zero-sum reinforcement learning where agents must dynamically model opponent interactions. The method employs a hybrid quantum-classical agent for the game Pong, using an 8-qubit parameterized quantum circuit as a feature extractor within a proximal policy optimization framework, comparing separable circuits against those with fixed or trainable entangling gates. Experimental results show that entangled circuits consistently outperform separable ones with similar parameter counts and, in low-capacity settings, match or surpass classical multilayer perceptron baselines, with representation analysis indicating they learn structurally distinct features that better model interacting state variables.
本研究探讨了量子纠缠是否能在经典对抗环境中提供竞争优势，特别是在需要动态建模对手交互的零和强化学习场景中。方法上，研究为游戏《乒乓》设计了一个混合量子-经典智能体，使用一个8量子比特的参数化量子电路作为特征提取器，并集成近端策略优化框架，比较了可分离电路与具有固定或可训练纠缠门的电路架构。实验结果表明，纠缠电路在参数量相近时持续优于可分离电路，且在低容量状态下达到或超越了经典多层感知机基准，表征相似性分析进一步揭示纠缠电路学习了结构独特的特征，从而更好地建模了交互状态变量。
From Prior to Pro: Efficient Skill Mastery via Distribution Contractive RL Finetuning
Authors: Zhanyi Sun, Shuran Song
First: 2026-03-10T22:49:46+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-10T22:49:46+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Project1
Abstract
We introduce Distribution Contractive Reinforcement Learning (DICE-RL), a framework that uses reinforcement learning (RL) as a "distribution contraction" operator to refine pretrained generative robot policies. DICE-RL turns a pretrained behavior prior into a high-performing "pro" policy by amplifying high-success behaviors from online feedback. We pretrain a diffusion- or flow-based policy for broad behavioral coverage, then finetune it with a stable, sample-efficient residual off-policy RL framework that combines selective behavior regularization with value-guided action selection. Extensive experiments and analyses show that DICE-RL reliably improves performance with strong stability and sample efficiency. It enables mastery of complex long-horizon manipulation skills directly from high-dimensional pixel inputs, both in simulation and on a real robot. Project website: https://zhanyisun.github.io/dice.rl.2026/.
中文标题/摘要
标题：从先验到专业：通过分布收缩强化学习微调实现高效技能掌握
我们提出了分布收缩强化学习（DICE-RL）框架，该框架利用强化学习（RL）作为“分布收缩”算子，以优化预训练的生成式机器人策略。DICE-RL通过在线反馈放大高成功率行为，将预训练的行为先验转化为高性能的“专业”策略。我们首先预训练一个基于扩散或流的策略以实现广泛的行为覆盖，随后通过一个稳定、样本高效的残差离策略RL框架进行微调，该框架结合了选择性行为正则化与价值引导的动作选择。大量实验与分析表明，DICE-RL在保持强稳定性和样本效率的同时，能可靠提升性能。该框架支持在仿真和真实机器人上，直接从高维像素输入中掌握复杂的长时程操作技能。项目网站：https://zhanyisun.github.io/dice.rl.2026/。

The method employs reinforcement learning as a distribution contraction operator, starting with a diffusion- or flow-based policy pretrained for broad coverage and finetuning it via a stable, sample-efficient residual off-policy RL framework that combines selective behavior regularization with value-guided action selection. Experimental results demonstrate that DICE-RL reliably improves performance with strong stability and sample efficiency, enabling mastery of complex long-horizon manipulation skills directly from high-dimensional pixel inputs in both simulation and real-robot settings.

Synthesizing Interpretable Control Policies through Large Language Model Guided Search
Authors: Carlo Bosio, Mark W. Mueller
Venue: Published at ACC 2025
First: 2024-10-07T18:12:20+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-10T22:31:58+00:00
Comments: 8 pages, 7 figures, conference paper
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
The combination of Large Language Models (LLMs), systematic evaluation, and evolutionary algorithms has enabled breakthroughs in combinatorial optimization and scientific discovery. We propose to extend this powerful combination to the control of dynamical systems, generating interpretable control policies capable of complex behaviors. With our novel method, we represent control policies as programs in standard languages like Python. We evaluate candidate controllers in simulation and evolve them using a pre-trained LLM. Unlike conventional learning-based control techniques, which rely on black-box neural networks to encode control policies, our approach enhances transparency and interpretability. We still take advantage of the power of large AI models, but only at the policy design phase, ensuring that all system components remain interpretable and easily verifiable at runtime. Additionally, the use of standard programming languages makes it straightforward for humans to finetune or adapt the controllers based on their expertise and intuition. We illustrate our method through its application to the synthesis of an interpretable control policy for the \textit{pendulum swing-up} and the \textit{ball in cup} tasks. We make the code available at https://github.com/muellerlab/synthesizing_interpretable_control_policies.git.
中文标题/摘要
标题：通过大语言模型引导搜索合成可解释控制策略
大语言模型（LLMs）、系统化评估与进化算法的结合，已在组合优化和科学发现领域取得突破。我们提出将这一强大组合扩展到动态系统控制领域，生成具备复杂行为能力的可解释控制策略。通过创新方法，我们将控制策略表示为Python等标准语言的程序代码，在仿真环境中评估候选控制器，并利用预训练大语言模型进行演化。与传统基于学习的控制技术依赖黑盒神经网络编码策略不同，我们的方法提升了透明度和可解释性。我们仍借助大型AI模型的能力，但仅将其用于策略设计阶段，确保所有系统组件在运行时保持可解释且易于验证。此外，采用标准编程语言使人类能基于专业知识和直觉直接微调或适配控制器。我们通过为“钟摆起摆”和“球入杯”任务合成可解释控制策略的应用案例，展示了该方法。代码发布于https://github.com/muellerlab/synthesizing_interpretable_control_policies.git。

This paper is motivated by the need for interpretable control policies in dynamical systems, moving away from opaque neural network-based controllers. The method involves representing control policies as programs in standard languages like Python, evaluating them in simulation, and evolving them using a pre-trained large language model to guide the search process. Experimental results demonstrate the approach's effectiveness in synthesizing interpretable controllers for tasks such as pendulum swing-up and ball in cup, achieving complex behaviors while maintaining transparency and allowing human-in-the-loop fine-tuning.
本文旨在为动态系统设计可解释的控制策略，以替代基于黑盒神经网络的传统方法。该方法将控制策略表示为Python等标准语言的程序，通过仿真评估候选控制器，并利用预训练的大语言模型引导进化搜索。实验结果表明，该方法成功合成了适用于摆锤起摆和球入杯任务的可解释控制器，在实现复杂行为的同时保持了策略的透明性，并支持基于人类专家知识的微调与适配。
SiMPO: Measure Matching for Online Diffusion Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Haitong Ma, Chenxiao Gao, Tianyi Chen, Na Li, Bo Dai
First: 2026-03-10T22:01:13+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-10T22:01:13+00:00
Comments: 22 pages, 6 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
A commonly used family of RL algorithms for diffusion policies conducts softmax reweighting over the behavior policy, which usually induces an over-greedy policy and fails to leverage feedback from negative samples. In this work, we introduce Signed Measure Policy Optimization (SiMPO), a simple and unified framework that generalizes reweighting scheme in diffusion RL with general monotonic functions. SiMPO revisits diffusion RL via a two-stage measure matching lens. First, we construct a virtual target policy by $f$-divergence regularized policy optimization, where we can relax the non-negativity constraint to allow for a signed target measure. Second, we use this signed measure to guide diffusion or flow models through reweighted matching. This formulation offers two key advantages: a) it generalizes to arbitrary monotonically increasing weighting functions; and b) it provides a principled justification and practical guidance for negative reweighting. Furthermore, we provide geometric interpretations to illustrate how negative reweighting actively repels the policy from suboptimal actions. Extensive empirical evaluations demonstrate that SiMPO achieves superior performance by leveraging these flexible weighting schemes, and we provide practical guidelines for selecting reweighting methods tailored to the reward landscape.
中文标题/摘要
标题：SiMPO：在线扩散强化学习的测度匹配方法
扩散策略中常用的强化学习算法族通过对行为策略进行softmax重加权，这通常会导致策略过度贪婪且无法利用负样本反馈。本文提出符号测度策略优化（SiMPO），这是一个简洁统一的框架，通过单调函数推广了扩散强化学习中的重加权方案。SiMPO通过两阶段测度匹配视角重新审视扩散强化学习：首先，通过$f$-散度正则化的策略优化构建虚拟目标策略，其中放宽非负约束以允许符号测度；其次，利用该符号测度通过重加权匹配指导扩散或流模型。该框架具有两大优势：a)可推广至任意单调递增加权函数；b)为负向重加权提供理论依据与实践指导。此外，我们通过几何解释说明负向重加权如何主动使策略远离次优动作。大量实验表明，SiMPO通过灵活加权方案实现了优越性能，并针对奖励函数形态提供了定制化重加权方法的选择指南。
Summary / 总结
The paper introduces SiMPO, a framework addressing limitations in diffusion reinforcement learning where standard softmax reweighting leads to over-greedy policies and ignores negative feedback. The method generalizes reweighting via a two-stage measure matching approach: first constructing a virtual target policy using f-divergence regularization that allows signed measures, then guiding diffusion models through reweighted matching. Experimental results show SiMPO achieves superior performance by flexibly leveraging both positive and negative samples, with geometric interpretations explaining how negative reweighting repels suboptimal actions, and it provides practical guidelines for selecting reweighting schemes based on reward landscapes.
本文提出了SiMPO框架，旨在解决扩散强化学习中标准softmax重加权导致策略过于贪婪且忽略负反馈的问题。该方法通过两阶段度量匹配泛化重加权：首先使用f-散度正则化构建允许带符号度量的虚拟目标策略，然后通过重加权匹配指导扩散模型。实验结果表明，SiMPO通过灵活利用正负样本实现了更优性能，其几何解释阐明了负重加权如何主动排斥次优动作，并为基于奖励景观选择重加权方案提供了实用指导。
Long Chain-of-Thought Compression via Fine-Grained Group Policy Optimization
Authors: Xinchen Han, Hossam Afifi, Michel Marot, Xilu Wang, Lu Yin
Venue: ICASSP
First: 2026-02-10T18:15:58+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-10T20:59:28+00:00
Comments: IEEE International Conference on Acoustics, Speech, and Signal Processing (ICASSP), 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Large Language Models (LLMs) often generate unnecessarily verbose Chain-of-Thought (CoT) reasoning that increases computational costs and latency without proportional performance gains. In this paper, we propose Fine-grained Group policy Optimization (FGO), a Reinforcement Learning (RL) algorithm that refines group responses by subdividing them and assigning appropriate weights based on length and entropy, thereby enabling effective CoT compression. Meanwhile, as an enhanced variant of Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO), FGO successfully addresses two major limitations of the GRPO: inefficient data utilization and entropy collapse. We evaluate FGO on multiple reasoning LLMs and benchmarks, including MATH500, AIME24, AMC23, and Minerva. Experimental results show that FGO achieves efficient CoT compression without degrading performance, and simultaneously resolves the key limitations of GRPO. Code: https://github.com/Mr-XcHan/FGO.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于细粒度分组策略优化的长链思维压缩方法
大语言模型（LLMs）生成的链式思维（CoT）推理常存在冗余冗长问题，导致计算成本与延迟增加却未带来相应性能提升。本文提出细粒度分组策略优化（FGO）算法，该强化学习方法通过细分组响应并依据长度与熵值分配权重，实现高效CoT压缩。作为分组相对策略优化（GRPO）的增强变体，FGO成功解决了GRPO的两大局限：数据利用效率低下与熵崩溃问题。我们在MATH500、AIME24、AMC23及Minerva等多个推理基准上评估FGO，实验表明该方法在保持性能的同时实现高效CoT压缩，并同步解决了GRPO的关键缺陷。代码：https://github.com/Mr-XcHan/FGO。

An Updated Assessment of Reinforcement Learning for Macro Placement
Authors: Chung-Kuan Cheng, Andrew B. Kahng, Sayak Kundu, Yucheng Wang, Zhiang Wang
First: 2023-02-21T21:26:28+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-10T20:18:33+00:00
Comments: There are total sixteen pages and two pages for the appendix. It includes six figures and eleven tables. This paper has been accepted and published in IEEE Transactions on CAD
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We provide an improved assessment of Google Brain's deep reinforcement learning approach to macro placement and its updated Circuit Training (CT) implementation in GitHub. A stronger simulated annealing (SA) baseline leverages the "go-with-the-winners" metaheuristic and a multi-threading implementation. We develop and release new public benchmarks in sub-10nm technology: LEF/DEF for Google's 7nm TSMC Ariane protobuf and scaled variants, as well as testcases implemented in the open-source ASAP7 7nm research enablement. We evaluate from-scratch training and fine-tuning results for the latest "AlphaChip" release of Circuit Training, alongside multiple alternative macro placers. We also study the recently-published pre-training guidance in. A commercial place-and-route tool is used to provide "true reward" post-route power, performance and area metrics. All data, evaluation flows and related scripts are publicly available in the MacroPlacement GitHub repository. Our study affords insights into reproducibility and reporting in the research literature, and points out still-missing confirmations (e.g., of CT's scalability and pre-training methodology) that remain open questions for the research community.

本文对Google Brain采用深度强化学习进行宏单元布局的方法及其在GitHub上更新的Circuit Training（CT）实现进行了改进评估。我们构建了更强的模拟退火（SA）基线，采用“胜者导向”元启发式算法和多线程实现。针对10纳米以下工艺，我们开发并发布了新的公开基准：包括Google 7纳米TSMC Ariane protobuf的LEF/DEF文件及其缩放变体，以及基于开源ASAP7 7纳米研究平台实现的测试用例。我们评估了最新发布的Circuit Training“AlphaChip”版本从零开始的训练与微调结果，并与多种替代宏单元布局工具进行对比。同时研究了近期发布的预训练指导方法。采用商用布局布线工具获取布线后“真实奖励”的功耗、性能与面积指标。所有数据、评估流程及相关脚本均在MacroPlacement GitHub仓库公开。本研究为文献中的可复现性与报告规范提供了见解，并指出仍需研究界验证的开放问题（如CT的可扩展性及预训练方法）。

This paper provides an updated evaluation of Google Brain's deep reinforcement learning (RL) approach for macro placement, specifically its Circuit Training (CT) implementation, motivated by the need for a stronger comparative analysis and reproducible benchmarks in advanced technology nodes. Actor-Accelerated Policy Dual Averaging for Reinforcement Learning in Continuous Action Spaces
Authors: Ji Gao, Caleb Ju, Guanghui Lan, Zhaohui Tong
First: 2026-03-10T20:05:18+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-10T20:05:18+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Policy Dual Averaging (PDA) offers a principled Policy Mirror Descent (PMD) framework that more naturally admits value function approximation than standard PMD, enabling the use of approximate advantage (or Q-) functions while retaining strong convergence guarantees. However, applying PDA in continuous state and action spaces remains computationally challenging, since action selection involves solving an optimization sub-problem at each decision step. In this paper, we propose \textit{actor-accelerated PDA}, which uses a learned policy network to approximate the solution of the optimization sub-problems, yielding faster runtimes while maintaining convergence guarantees. We provide a theoretical analysis that quantifies how actor approximation error impacts the convergence of PDA under suitable assumptions. We then evaluate its performance on several benchmarks in robotics, control, and operations research problems. Actor-accelerated PDA achieves superior performance compared to popular on-policy baselines such as Proximal Policy Optimization (PPO). Overall, our results bridge the gap between the theoretical advantages of PDA and its practical deployment in continuous-action problems with function approximation.
中文标题/摘要
标题：连续动作空间中强化学习的行动者加速策略对偶平均法
策略对偶平均（PDA）提供了一个原则性的策略镜像下降（PMD）框架，相比标准PMD能更自然地引入价值函数近似，允许使用近似优势（或Q）函数，同时保持强收敛保证。然而，在连续状态和动作空间中应用PDA仍存在计算挑战，因为动作选择需要在每个决策步骤求解优化子问题。本文提出\textit{行动者加速PDA}，通过学习的策略网络来近似优化子问题的解，在保持收敛保证的同时显著提升运行效率。我们提供了理论分析，量化了在适当假设下行动者近似误差对PDA收敛性的影响，并在机器人、控制与运筹学领域的多个基准问题上评估其性能。与近端策略优化（PPO）等主流同策略基线方法相比，行动者加速PDA展现出更优性能。总体而言，本研究弥合了PDA的理论优势与其在函数近似的连续动作问题中实际应用之间的鸿沟。

The method introduces actor-accelerated PDA, which uses a learned policy network to approximate the solutions to these sub-problems, thereby accelerating runtime while preserving theoretical convergence guarantees, with analysis linking actor approximation error to convergence. Experimental results on robotics, control, and operations research benchmarks show that this approach outperforms on-policy baselines like Proximal Policy Optimization (PPO), bridging the gap between PDA's theoretical benefits and practical deployment.

Logarithmic Regret for Online KL-Regularized Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Heyang Zhao, Chenlu Ye, Wei Xiong, Quanquan Gu, Tong Zhang
First: 2025-02-11T11:11:05+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-10T19:02:02+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Recent advances in Reinforcement Learning from Human Feedback (RLHF) have shown that KL-regularization plays a pivotal role in improving the efficiency of RL fine-tuning for large language models (LLMs). Despite its empirical advantage, the theoretical difference between KL-regularized RL and standard RL remains largely under-explored. While there is a recent line of work on the theoretical analysis of KL-regularized objective in decision making \citep{xiong2024iterative, xie2024exploratory,zhao2024sharp}, these analyses either reduce to the traditional RL setting or rely on strong coverage assumptions. In this paper, we propose an optimism-based KL-regularized online contextual bandit algorithm, and provide a novel analysis of its regret. By carefully leveraging the benign optimization landscape induced by the KL-regularization and the optimistic reward estimation, our algorithm achieves an $\mathcal{O}\big(η\log (N_{\mathcal R} T)\cdot d_{\mathcal R}\big)$ logarithmic regret bound, where $η, N_{\mathcal R},T,d_{\mathcal R}$ denote the KL-regularization parameter, the cardinality of the reward function class, number of rounds, and the complexity of the reward function class. Furthermore, we extend our algorithm and analysis to reinforcement learning by developing a novel decomposition over transition steps and also obtain a similar logarithmic regret bound.
中文标题/摘要
标题：在线KL正则化强化学习的对数遗憾界
人类反馈强化学习（RLHF）的最新进展表明，KL正则化在提升大语言模型（LLM）强化学习微调效率方面具有关键作用。尽管存在实证优势，KL正则化强化学习与标准强化学习的理论差异仍未得到充分探索。近期虽有研究对决策中KL正则化目标进行理论分析（\citep{xiong2024iterative, xie2024exploratory,zhao2024sharp}），但这些分析要么退化为传统强化学习设定，要么依赖强覆盖假设。本文提出一种基于乐观策略的KL正则化在线上下文赌博算法，并对其遗憾界进行了创新性分析。通过巧妙利用KL正则化诱导的良性优化景观与乐观奖励估计，我们的算法实现了$\mathcal{O}\big(η\log (N_{\mathcal R} T)\cdot d_{\mathcal R}\big)$的对数遗憾界，其中$η, N_{\mathcal R},T,d_{\mathcal R}$分别表示KL正则化参数、奖励函数类基数、回合数和奖励函数类复杂度。进一步，我们通过设计新颖的状态转移步分解方法，将算法与分析拓展至强化学习场景，并获得了类似的对数遗憾界。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the empirical success of KL-regularization in Reinforcement Learning from Human Feedback (RLHF) and the lack of theoretical understanding under weak assumptions, this paper proposes an optimism-based online contextual bandit algorithm for KL-regularized learning. The method carefully leverages the favorable optimization landscape created by KL regularization and uses optimistic reward estimation to guide exploration. The main experimental result is a theoretical guarantee: the algorithm achieves a logarithmic regret bound of O(η log(N_R T) · d_R), which is later extended to a similar bound in the full reinforcement learning setting through a novel decomposition over transition steps.
本文的动机源于KL正则化在人类反馈强化学习（RLHF）中的实证成功及其在弱假设下理论理解的缺乏，为此提出了一种基于乐观策略的在线上下文赌博算法用于KL正则化学习。该方法巧妙利用了KL正则化带来的良性优化格局，并采用乐观奖励估计来引导探索。主要理论结果是算法获得了O(η log(N_R T) · d_R)的对数遗憾界，随后通过一种针对状态转移步骤的新颖分解，该结果被扩展到完整的强化学习设定中，并获得了类似的对数遗憾界。
ReMix: Reinforcement routing for mixtures of LoRAs in LLM finetuning
Authors: Ruizhong Qiu, Hanqing Zeng, Yinglong Xia, Yiwen Meng, Ren Chen, Jiarui Feng, Dongqi Fu, Qifan Wang, Jiayi Liu, Jun Xiao, Xiangjun Fan, Benyu Zhang, Hong Li, Zhining Liu, Hyunsik Yoo, Zhichen Zeng, Tianxin Wei, Hanghang Tong
Venue: ICLR 2026
First: 2026-03-10T18:51:27+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-10T18:51:27+00:00
Comments: LLA @ ICLR 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Low-rank adapters (LoRAs) are a parameter-efficient finetuning technique that injects trainable low-rank matrices into pretrained models to adapt them to new tasks. Mixture-of-LoRAs models expand neural networks efficiently by routing each layer input to a small subset of specialized LoRAs of the layer. Existing Mixture-of-LoRAs routers assign a learned routing weight to each LoRA to enable end-to-end training of the router. Despite their empirical promise, we observe that the routing weights are typically extremely imbalanced across LoRAs in practice, where only one or two LoRAs often dominate the routing weights. This essentially limits the number of effective LoRAs and thus severely hinders the expressive power of existing Mixture-of-LoRAs models. In this work, we attribute this weakness to the nature of learnable routing weights and rethink the fundamental design of the router. To address this critical issue, we propose a new router designed that we call Reinforcement Routing for Mixture-of-LoRAs (ReMix). Our key idea is using non-learnable routing weights to ensure all active LoRAs to be equally effective, with no LoRA dominating the routing weights. However, our routers cannot be trained directly via gradient descent due to our non-learnable routing weights. Hence, we further propose an unbiased gradient estimator for the router by employing the reinforce leave-one-out (RLOO) technique, where we regard the supervision loss as the reward and the router as the policy in reinforcement learning. Our gradient estimator also enables to scale up training compute to boost the predictive performance of our ReMix. Extensive experiments demonstrate that our proposed ReMix significantly outperform state-of-the-art parameter-efficient finetuning methods under a comparable number of activated parameters.
中文标题/摘要
标题：ReMix：大语言模型微调中LoRA混合的强化路由方法
低秩适配器（LoRA）是一种参数高效的微调技术，通过向预训练模型注入可训练的低秩矩阵来适应新任务。混合LoRA模型通过将每层输入路由到该层少量专用LoRA子集，实现了神经网络的高效扩展。现有混合LoRA路由器为每个LoRA分配可学习的路由权重，以实现路由器的端到端训练。尽管经验表明其具有潜力，但我们观察到实际应用中路由权重在LoRA间通常极不均衡，往往仅有一两个LoRA主导路由权重。这实质上限制了有效LoRA的数量，从而严重制约了现有混合LoRA模型的表达能力。本研究将此缺陷归因于可学习路由权重的本质特性，并重新思考路由器的根本设计。为解决这一关键问题，我们提出了一种称为“混合LoRA强化路由”（ReMix）的新型路由器设计。核心思路是采用不可学习的路由权重，确保所有活跃LoRA具有同等效力，避免任何LoRA主导路由权重。然而，由于采用不可学习权重，我们的路由器无法直接通过梯度下降训练。为此，我们进一步提出基于强化学习留一法（RLOO）技术的无偏梯度估计器，将监督损失视为奖励、路由器视为强化学习中的策略。该梯度估计器还能扩展训练计算规模，以提升ReMix的预测性能。大量实验表明，在激活参数量相当的情况下，我们提出的ReMix显著优于当前最先进的参数高效微调方法。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the issue of imbalanced routing weights in existing Mixture-of-LoRAs models, where only a few LoRAs dominate, limiting expressive power. To solve this, the authors propose ReMix, a reinforcement routing method that uses non-learnable routing weights to ensure all active LoRAs are equally effective, and they introduce an unbiased gradient estimator via the reinforce leave-one-out technique to enable training. Experimental results show that ReMix outperforms state-of-the-art parameter-efficient finetuning methods under comparable activated parameters.
本文针对现有混合低秩适配器模型中路由权重严重不平衡、导致少数LoRA主导而限制表达能力的问题，提出了一种名为ReMix的强化路由方法。该方法采用不可学习的路由权重以确保所有活跃LoRA同等有效，并通过强化学习中的留一法策略梯度估计器实现训练。实验结果表明，在激活参数量相当的情况下，ReMix显著优于当前最先进的参数高效微调方法。
CLIPO: Contrastive Learning in Policy Optimization Generalizes RLVR
Authors: Sijia Cui, Pengyu Cheng, Jiajun Song, Yongbo Gai, Guojun Zhang, Zhechao Yu, Jianhe Lin, Xiaoxi Jiang, Guanjun Jiang
First: 2026-03-10T17:59:54+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-10T17:59:54+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) has significantly advanced the reasoning capacity of Large Language Models (LLMs). However, RLVR solely relies on final answers as outcome rewards, neglecting the correctness of intermediate reasoning steps. Training on these process-wrong but outcome-correct rollouts can lead to hallucination and answer-copying, severely undermining the model's generalization and robustness. To address this, we incorporate a Contrastive Learning mechanism into the Policy Optimization (CLIPO) to generalize the RLVR process. By optimizing a contrastive loss over successful rollouts, CLIPO steers the LLM to capture the invariant structure shared across correct reasoning paths. This provides a more robust cross-trajectory regularization than the original single-path supervision in RLVR, effectively mitigating step-level reasoning inconsistencies and suppressing hallucinatory artifacts. In experiments, CLIPO consistently improves multiple RLVR baselines across diverse reasoning benchmarks, demonstrating uniform improvements in generalization and robustness for policy optimization of LLMs. Our code and training recipes are available at https://github.com/Qwen-Applications/CLIPO.
中文标题/摘要
标题：CLIPO：策略优化中的对比学习泛化RLVR方法
可验证奖励强化学习（RLVR）显著提升了大型语言模型的推理能力，但其仅依赖最终答案作为结果奖励，忽略了中间推理步骤的正确性。对过程错误但结果正确的推演轨迹进行训练可能导致幻觉和答案抄袭，严重损害模型的泛化性与鲁棒性。为此，我们在策略优化中引入对比学习机制（CLIPO）以泛化RLVR过程。通过对成功推演轨迹优化对比损失，CLIPO引导大语言模型捕捉正确推理路径间共享的不变结构。相比RLVR原有的单路径监督，该方法提供了更鲁棒的跨轨迹正则化，有效缓解步骤级推理不一致性并抑制幻觉伪影。实验表明，CLIPO在多样化推理基准测试中持续提升多个RLVR基线模型，在大语言模型策略优化的泛化性与鲁棒性方面均展现出一致改进。代码与训练方案已开源：https://github.com/Qwen-Applications/CLIPO。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses a key limitation in Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) for Large Language Models, where reliance solely on final answer rewards neglects incorrect intermediate reasoning steps, leading to hallucinations and poor generalization. The proposed method, CLIPO, integrates a Contrastive Learning mechanism into Policy Optimization to generalize RLVR by optimizing a contrastive loss over successful rollouts, enabling the model to capture invariant structures across correct reasoning paths for better regularization. Experimental results show that CLIPO consistently enhances multiple RLVR baselines across diverse reasoning benchmarks, improving generalization and robustness in policy optimization for LLMs.
本文针对大型语言模型中可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR）的一个关键局限，即仅依赖最终答案奖励而忽略错误的中间推理步骤，导致幻觉和泛化能力差的问题。提出的方法CLIPO将对比学习机制融入策略优化中，通过优化成功轨迹上的对比损失来泛化RLVR，使模型能够捕捉正确推理路径间的共享不变结构，实现更好的正则化。实验结果表明，CLIPO在多种推理基准测试中持续提升了多个RLVR基线，增强了LLM策略优化的泛化能力和鲁棒性。
ARLBench: Flexible and Efficient Benchmarking for Hyperparameter Optimization in Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Jannis Becktepe, Julian Dierkes, Carolin Benjamins, Aditya Mohan, David Salinas, Raghu Rajan, Frank Hutter, Holger Hoos, Marius Lindauer, Theresa Eimer
Venue: Journal of Data-centric Machine Learning Research; 2026
First: 2024-09-27T15:22:28+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-10T17:58:13+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Hyperparameters are a critical factor in reliably training well-performing reinforcement learning (RL) agents. Unfortunately, developing and evaluating automated approaches for tuning such hyperparameters is both costly and time-consuming. As a result, such approaches are often only evaluated on a single domain or algorithm, making comparisons difficult and limiting insights into their generalizability. We propose ARLBench, a benchmark for hyperparameter optimization (HPO) in RL that allows comparisons of diverse HPO approaches while being highly efficient in evaluation. To enable research into HPO in RL, even in settings with low compute resources, we select a representative subset of HPO tasks spanning a variety of algorithm and environment combinations. This selection allows for generating a performance profile of an automated RL (AutoRL) method using only a fraction of the compute previously necessary, enabling a broader range of researchers to work on HPO in RL. With the extensive and large-scale dataset on hyperparameter landscapes that our selection is based on, ARLBench is an efficient, flexible, and future-oriented foundation for research on AutoRL. Both the benchmark and the dataset are available at https://github.com/automl/arlbench.
中文标题/摘要
标题：ARLBench：强化学习中超参数优化的灵活高效基准测试框架
超参数是可靠训练高性能强化学习智能体的关键因素。然而，开发和评估自动调参方法成本高昂且耗时，导致现有研究常局限于单一领域或算法，难以进行横向比较并制约了方法泛化性的深入探究。本文提出ARLBench——一个专为强化学习超参数优化设计的基准测试框架，能够在高效评估的同时支持多种优化方法的系统性比较。为降低计算资源门槛，我们选取了涵盖多类算法与环境组合的代表性任务子集，使研究者仅需传统方法所需计算量的一小部分即可生成自动化强化学习方法的性能图谱。基于我们构建的大规模超参数景观数据集，ARLBench为自动化强化学习研究提供了高效、灵活且具前瞻性的基础平台。基准框架与数据集已开源：https://github.com/automl/arlbench。
Summary / 总结
The motivation for ARLBench is to address the high computational cost and limited scope of evaluating hyperparameter optimization (HPO) methods in reinforcement learning (RL), which often restricts comparisons to single domains or algorithms.
