When Learning Rates Go Wrong: Early Structural Signals in PPO Actor-Critic
Authors: Alberto Fernández-Hernández, Cristian Pérez-Corral, Jose I. Mestre, Manuel F. Dolz, Jose Duato, Enrique S. Quintana-Ortí
First: 2026-03-10T17:46:31+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-10T17:46:31+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Deep Reinforcement Learning systems are highly sensitive to the learning rate (LR), and selecting stable and performant training runs often requires extensive hyperparameter search. In Proximal Policy Optimization (PPO) actor--critic methods, small LR values lead to slow convergence, whereas large LR values may induce instability or collapse. We analyse this phenomenon from the behavior of the hidden neurons in the network using the Overfitting-Underfitting Indicator (OUI), a metric that quantifies the balance of binary activation patterns over a fixed probe batch. We introduce an efficient batch-based formulation of OUI and derive a theoretical connection between LR and activation sign changes, clarifying how a correct evolution of the neuron's inner structure depends on the step size. Empirically, across three discrete-control environments and multiple seeds, we show that OUI measured at only 10\% of training already discriminates between LR regimes. We observe a consistent asymmetry: critic networks achieving highest return operate in an intermediate OUI band (avoiding saturation), whereas actor networks achieving highest return exhibit comparatively high OUI values. We then compare OUI-based screening rules against early return, clip-based, divergence-based, and flip-based criteria under matched recall over successful runs. In this setting, OUI provides the strongest early screening signal: OUI alone achieves the best precision at broader recall, while combining early return with OUI yields the highest precision in best-performing screening regimes, enabling aggressive pruning of unpromising runs without requiring full training.
中文标题/摘要
标题：学习率失效时：PPO演员-评论家方法中的早期结构信号
深度强化学习系统对学习率高度敏感，选择稳定高效的训练过程通常需要大量超参数搜索。在近端策略优化演员-评论家方法中，过小的学习率导致收敛缓慢，而过大的学习率可能引发不稳定或崩溃。我们通过网络的隐藏神经元行为分析这一现象，使用过拟合-欠拟合指示器——一种量化固定探测批次上二元激活模式平衡性的指标。我们提出了OUI的高效批次计算形式，并建立了学习率与激活符号变化的理论关联，阐明了神经元内部结构的正确演化如何依赖于步长。 在三个离散控制环境和多种随机种子的实证研究中，我们证明仅需训练过程10%时测量的OUI即可区分不同学习率机制。我们观察到一致的不对称性：获得最高回报的评论家网络运行于中等OUI区间（避免饱和），而获得最高回报的演员网络则表现出相对较高的OUI值。随后，我们在成功训练过程的匹配召回率下，将基于OUI的筛选规则与早期回报、裁剪机制、发散性和翻转性标准进行比较。在此设定下，OUI提供了最强的早期筛选信号：单独使用OUI可在更宽召回率范围内获得最佳精确度，而将早期回报与OUI结合则在最佳筛选机制中实现最高精确度，从而无需完整训练即可对无前景的训练过程进行激进剪枝。

The paper addresses the sensitivity of deep reinforcement learning, specifically Proximal Policy Optimization (PPO), to learning rate selection, where improper rates cause slow convergence or instability. The method employs the Overfitting-Underfitting Indicator (OUI), a metric analyzing binary activation patterns in hidden neurons to quantify structural evolution, with a theoretical link established between learning rate and activation sign changes. Experimental results across discrete-control environments show that OUI measured early in training effectively discriminates learning rate regimes, revealing asymmetric patterns between actor and critic networks, and outperforms other early screening criteria in precision for pruning unpromising runs.
本文针对深度强化学习中近端策略优化（PPO）对学习率高度敏感的问题展开研究，不当的学习率会导致收敛缓慢或不稳定。方法上采用过拟合-欠拟合指标（OUI），通过分析隐藏神经元的二元激活模式来量化网络结构演化，并从理论上建立了学习率与激活符号变化之间的联系。实验结果表明，在离散控制环境中，早期训练的OUI测量能有效区分学习率区间，揭示了执行器与评论器网络的不对称模式，且OUI在早期筛选中的精度优于其他指标，有助于高效剪除无望的训练过程。
Code-Space Response Oracles: Generating Interpretable Multi-Agent Policies with Large Language Models
Authors: Daniel Hennes, Zun Li, John Schultz, Marc Lanctot
First: 2026-03-10T17:37:06+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-10T17:37:06+00:00
Comments: Accepted as an Extended Abstract at the Twenty-Fifth International Conference on Autonomous Agents and Multiagent Systems (AAMAS)
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Recent advances in multi-agent reinforcement learning, particularly Policy-Space Response Oracles (PSRO), have enabled the computation of approximate game-theoretic equilibria in increasingly complex domains. However, these methods rely on deep reinforcement learning oracles that produce `black-box' neural network policies, making them difficult to interpret, trust or debug. We introduce Code-Space Response Oracles (CSRO), a novel framework that addresses this challenge by replacing RL oracles with Large Language Models (LLMs). CSRO reframes the best response computation as a code generation task, prompting an LLM to generate policies directly as human-readable code. This approach not only yields inherently interpretable policies but also leverages the LLM's pretrained knowledge to discover complex, human-like strategies. We explore multiple ways to construct and enhance an LLM-based oracle: zero-shot prompting, iterative refinement and \emph{AlphaEvolve}, a distributed LLM-based evolutionary system. We demonstrate that CSRO achieves performance competitive with baselines while producing a diverse set of explainable policies. Our work presents a new perspective on multi-agent learning, shifting the focus from optimizing opaque policy parameters to synthesizing interpretable algorithmic behavior.
中文标题/摘要
标题：代码空间响应预言机：利用大型语言模型生成可解释的多智能体策略
多智能体强化学习的最新进展，特别是策略空间响应预言机（PSRO），已能在日益复杂的领域中计算近似博弈论均衡。然而，这些方法依赖于产生“黑盒”神经网络策略的深度强化学习预言机，使其难以解释、信任或调试。我们提出代码空间响应预言机（CSRO），这一新颖框架通过用大型语言模型（LLM）替代强化学习预言机来解决此挑战。CSRO将最佳响应计算重构为代码生成任务，提示LLM直接生成人类可读的代码策略。该方法不仅产生本质可解释的策略，还利用LLM的预训练知识发现复杂、类人的策略。我们探索了多种构建和增强基于LLM的预言机的方法：零样本提示、迭代优化和AlphaEvolve——一个基于LLM的分布式进化系统。实验表明，CSRO在保持与基线方法相当性能的同时，能生成多样化的可解释策略。本研究为多智能体学习提供了新视角，将焦点从优化不透明的策略参数转向合成可解释的算法行为。

Adversarial Latent-State Training for Robust Policies in Partially Observable Domains
Authors: Angad Singh Ahuja
First: 2026-03-07T19:06:49+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-10T17:36:57+00:00
Comments: 25 pages, 3 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Robustness under latent distribution shift remains challenging in partially observable reinforcement learning. We formalize a focused setting where an adversary selects a hidden initial latent distribution before the episode, termed an adversarial latent-initial-state POMDP. Theoretically, we prove a latent minimax principle, characterize worst-case defender distributions, and derive approximate best-response inequalities with finite-sample concentration bounds that make the optimization and sampling terms explicit. Empirically, using a Battleship benchmark, we demonstrate that targeted exposure to shifted latent distributions reduces average robustness gaps between Spread and Uniform distributions from 10.3 to 3.1 shots at equal budget. Furthermore, iterative best-response training exhibits budget-sensitive behavior that is qualitatively consistent with the theorem-guided diagnostics once one accounts for discounted PPO surrogates and finite-sample noise. Ultimately, we show that for latent-initial-state problems, the framework yields a clean evaluation game and useful theorem-motivated diagnostics while also making clear where implementation-level surrogates and optimization limits enter.
中文标题/摘要
标题：面向部分可观测领域鲁棒策略的对抗性潜在状态训练
在部分可观测强化学习中，潜在分布偏移下的鲁棒性仍是挑战。我们形式化了一个聚焦设定：智能体在回合开始前选择隐藏的初始潜在分布，称为对抗性潜在初始状态POMDP。理论上，我们证明了潜在极小极大原理，刻画了最坏情况防御者分布，并推导出具有有限样本集中界限的近似最优响应不等式，使优化项与采样项显式化。在Battleship基准测试中，实验表明定向暴露于偏移潜在分布可将Spread与Uniform分布间的平均鲁棒性差距在同等预算下从10.3次射击降至3.1次。进一步地，迭代最优响应训练展现出预算敏感行为，在考虑折扣PPO替代函数与有限样本噪声后，该行为与定理指导的诊断定性一致。最终我们证明，对于潜在初始状态问题，该框架提供了清晰的评估博弈与实用的定理驱动诊断，同时明确了实现层替代函数与优化限制的边界。

The paper addresses the challenge of robustness under latent distribution shifts in partially observable reinforcement learning by formalizing an adversarial latent-initial-state POMDP, where an adversary selects a hidden initial latent distribution. Theoretically, it establishes a latent minimax principle, characterizes worst-case defender distributions, and provides finite-sample concentration bounds with explicit optimization and sampling terms. MCP Bridge: A Lightweight, LLM-Agnostic RESTful Proxy for Model Context Protocol Servers
Authors: Arash Ahmadi, Sarah Sharif, Yaser M. Banad
First: 2025-04-11T22:19:48+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-10T17:34:59+00:00
Comments: 42 pages, 28 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large Language Models (LLMs) are increasingly augmented with external tools through standardized interfaces like the Model Context Protocol (MCP). However, current MCP implementations face critical limitations: they typically require local process execution through STDIO transports, making them impractical for resource-constrained environments like mobile devices, web browsers, and edge computing. We present MCP Bridge, a lightweight RESTful proxy that connects to multiple MCP servers and exposes their capabilities through a unified API. Unlike existing solutions, MCP Bridge is fully LLM-agnostic, supporting any backend regardless of vendor. The system implements a risk-based execution model with three security levels-standard execution, confirmation workflow, and Docker isolation-while maintaining backward compatibility with standard MCP clients. However, reliable execution within this framework requires models that can strictly adhere to protocol schemas. To this end, we also fine-tuned the Qwen3 4B and 8B model family on the Agent-Ark/Toucan-1.5M dataset using four Reinforcement Learning techniques: Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO), Dr. GRPO, Beta Normalization Policy Optimization (BNPO), and Decoupled Clip and Dynamic sAmpling Policy Optimization (DAPO). Evaluated on the MCPToolBench++ benchmark, our optimized model achieves an F1 score of 73.0% that outperforms GPT-OSS-120B (62.17%) and remains competitive with the 70B+ parameter baselines. Evaluation demonstrates that MCP Bridge successfully addresses the constraints of direct MCP connections while providing enhanced security controls and cross-platform compatibility, enabling sophisticated LLM-powered applications in previously inaccessible environments.
中文标题/摘要
标题：MCP Bridge：面向模型上下文协议服务器的轻量级、LLM无关RESTful代理
大型语言模型（LLMs）正日益通过模型上下文协议（MCP）等标准化接口与外部工具增强集成。然而，现有MCP实现面临关键局限：通常需通过STDIO传输在本地进程执行，难以适用于移动设备、网页浏览器和边缘计算等资源受限环境。本文提出MCP Bridge——一种轻量级RESTful代理，可连接多个MCP服务器并通过统一API暴露其功能。与现有方案不同，MCP Bridge完全与LLM无关，支持任意供应商的后端。系统采用基于风险的执行模型，提供标准执行、确认工作流和Docker隔离三级安全机制，同时保持与标准MCP客户端的向后兼容性。但该框架的可靠执行需要模型严格遵循协议架构。为此，我们基于Agent-Ark/Toucan-1.5M数据集，采用四种强化学习技术——组相对策略优化（GRPO）、Dr. GRPO、Beta归一化策略优化（BNPO）以及解耦裁剪与动态采样策略优化（DAPO）——对Qwen3 4B和8B模型系列进行微调。在MCPToolBench++基准测试中，优化模型取得73.0%的F1分数，超越GPT-OSS-120B（62.17%），并与70B+参数基线模型保持竞争力。评估表明，MCP Bridge成功解决了直接MCP连接的限制，同时提供增强的安全控制与跨平台兼容性，为先前难以部署的环境实现了复杂的LLM驱动应用。

A Distributional Treatment of Real2Sim2Real for Object-Centric Agent Adaptation in Vision-Driven Deformable Linear Object Manipulation
Authors: Georgios Kamaras, Subramanian Ramamoorthy
Venue: In IEEE Robotics and Automation Letters, Volume 10, Issue 8, August 2025, Pages 8075-8082
First: 2025-02-25T20:01:06+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-10T17:25:35+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We present an integrated (or end-to-end) framework for the Real2Sim2Real problem of manipulating deformable linear objects (DLOs) based on visual perception. Working with a parameterised set of DLOs, we use likelihood-free inference (LFI) to compute the posterior distributions for the physical parameters using which we can approximately simulate the behaviour of each specific DLO. We use these posteriors for domain randomisation while training, in simulation, object-specific visuomotor policies (i.e. assuming only visual and proprioceptive sensory) for a DLO reaching task, using model-free reinforcement learning. We demonstrate the utility of this approach by deploying sim-trained DLO manipulation policies in the real world in a zero-shot manner, i.e. without any further fine-tuning. In this context, we evaluate the capacity of a prominent LFI method to perform fine classification over the parametric set of DLOs, using only visual and proprioceptive data obtained in a dynamic manipulation trajectory. We then study the implications of the resulting domain distributions in sim-based policy learning and real-world performance.
中文标题/摘要
标题：面向视觉驱动可变形线性物体操控中物体中心智能体适配的Real2Sim2Real分布化处理方法
本文提出一种针对基于视觉感知的可变形线性物体操控中Real2Sim2Real问题的端到端集成框架。通过参数化DLO集合，采用无似然推断计算物理参数的后验分布，从而近似模拟各特定DLO的行为特性。在仿真训练中，利用这些后验分布进行领域随机化，通过无模型强化学习训练面向DLO抓取任务的物体特异性视觉运动策略（仅依赖视觉与本体感知）。通过零样本方式将仿真训练的DLO操控策略部署至现实场景（无需额外微调），验证了该方法的实用性。在此背景下，评估了主流LFI方法在动态操控轨迹中仅凭视觉与本体感知数据对参数化DLO集合进行精细分类的能力，进而研究了所得领域分布在仿真策略学习与现实场景性能中的影响机制。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need to adapt robotic agents to manipulate diverse deformable linear objects (DLOs) using vision, this paper introduces an integrated Real2Sim2Real framework. The method employs likelihood-free inference to compute posterior distributions over physical parameters from real-world data, enabling the simulation of specific DLO behaviors; these posteriors are then used for domain randomization during the training of visuomotor policies via model-free reinforcement learning in simulation. Experimental results demonstrate that policies trained in simulation can be deployed zero-shot in the real world, successfully performing DLO reaching tasks, and the study evaluates the framework's ability to classify DLO parameters accurately and its impact on policy performance.
针对机器人需基于视觉操控不同可变形线性物体的适应性问题，本文提出了一种集成的Real2Sim2Real框架。该方法采用无似然推断从真实数据中计算物理参数的后验分布，以模拟特定物体的行为；随后利用这些后验进行域随机化，在仿真中通过无模型强化学习训练视觉运动策略。实验结果表明，仿真训练的策略能够零样本部署到真实世界，成功完成可变形线性物体的抓取任务，同时研究评估了该框架在参数分类上的准确性及其对策略性能的影响。
Influencing LLM Multi-Agent Dialogue via Policy-Parameterized Prompts
Authors: Hongbo Bo, Jingyu Hu, Weiru Liu
First: 2026-03-10T16:47:25+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-10T16:47:25+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large Language Models (LLMs) have emerged as a new paradigm for multi-agent systems. However, existing research on the behaviour of LLM-based multi-agents relies on ad hoc prompts and lacks a principled policy perspective. Different from reinforcement learning, we investigate whether prompt-as-action can be parameterized so as to construct a lightweight policy which consists of a sequence of state-action pairs to influence conversational behaviours without training. Our framework regards prompts as actions executed by LLMs, and dynamically constructs prompts through five components based on the current state of the agent. To test the effectiveness of parameterized control, we evaluated the dialogue flow based on five indicators: responsiveness, rebuttal, evidence usage, non-repetition, and stance shift. We conduct experiments using different LLM-driven agents in two discussion scenarios related to the general public and show that prompt parameterization can influence the dialogue dynamics. This result shows that policy-parameterised prompts offer a simple and effective mechanism to influence the dialogue process, which will help the research of multi-agent systems in the direction of social simulation.
中文标题/摘要
标题：通过策略参数化提示影响大语言模型多智能体对话
大语言模型已成为多智能体系统的新范式，但现有研究依赖临时性提示，缺乏原则性的策略视角。不同于强化学习，本文探究提示作为动作能否被参数化，从而构建轻量级策略——由状态-动作对序列组成，无需训练即可影响对话行为。该框架将提示视为大语言模型执行的动作，并基于智能体当前状态通过五个组件动态构建提示。为验证参数化控制效果，我们从响应性、反驳性、证据使用、非重复性和立场转变五个指标评估对话流。通过在两个公众讨论场景中使用不同大语言模型驱动智能体进行实验，证明提示参数化能有效影响对话动态。结果表明策略参数化提示为影响对话过程提供了简洁有效的机制，将推动多智能体系统在社会模拟方向的研究。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the lack of a principled policy framework in LLM-based multi-agent systems, where behavior is typically guided by ad hoc prompts. The authors propose a method that treats prompts as parameterized actions, constructing a lightweight policy from state-action pairs to influence conversational dynamics without model training. In experiments across two public discussion scenarios, evaluation using metrics like responsiveness and evidence usage demonstrated that this prompt parameterization effectively steers dialogue flow, offering a simple mechanism for social simulation research.
本文针对基于大语言模型的多智能体系统中缺乏原则性策略框架、通常依赖临时提示的问题，提出了一种将提示视为参数化行动的方法，通过状态-行动对构建轻量级策略以影响对话动态，而无需模型训练。在两个公共讨论场景的实验中，使用响应性、证据使用等指标评估表明，这种提示参数化能有效引导对话流程，为社交模拟研究提供了一种简单机制。
Emerging Extrinsic Dexterity in Cluttered Scenes via Dynamics-aware Policy Learning
Authors: Yixin Zheng, Jiangran Lyu, Yifan Zhang, Jiayi Chen, Mi Yan, Yuntian Deng, Xuesong Shi, Xiaoguang Zhao, Yizhou Wang, Zhizheng Zhang, He Wang
First: 2026-03-10T16:40:30+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-10T16:40:30+00:00
Comments: Project Page: https://pku-epic.github.io/DAPL/
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Project1
Abstract
Extrinsic dexterity leverages environmental contact to overcome the limitations of prehensile manipulation. However, achieving such dexterity in cluttered scenes remains challenging and underexplored, as it requires selectively exploiting contact among multiple interacting objects with inherently coupled dynamics. Existing approaches lack explicit modeling of such complex dynamics and therefore fall short in non-prehensile manipulation in cluttered environments, which in turn limits their practical applicability in real-world environments. In this paper, we introduce a Dynamics-Aware Policy Learning (DAPL) framework that can facilitate policy learning with a learned representation of contact-induced object dynamics in cluttered environments. This representation is learned through explicit world modeling and used to condition reinforcement learning, enabling extrinsic dexterity to emerge without hand-crafted contact heuristics or complex reward shaping. We evaluate our approach in both simulation and the real world. Our method outperforms prehensile manipulation, human teleoperation, and prior representation-based policies by over 25% in success rate on unseen simulated cluttered scenes with varying densities. The real-world success rate reaches around 50% across 10 cluttered scenes, while a practical grocery deployment further demonstrates robust sim-to-real transfer and applicability.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于动态感知策略学习的杂乱场景外源灵巧性涌现
外源灵巧性利用环境接触来克服抓取式操作的局限。然而，在杂乱场景中实现此类灵巧性仍具挑战且研究不足，因其需在具有固有耦合动力学的多个交互物体间选择性利用接触。现有方法缺乏对此类复杂动力学的显式建模，因此在杂乱环境中的非抓取式操作表现不足，进而限制了其在实际场景中的应用。本文提出动态感知策略学习框架，该框架可通过学习杂乱环境中接触引发的物体动力学表征来促进策略学习。该表征通过显式世界建模习得，并用于条件强化学习，使外源灵巧性无需人工接触启发规则或复杂奖励设计即可涌现。我们在仿真和现实世界中对方法进行评估。在具有不同密度的未见杂乱仿真场景中，本方法成功率较抓取式操作、人工遥操作及先前的基于表征的策略提升超25%。在10个真实杂乱场景中成功率约达50%，而实际杂货部署进一步验证了稳健的仿真到现实迁移能力与应用潜力。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the challenge of achieving extrinsic dexterity in cluttered scenes, where robots must exploit environmental contacts among multiple objects with coupled dynamics, a task underexplored due to the lack of explicit dynamics modeling in prior methods. It proposes a Dynamics-Aware Policy Learning (DAPL) framework that learns a representation of contact-induced object dynamics through world modeling and uses it to condition reinforcement learning, eliminating the need for hand-crafted heuristics. Experimental results show the method outperforms prehensile manipulation, human teleoperation, and prior representation-based policies by over 25% in success rate on unseen simulated cluttered scenes, with real-world tests achieving around 50% success across 10 scenes and demonstrating robust sim-to-real transfer in a grocery deployment.
本文针对杂乱场景中外在灵巧性实现的挑战展开研究，该场景中机器人需利用多个物体间耦合动力学产生的环境接触，而现有方法因缺乏显式动力学建模而探索不足。作者提出了动力学感知策略学习框架，通过世界建模学习接触引发的物体动力学表征，并以此条件化强化学习，无需手工启发式设计。实验结果表明，该方法在未见过的模拟杂乱场景中，成功率比抓握式操作、人类遥操作及先前基于表征的策略高出25%以上，真实世界测试在10个杂乱场景中达到约50%的成功率，并在杂货部署中展示了稳健的仿真到现实迁移能力。
Improved Robustness of Deep Reinforcement Learning for Control of Time-Varying Systems by Bounded Extremum Seeking
Authors: Shaifalee Saxena, Alan Williams, Rafael Fierro, Alexander Scheinker
First: 2025-10-02T18:53:02+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-10T16:27:14+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
In this paper, we study the use of robust model independent bounded extremum seeking (ES) feedback control to improve the robustness of deep reinforcement learning (DRL) controllers for a class of nonlinear time-varying systems. DRL has the potential to learn from large datasets to quickly control or optimize the outputs of many-parameter systems, but its performance degrades catastrophically when the system model changes rapidly over time. Bounded ES can handle time-varying systems with unknown control directions, but its convergence speed slows down as the number of tuned parameters increases and, like all local adaptive methods, it can get stuck in local minima. We demonstrate that together, DRL and bounded ES result in a hybrid controller whose performance exceeds the sum of its parts with DRL taking advantage of historical data to learn how to quickly control a many-parameter system to a desired setpoint while bounded ES ensures its robustness to time variations. We present a numerical study of a general time-varying system and a combined ES-DRL controller for automatic tuning of the Low Energy Beam Transport section at the Los Alamos Neutron Science Center linear particle accelerator.
中文标题/摘要
标题：通过有界极值搜索提升深度强化学习控制时变系统的鲁棒性
本文研究利用鲁棒模型无关有界极值搜索反馈控制，提升深度强化学习控制器对一类非线性时变系统的鲁棒性。深度强化学习能够从大规模数据中学习，快速控制或优化多参数系统的输出，但当系统模型随时间快速变化时，其性能会急剧下降。有界极值搜索可处理控制方向未知的时变系统，但随着调谐参数增多其收敛速度会减慢，且与所有局部自适应方法一样可能陷入局部极小值。我们证明，深度强化学习与有界极值搜索结合形成的混合控制器性能超越二者独立效果之和：深度强化学习利用历史数据学习如何快速控制多参数系统至目标设定点，而有界极值搜索则确保其对时变特性的鲁棒性。本文通过数值研究展示了一个通用时变系统案例，以及应用于洛斯阿拉莫斯中子科学中心直线粒子加速器低能束流传输段自动调谐的极值搜索-深度强化学习复合控制器。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the challenge of controlling nonlinear time-varying systems where deep reinforcement learning (DRL) controllers often fail under rapid model changes, and bounded extremum seeking (ES) struggles with slow convergence in high-dimensional spaces and local minima. The proposed method combines DRL, which leverages historical data for fast setpoint control in many-parameter systems, with bounded ES, which provides robustness to time variations and unknown control directions, forming a hybrid controller. Experimental results from a numerical study and application to a particle accelerator's beam transport section demonstrate that the hybrid ES-DRL controller achieves superior performance, exceeding the individual capabilities of each approach by ensuring both speed and robustness.
本文针对非线性时变系统的控制问题，其中深度强化学习（DRL）控制器在模型快速变化时性能会严重下降，而有界极值搜索（ES）则面临高维参数收敛速度慢和易陷入局部最优的局限。所提出的方法将DRL（利用历史数据实现多参数系统的快速设定点控制）与有界ES（提供对时变性和未知控制方向的鲁棒性）相结合，形成混合控制器。通过数值模拟和对线性粒子加速器中低能束流传输段的自动调谐应用，实验结果表明，该混合ES-DRL控制器性能卓越，综合了两种方法的优势，在保证速度的同时增强了鲁棒性。
Breaking the Factorization Barrier in Diffusion Language Models
Authors: Ian Li, Zilei Shao, Benjie Wang, Rose Yu, Guy Van den Broeck, Anji Liu
First: 2026-02-09T08:36:39+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-10T15:39:24+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Diffusion language models theoretically allow for efficient parallel generation but are practically hindered by the "factorization barrier": the assumption that simultaneously predicted tokens are independent. This limitation forces a trade-off: models must either sacrifice speed by resolving dependencies sequentially or suffer from incoherence due to factorization. We argue that this barrier arises not from limited backbone expressivity, but from a structural misspecification: models are restricted to fully factorized outputs because explicitly parameterizing a joint distribution would require the Transformer to output a prohibitively large number of parameters. We propose Coupled Discrete Diffusion (CoDD), a hybrid framework that breaks this barrier by replacing the fully-factorized output distribution with a lightweight, tractable probabilistic inference layer. This formulation yields a distribution family that is significantly more expressive than standard factorized priors, enabling the modeling of complex joint dependencies, yet remains compact enough to avoid the prohibitive parameter explosion associated with full joint modeling. Empirically, CoDD seamlessly enhances diverse diffusion language model architectures with negligible overhead, matching the reasoning performance of computationally intensive Reinforcement Learning baselines at a fraction of the training cost. Furthermore, it prevents performance collapse in few-step generation, enabling high-quality outputs at significantly reduced latencies. Code available at: https://github.com/liuanji/CoDD
中文标题/摘要
标题：突破扩散语言模型中的因式分解壁垒
扩散语言模型理论上支持高效并行生成，但实践中受限于“因式分解壁垒”：即假设同时预测的标记相互独立。这一限制迫使模型面临权衡：要么通过顺序解析依赖关系牺牲速度，要么因因式化导致生成内容不连贯。我们认为该壁垒并非源于主干网络表达能力不足，而是结构设定错误：模型被限制为完全因式化的输出，因为显式参数化联合分布需要Transformer输出难以承受的巨量参数。我们提出耦合离散扩散（CoDD）——一种混合框架，通过将完全因式化的输出分布替换为轻量级、易处理的概率推理层来突破此壁垒。该框架生成的分布族表达能力远超标准因式化先验，能建模复杂联合依赖关系，同时保持紧凑性以避免完全联合建模导致的参数爆炸。实证表明，CoDD能以可忽略的开销无缝增强多种扩散语言模型架构，在仅需少量训练成本的情况下，达到计算密集型强化学习基线的推理性能。此外，该方法能防止少步生成中的性能崩溃，在显著降低延迟的同时实现高质量输出。代码发布于：https://github.com/liuanji/CoDD
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the factorization barrier in diffusion language models, where the assumption of independent token predictions forces a trade-off between generation speed and coherence. The authors propose Coupled Discrete Diffusion (CoDD), a hybrid framework that replaces the fully factorized output distribution with a lightweight probabilistic inference layer, enabling the modeling of complex joint dependencies without prohibitive parameter growth. Experimental results show that CoDD enhances diverse diffusion architectures with minimal overhead, matching the reasoning performance of Reinforcement Learning baselines at much lower training costs and preventing performance collapse in few-step generation, thus enabling high-quality outputs at reduced latencies.
本文针对扩散语言模型中的因子化障碍问题展开研究，该障碍源于同时预测的令牌被假设为独立，导致模型必须在生成速度与连贯性之间做出权衡。作者提出了耦合离散扩散（CoDD）这一混合框架，通过用轻量级概率推理层替代完全因子化的输出分布，从而能够建模复杂的联合依赖关系，同时避免参数爆炸。实验结果表明，CoDD以可忽略的开销增强了多种扩散架构，以远低于强化学习基线的训练成本匹配了其推理性能，并防止了少步生成中的性能崩溃，实现了在显著降低延迟下的高质量输出。
Good Reasoning Makes Good Demonstrations: Implicit Reasoning Quality Supervision via In-Context Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Tiehua Mei, Minxuan Lv, Leiyu Pan, Zhenpeng Su, Hongru Hou, Hengrui Chen, Ao Xu, Deqing Yang
First: 2026-03-10T15:33:07+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-10T15:33:07+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) improves reasoning in large language models but treats all correct solutions equally, potentially reinforcing flawed traces that get correct answers by chance. We observe that better reasoning are better teachers: high-quality solutions serve as more effective demonstrations than low-quality ones. We term this teaching ability Demonstration Utility, and show that the policy model's own in-context learning ability provides an efficient way to measure it, yielding a quality signal termed Evidence Gain. To employ this signal during training, we introduce In-Context RLVR. By Bayesian analysis, we show that this objective implicitly reweights rewards by Evidence Gain, assigning higher weights to high-quality traces and lower weights to low-quality ones, without requiring costly computation or external evaluators. Experiments on mathematical benchmarks show improvements in both accuracy and reasoning quality over standard RLVR.
中文标题/摘要
标题：优质推理成就优质演示：通过上下文强化学习实现隐式推理质量监督
可验证奖励强化学习（RLVR）虽能提升大语言模型的推理能力，但将所有正确解答等同对待，可能强化那些偶然得出正确答案的缺陷推理轨迹。我们发现，更优的推理即更优的教师：高质量解答比低质量解答能提供更有效的演示示范。我们将这种教学能力定义为演示效用，并证明策略模型自身的上下文学习能力可高效度量该效用，由此产生名为证据增益的质量信号。为在训练中利用此信号，我们提出上下文RLVR方法。通过贝叶斯分析表明，该目标能依据证据增益隐式调整奖励权重，为高质量轨迹分配更高权重、低质量轨迹分配更低权重，且无需昂贵计算或外部评估器。数学基准实验显示，该方法在准确性与推理质量上均优于标准RLVR。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses a limitation in Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR), which treats all correct reasoning traces equally, potentially reinforcing flawed reasoning that leads to correct answers by chance. The authors propose that high-quality reasoning traces serve as better demonstrations, a concept termed Demonstration Utility, and they measure this via the policy model's in-context learning ability, yielding a quality signal called Evidence Gain. Their method, In-Context RLVR, implicitly reweights rewards based on Evidence Gain through Bayesian analysis, prioritizing high-quality traces without extra computational cost. Experimental results on mathematical benchmarks demonstrate improvements in both accuracy and reasoning quality compared to standard RLVR.
本文针对可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR）的局限性，即对所有正确的推理轨迹一视同仁，可能强化那些偶然得出正确答案但有缺陷的推理。作者提出高质量推理轨迹能作为更好的示范，这一概念称为示范效用，并通过策略模型的上下文学习能力来度量，产生一个称为证据增益的质量信号。他们提出的方法——上下文RLVR，通过贝叶斯分析基于证据增益隐式地重新加权奖励，优先考虑高质量轨迹，无需额外计算成本。在数学基准测试上的实验结果表明，相较于标准RLVR，该方法在准确性和推理质量上均有提升。
A Survey of Weight Space Learning: Understanding, Representation, and Generation
Authors: Xiaolong Han, Zehong Wang, Bo Zhao, Binchi Zhang, Jundong Li, Damian Borth, Rose Yu, Haggai Maron, Yanfang Ye, Lu Yin, Ferrante Neri
First: 2026-03-10T15:32:23+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-10T15:32:23+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Neural network weights are typically viewed as the end product of training, while most deep learning research focuses on data, features, and architectures. However, recent advances show that the set of all possible weight values (weight space) itself contains rich structure: pretrained models form organized distributions, exhibit symmetries, and can be embedded, compared, or even generated. Understanding such structures has tremendous impact on how neural networks are analyzed and compared, and on how knowledge is transferred across models, beyond individual training instances. This emerging research direction, which we refer to as Weight Space Learning (WSL), treats neural weights as a meaningful domain for analysis and modeling. This survey provides the first unified taxonomy of WSL. We categorize existing methods into three core dimensions: Weight Space Understanding (WSU), which studies the geometry and symmetries of weights; Weight Space Representation (WSR), which learns embeddings over model weights; and Weight Space Generation (WSG), which synthesizes new weights through hypernetworks or generative models. We further show how these developments enable practical applications, including model retrieval, continual and federated learning, neural architecture search, and data-free reconstruction. By consolidating fragmented progress under a coherent framework, this survey highlights weight space as a learnable, structured domain with growing impact across model analysis, transferring, and weight generation. We release an accompanying resource at https://github.com/Zehong-Wang/Awesome-Weight-Space-Learning.
中文标题/摘要
标题：权重空间学习综述：理解、表示与生成
神经网络权重通常被视为训练的最终产物，而多数深度学习研究聚焦于数据、特征与架构。然而，近期研究表明所有权重可能取值构成的集合（权重空间）本身蕴含丰富结构：预训练模型形成有组织的分布、呈现对称性，并可被嵌入、比较甚至生成。理解此类结构对神经网络的分析比较方式、以及跨模型知识迁移（超越单一训练实例）具有重大影响。这一新兴研究方向——我们称之为权重空间学习（WSL）——将神经权重视为具有分析建模意义的领域。本综述首次提出WSL的统一分类体系，将现有方法归纳为三个核心维度：权重空间理解（WSU），研究权重的几何特性与对称性；权重空间表示（WSR），学习模型权重的嵌入表示；权重空间生成（WSG），通过超网络或生成模型合成新权重。我们进一步阐述这些进展如何推动实际应用，包括模型检索、持续与联邦学习、神经架构搜索及无数据重建。通过将碎片化进展整合至连贯框架，本综述强调权重空间作为可学习的结构化领域，在模型分析、迁移与权重生成方面的影响力日益增强。相关资源发布于https://github.com/Zehong-Wang/Awesome-Weight-Space-Learning。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the recognition that neural network weight spaces possess rich, structured information beyond individual training outcomes, this survey introduces Weight Space Learning (WSL) as a unified framework for analyzing, representing, and generating model weights. The method categorizes existing research into three dimensions: understanding weight geometry and symmetries, learning embeddings for weight representation, and generating new weights via hypernetworks or generative models. Experimental results and applications demonstrate that these approaches enable practical advances in model retrieval, continual learning, federated learning, neural architecture search, and data-free reconstruction, establishing weight space as a foundational domain for model analysis and transfer.
该研究的动机源于认识到神经网络权重空间蕴含超越单个训练结果的丰富结构化信息，因此提出了权重空间学习这一统一框架，用于分析、表示和生成模型权重。方法将现有研究归类为三个维度：理解权重的几何结构与对称性、学习权重的嵌入表示、以及通过超网络或生成模型合成新权重。实验结果表明，这些方法能够有效推动模型检索、持续学习、联邦学习、神经架构搜索和无数据重建等实际应用，确立了权重空间作为模型分析与知识迁移的基础领域。
Stepwise Guided Policy Optimization: Coloring your Incorrect Reasoning in GRPO
Authors: Peter Chen, Xiaopeng Li, Ziniu Li, Xi Chen, Tianyi Lin
First: 2025-05-16T18:02:05+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-10T15:26:37+00:00
Comments: Accepted by TMLR; 47 pages
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement learning (RL) has proven effective in strengthening the reasoning capabilities of large language models (LLMs). A widely adopted method, Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO), has shown strong empirical results in training recent reasoning models, but it fails to update the policy when all responses within a group are incorrect (i.e., all-negative-sample groups). This limitation highlights a gap between artificial and human intelligence: unlike humans, who can learn from mistakes, GRPO discards these failure signals. We introduce a simple framework to mitigate the all-negative-sample issue by incorporating response diversity within groups using a step-wise judge model, which can be trained directly or adapted from existing LLMs. In a simplified setting, we prove that this diversification accelerates GRPO's learning dynamics. We then empirically validate Stepwise Guided Policy Optimization (SGPO) across model sizes (7B, 14B, 32B) in both offline and online training on nine reasoning benchmarks (including base and distilled variants). Overall, SGPO improves average performance and is effective in early and mid-training when all-negative groups are prevalent, while improvements are not uniform across every benchmark and depend on the structure and informativeness of negative samples. Finally, SGPO does not require the judge model to generate correct solutions, distinguishing it from knowledge distillation methods.
中文标题/摘要
标题：逐步引导策略优化：在GRPO中标记错误推理路径
强化学习（RL）已被证明能有效增强大语言模型（LLM）的推理能力。广泛采用的组相对策略优化（GRPO）方法在训练近期推理模型时展现出显著的实证效果，但当组内所有响应均错误（即全负样本组）时，该方法无法更新策略。这一局限凸显了人工智能与人类智能的差距：与人类能从错误中学习不同，GRPO丢弃了这些失败信号。我们提出一个简单框架，通过引入基于逐步评判模型的组内响应多样性来缓解全负样本问题，该评判模型可直接训练或从现有LLM适配。在简化设定中，我们证明这种多样化能加速GRPO的学习动态。随后，我们在九个推理基准测试（含基础版与蒸馏变体）上，通过离线与在线训练对不同规模模型（7B、14B、32B）进行了Stepwise Guided Policy Optimization（SGPO）的实证验证。总体而言，SGPO提升了平均性能，且在全负样本组频现的训练早中期效果显著，但改进并非在所有基准测试中均匀体现，其效果取决于负样本的结构与信息量。最后，SGPO无需评判模型生成正确答案，这使其区别于知识蒸馏方法。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the limitation of Group Relative Policy Optimization (GRPO) in handling all-negative-sample groups where all responses are incorrect, which prevents learning from mistakes unlike human intelligence, this paper introduces Stepwise Guided Policy Optimization (SGPO) to enhance reasoning in large language models. The method incorporates response diversity within groups using a stepwise judge model, either trained directly or adapted from existing LLMs, to mitigate the issue; theoretically, this diversification accelerates GRPO's learning dynamics in a simplified setting. Experimental results across model sizes (7B to 32B) on nine reasoning benchmarks in offline and online training show that SGPO improves average performance, particularly in early and mid-training when all-negative groups are common, though improvements vary by benchmark and depend on negative sample structure, without requiring the judge model to generate correct solutions, distinguishing it from knowledge distillation.
本文的动机是解决群体相对策略优化（GRPO）在处理全负样本组（即所有回答均错误）时的局限性，该问题阻碍了从错误中学习，而人类智能却具备此能力。方法上，提出了逐步引导策略优化（SGPO），通过使用逐步判断模型（可直接训练或从现有大语言模型适配）在组内引入回答多样性，以缓解全负样本问题；理论分析表明，在简化设定中，这种多样化加速了GRPO的学习动态。主要实验结果在多个模型规模（7B至32B）和九个推理基准（包括基础和蒸馏变体）的离线与在线训练中验证，SGPO提高了平均性能，尤其在全负样本组常见的中早期训练阶段效果显著，但改进因基准而异并依赖于负样本的结构和信息量，且无需判断模型生成正确答案，从而与知识蒸馏方法区分开来。
Information Theoretic Bayesian Optimization over the Probability Simplex
Authors: Federico Pavesi, Antonio Candelieri, Noémie Jaquier
First: 2026-03-10T15:25:56+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-10T15:25:56+00:00
Comments: 16 pages, 5 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Bayesian optimization is a data-efficient technique that has been shown to be extremely powerful to optimize expensive, black-box, and possibly noisy objective functions. Many applications involve optimizing probabilities and mixtures which naturally belong to the probability simplex, a constrained non-Euclidean domain defined by non-negative entries summing to one. This paper introduces $α$-GaBO, a novel family of Bayesian optimization algorithms over the probability simplex. Our approach is grounded in information geometry, a branch of Riemannian geometry which endows the simplex with a Riemannian metric and a class of connections. Based on information geometry theory, we construct Matérn kernels that reflect the geometry of the probability simplex, as well as a one-parameter family of geometric optimizers for the acquisition function. We validate our method on benchmark functions and on a variety of real-world applications including mixtures of components, mixtures of classifiers, and a robotic control task, showing its increased performance compared to constrained Euclidean approaches.
中文标题/摘要
标题：概率单纯形上的信息论贝叶斯优化
贝叶斯优化是一种数据高效的技术，已被证明在优化昂贵、黑盒且可能含噪声的目标函数方面极具优势。许多应用涉及优化概率和混合模型，这些模型天然属于概率单纯形——一个由非负元素且和为1定义的约束非欧几里得域。本文提出了$α$-GaBO，一种在概率单纯形上进行贝叶斯优化的新型算法族。该方法基于信息几何学（黎曼几何的一个分支），为单纯形赋予了黎曼度量和一类联络。基于信息几何理论，我们构建了反映概率单纯形几何结构的Matérn核函数，以及用于采集函数的单参数几何优化器族。我们在基准函数和多种实际应用（包括组件混合、分类器混合和机器人控制任务）上验证了本方法，结果表明其性能优于约束欧几里得方法。
Summary / 总结
The paper is motivated by the need to perform Bayesian optimization over the probability simplex, a common domain for problems involving probabilities and mixtures where standard Euclidean methods are inadequate. The method, named α-GaBO, leverages information geometry to construct Matérn kernels that respect the simplex's Riemannian structure and introduces a family of geometric optimizers for the acquisition function. Experimental results on benchmark functions and real-world tasks, such as mixture optimization and robotic control, demonstrate that α-GaBO outperforms constrained Euclidean optimization approaches.
本文的动机是在概率单纯形上进行贝叶斯优化，这是涉及概率和混合问题的常见领域，而标准的欧几里得方法在此不适用。该方法名为α-GaBO，利用信息几何构建了反映单纯形黎曼结构的Matérn核，并引入了一系列用于获取函数的几何优化器。在基准函数和实际任务（如混合优化和机器人控制）上的实验结果表明，α-GaBO的性能优于受约束的欧几里得优化方法。
Dynamic Vehicle Routing Problem with Prompt Confirmation of Advance Requests
Authors: Amutheezan Sivagnanam, Ayan Mukhopadhyay, Samitha Samaranayake, Abhishek Dubey, Aron Laszka
First: 2026-03-08T02:34:41+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-10T15:21:16+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Transit agencies that operate on-demand transportation services have to respond to trip requests from passengers in real time, which involves solving dynamic vehicle routing problems with pick-up and drop-off constraints. Based on discussions with public transit agencies, we observe a real-world problem that is not addressed by prior work: when trips are booked in advance (e.g., trip requests arrive a few hours in advance of their requested pick-up times), the agency needs to promptly confirm whether a request can be accepted or not, and ensure that accepted requests are served as promised. State-of-the-art computational approaches either provide prompt confirmation but lack the ability to continually optimize and improve routes for accepted requests, or they provide continual optimization but cannot guarantee serving all accepted requests. To address this gap, we introduce a novel problem formulation of dynamic vehicle routing with prompt confirmation and continual optimization. We propose a novel computational approach for this vehicle routing problem, which integrates a quick insertion search for prompt confirmation with an anytime algorithm for continual optimization. To maximize the number requests served, we train a non-myopic objective function using reinforcement learning, which guides both the insertion and the anytime algorithms towards optimal, non-myopic solutions. We evaluate our computational approach on a real-world microtransit dataset from a public transit agency in the U.S., demonstrating that our proposed approach provides prompt confirmation while significantly increasing the number of requests served compared to existing approaches.
中文标题/摘要
标题：具备提前请求即时确认功能的动态车辆路径规划问题
运营按需交通服务的公交机构需实时响应乘客出行请求，这涉及解决带有接送约束的动态车辆路径问题。基于与公交机构的研讨，我们发现既有研究未解决的实际问题：当行程被提前预订时（例如出行请求在预约接载时间前数小时到达），机构需即时确认请求能否受理，并确保已受理请求按承诺履行。现有计算方法要么能提供即时确认但缺乏对已受理请求的持续路径优化能力，要么能持续优化但无法保证所有受理请求的服务履约。为填补这一空白，我们提出一种融合即时确认与持续优化的新型动态车辆路径问题框架，并针对该路径问题设计创新计算方法——将用于即时确认的快速插入搜索与支持持续优化的任意时间算法相结合。为最大化服务请求数量，我们通过强化学习训练非短视目标函数，引导插入算法与任意时间算法获得最优非短视解。基于美国某公交机构的真实微出行数据集评估表明：相较于现有方法，本方案在提供即时确认的同时，显著提升了可服务的请求数量。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses a practical gap in dynamic vehicle routing for on-demand transit services, where agencies must promptly confirm advance trip bookings while ensuring accepted requests are served and routes are continually optimized. The authors propose a novel computational approach that combines a quick insertion search for immediate confirmation with an anytime algorithm for ongoing optimization, guided by a reinforcement-learned non-myopic objective to maximize served requests. Experimental evaluation on a real-world U.S. microtransit dataset shows the method provides prompt confirmation and significantly increases the number of requests served compared to existing approaches.
本文针对按需交通服务中的动态车辆路径规划问题，解决了现有方法无法同时实现提前预订请求的即时确认与持续路线优化的实际缺陷。作者提出了一种新颖的计算方法，将用于快速确认的插入搜索与持续优化的随时算法相结合，并通过强化学习训练的非短视目标函数来最大化服务请求数量。基于美国公共交通机构的真实微出行数据集评估表明，该方法在提供即时确认的同时，相比现有方法显著增加了可服务的请求数量。
Rewards as Labels: Revisiting RLVR from a Classification Perspective
Authors: Zepeng Zhai, Meilin Chen, Jiaxuan Zhao, Junlang Qian, Lei Shen, Yuan Lu
First: 2026-02-05T13:11:36+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-10T14:02:06+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards has recently advanced the capabilities of Large Language Models in complex reasoning tasks by providing explicit rule-based supervision. Among RLVR methods, GRPO and its variants have achieved strong empirical performance. Despite their success, we identify that they suffer from Gradient Misassignment in Positives and Gradient Domination in Negatives, which lead to inefficient and suboptimal policy updates. To address these issues, we propose Rewards as Labels (REAL), a novel framework that revisits verifiable rewards as categorical labels rather than scalar weights, thereby reformulating policy optimization as a classification problem. Building on this, we further introduce anchor logits to enhance policy learning. Our analysis reveals that REAL induces a monotonic and bounded gradient weighting, enabling balanced gradient allocation across rollouts and effectively mitigating the identified mismatches. Extensive experiments on mathematical reasoning benchmarks show that REAL improves training stability and consistently outperforms GRPO and strong variants such as DAPO. On the 1.5B model, REAL improves average Pass@1 over DAPO by 6.7%. These gains further scale to 7B model, REAL continues to outperform DAPO and GSPO by 6.2% and 1.7%, respectively. Notably, even with a vanilla binary cross-entropy, REAL remains stable and exceeds DAPO by 4.5% on average.
中文标题/摘要
标题：奖励作为标签：从分类视角重审RLVR
可验证奖励的强化学习通过提供明确的基于规则的监督，近期显著提升了大型语言模型在复杂推理任务中的能力。在RLVR方法中，GRPO及其变体已取得优异的实证性能。尽管成果显著，我们发现这些方法存在正样本梯度错配与负样本梯度主导问题，导致策略更新效率低下且非最优。为解决这些问题，我们提出奖励作为标签框架，将可验证奖励重新视为分类标签而非标量权重，从而将策略优化重构为分类问题。在此基础上，我们进一步引入锚定逻辑值以增强策略学习。分析表明，REAL能产生单调有界的梯度加权，实现跨回合的平衡梯度分配，有效缓解已识别的失配问题。在数学推理基准上的大量实验显示，REAL提升了训练稳定性，并持续超越GRPO及DAPO等强效变体。在15亿参数模型中，REAL的Pass@1平均指标较DAPO提升6.7%。该优势进一步扩展至70亿参数模型，REAL分别以6.2%和1.7%持续超越DAPO与GSPO。值得注意的是，即使采用基础二元交叉熵，REAL仍保持稳定，平均性能超越DAPO达4.5%。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by identified inefficiencies in existing Reinforcement Learning with Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) methods, specifically Gradient Misassignment in Positives and Gradient Domination in Negatives in approaches like GRPO, this paper proposes a novel framework called Rewards as Labels (REAL). The method reformulates policy optimization as a classification problem by treating verifiable rewards as categorical labels rather than scalar weights, and further introduces anchor logits to enhance learning. Experimental results on mathematical reasoning benchmarks demonstrate that REAL improves training stability and consistently outperforms strong baselines, including GRPO and DAPO, achieving significant performance gains of up to 6.7% in Pass@1 on a 1.5B model, with these improvements scaling effectively to larger 7B models.
本文的动机源于现有可验证奖励强化学习方法（如GRPO）中存在的梯度分配不当与梯度主导问题，导致策略更新低效。为此，作者提出了名为“奖励即标签”的新框架，其核心方法是将可验证的奖励重新视为分类标签而非标量权重，从而将策略优化重构为一个分类问题，并引入锚定逻辑值以增强学习。在数学推理基准上的主要实验结果表明，该方法显著提升了训练稳定性，并持续超越了GRPO、DAPO等强基线模型，在15亿参数模型上将平均Pass@1性能提升了6.7%，且该优势在70亿参数模型上依然保持。
ActiveUltraFeedback: Efficient Preference Data Generation using Active Learning
Authors: Davit Melikidze, Marian Schneider, Jessica Lam, Martin Wertich, Ido Hakimi, Barna Pásztor, Andreas Krause
First: 2026-03-10T13:59:50+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-10T13:59:50+00:00
Comments: 35 pages, 6 figures, 24 tables
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Reinforcement Learning from Human Feedback (RLHF) has become the standard for aligning Large Language Models (LLMs), yet its efficacy is bottlenecked by the high cost of acquiring preference data, especially in low-resource and expert domains. To address this, we introduce ACTIVEULTRAFEEDBACK, a modular active learning pipeline that leverages uncertainty estimates to dynamically identify the most informative responses for annotation. Our pipeline facilitates the systematic evaluation of standard response selection methods alongside DOUBLE REVERSE THOMPSON SAMPLING (DRTS) and DELTAUCB, two novel methods prioritizing response pairs with large predicted quality gaps, leveraging recent results showing that such pairs provide good signals for fine-tuning. Our experiments demonstrate that ACTIVEULTRAFEEDBACK yields high-quality datasets that lead to significant improvements in downstream performance, notably achieving comparable or superior results with as little as one-sixth of the annotated data relative to static baselines. Our pipeline is available at https://github.com/lasgroup/ActiveUltraFeedback and our preference datasets at https://huggingface.co/ActiveUltraFeedback.
中文标题/摘要
标题：ActiveUltraFeedback：利用主动学习高效生成偏好数据
基于人类反馈的强化学习（RLHF）已成为对齐大型语言模型（LLMs）的标准方法，但其效果受限于获取偏好数据的高昂成本，在低资源和专业领域尤为突出。为此，我们提出ACTIVEULTRAFEEDBACK——一种模块化主动学习流程，通过不确定性估计动态识别最具信息价值的待标注响应。该流程支持对标准响应选择方法及两种新方法进行系统评估：双重逆汤普森采样（DRTS）和DELTAUCB。这两种新方法优先选择预测质量差距较大的响应对，其依据是近期研究表明此类响应对能为微调提供优质信号。实验表明，ACTIVEULTRAFEEDBACK生成的高质量数据集能显著提升下游任务性能，仅需静态基线方法六分之一的标注数据即可获得相当或更优的结果。项目代码发布于https://github.com/lasgroup/ActiveUltraFeedback，偏好数据集发布于https://huggingface.co/ActiveUltraFeedback。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the high cost of acquiring preference data for Reinforcement Learning from Human Feedback (RLHF), especially in low-resource domains, by introducing ActiveUltraFeedback, an active learning pipeline that uses uncertainty estimates to dynamically select the most informative responses for annotation. The method incorporates novel selection strategies like Double Reverse Thompson Sampling (DRTS) and DeltaUCB, which prioritize response pairs with large predicted quality gaps to provide strong training signals. Experimental results show that this approach generates high-quality datasets, achieving comparable or superior downstream performance with as little as one-sixth of the annotated data compared to static baselines.
本文针对基于人类反馈的强化学习（RLHF）中偏好数据获取成本高的问题，特别是在低资源和专业领域，提出了ActiveUltraFeedback，一种利用不确定性估计动态选择最具信息量的响应进行标注的主动学习流程。该方法引入了如双逆汤普森采样（DRTS）和DeltaUCB等新颖选择策略，优先选择预测质量差距大的响应对以提供有效的训练信号。实验结果表明，该方法能生成高质量数据集，仅需静态基线六分之一的标注数据即可实现相当或更优的下游性能。
Periodic Asynchrony: An On-Policy Approach for Accelerating LLM Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Jian Lu
First: 2025-11-24T08:22:50+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-10T13:59:11+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Since the introduction of the GRPO algorithm, reinforcement learning (RL) has attracted increasing attention for LLM post-training, yet training efficiency remains a critical challenge. In mainstream RL frameworks, inference and training are co-located on the same devices, and their synchronous execution prevents concurrent inference and training. In this work, we revisit the strategy of separating inference and training deployment, and propose a periodically asynchronous framework that transforms synchronous RL training into an asynchronous producer-consumer pipeline. Unlike existing asynchronous approaches that introduce off-policy bias, our design is provably equivalent to its synchronous counterpart, preserving strict on-policy correctness without any algorithmic modifications. We further introduce a unified tri-model architecture and a shared-prompt attention mechanism to support efficient asynchronous execution and reduce redundant computation. Experiments on NPU platforms demonstrate a three- to five-fold improvement in end-to-end training throughput over mainstream RL frameworks, while maintaining fully comparable accuracy, indicating its potential for widespread application.
中文标题/摘要
标题：周期性异步：一种加速大语言模型强化学习的同策略方法
自GRPO算法提出以来，强化学习在大语言模型后训练中日益受到关注，但训练效率仍是关键挑战。主流强化学习框架将推理与训练部署在同一设备上，其同步执行阻碍了二者的并发进行。本研究重新审视推理与训练分离部署的策略，提出一种周期性异步框架，将同步强化学习训练转化为异步生产者-消费者流水线。与现有会引入异策略偏差的异步方法不同，我们的设计可证明与其同步版本等效，在无需算法修改的情况下保持严格的同策略正确性。我们进一步引入统一的三模型架构和共享提示注意力机制，以支持高效异步执行并减少冗余计算。在NPU平台上的实验表明，相比主流强化学习框架，端到端训练吞吐量提升三至五倍，同时保持完全相当的精度，显示出其广泛应用的潜力。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the training efficiency challenges in synchronous reinforcement learning (RL) for large language models (LLMs), where inference and training are co-located and block each other, this paper proposes a periodically asynchronous framework that decouples inference and training into a producer-consumer pipeline. The method introduces a unified tri-model architecture and a shared-prompt attention mechanism to enable efficient asynchronous execution while provably maintaining on-policy correctness equivalent to synchronous RL, avoiding off-policy bias. Experimental results on NPU platforms show a three- to five-fold improvement in end-to-end training throughput compared to mainstream RL frameworks, with fully comparable accuracy, highlighting its practical potential.
本文针对大型语言模型强化学习后训练中同步执行导致的效率瓶颈，即推理与训练同设备部署且相互阻塞的问题，提出了一种周期性异步框架，将同步训练转化为生产者-消费者的异步流水线。该方法通过统一的三模型架构和共享提示注意力机制，在保证与同步方法算法等价、不引入离策略偏差的前提下，实现了高效异步计算并减少了冗余。在NPU平台上的实验表明，该框架相比主流强化学习方法将端到端训练吞吐量提升了三到五倍，同时保持了完全相当的准确性，显示出广泛应用的潜力。
Continual uncertainty learning
Authors: Heisei Yonezawa, Ansei Yonezawa, Itsuro Kajiwara
First: 2026-02-19T08:39:42+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-10T11:26:16+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Robust control of mechanical systems with multiple uncertainties remains a fundamental challenge, particularly when nonlinear dynamics and operating-condition variations are intricately intertwined. Although deep reinforcement learning (DRL) combined with domain randomization has shown promise in mitigating the sim-to-real gap, simultaneously handling all the sources of uncertainty often leads to sub-optimal policies and poor learning efficiency. This study formulates a new curriculum-based continual learning framework for robust control problems involving nonlinear dynamical systems in which multiple sources of uncertainty are simultaneously superimposed. The key idea is to decompose a complex control problem with multiple uncertainties into a sequence of continual learning tasks, in which the strategies for handling each uncertainty are acquired sequentially. The original system is extended into a finite set of plants whose dynamic uncertainties are gradually expanded and diversified as learning progresses. The policy is stably updated across the entire plant sets associated with tasks defined by different uncertainty configurations without catastrophic forgetting. To ensure high learning efficiency, we jointly incorporate a model-based controller (MBC), which guarantees a shared baseline performance across the plant sets, into the learning process in order to accelerate the convergence. This residual learning scheme facilitates task-specific optimization of the DRL agent for each uncertainty, thereby enhancing sample efficiency. Finally, this study adopts the proposed method to design an active vibration controller for automotive powertrains as a practical industrial application. We verify that the resulting controller is robust against structural nonlinearities and dynamic variations; thus, it can realize successful sim-to-real transfer.
中文标题/摘要
标题：持续不确定性学习
具有多重不确定性的机械系统鲁棒控制仍是一个根本性挑战，尤其在非线性动力学与工况变化错综交织时。尽管深度强化学习结合领域随机化在缩小仿真与现实差距方面展现出潜力，但同步处理所有不确定性源常导致策略次优与学习效率低下。本研究针对涉及多重不确定性同时叠加的非线性动力学系统鲁棒控制问题，提出一种基于课程学习的持续学习框架。其核心思想是将含多重不确定性的复杂控制问题分解为一系列持续学习任务，按序习得处理各类不确定性的策略。通过将原系统扩展为有限设备集，其动态不确定性随学习进程逐步扩展与多样化。策略能在由不同不确定性配置定义的任务所关联的完整设备集上稳定更新，避免灾难性遗忘。为确保高效学习，我们联合引入基于模型的控制器至学习过程，该控制器能保障跨设备集的共享基线性能，从而加速收敛。此残差学习机制促进了深度强化学习智能体针对各不确定性的任务特异性优化，进而提升样本效率。最后，本研究将所提方法应用于汽车动力总成主动振动控制器设计这一实际工业场景，验证了所得控制器对结构非线性和动态变化具有鲁棒性，可实现成功的仿真到现实迁移。
Summary / 总结
The study is motivated by the challenge of robustly controlling mechanical systems with multiple, intertwined uncertainties, where existing deep reinforcement learning (DRL) methods often yield inefficient learning and sub-optimal policies. The method introduces a curriculum-based continual learning framework that decomposes the complex control problem into sequential tasks, gradually expanding dynamic uncertainties across a set of plants to learn strategies for each uncertainty without catastrophic forgetting, while incorporating a model-based controller to accelerate convergence via residual learning. Experimental results from an automotive powertrain vibration control application demonstrate that the resulting controller achieves robustness against structural nonlinearities and dynamic variations, enabling successful sim-to-real transfer.
本研究旨在解决具有多重交织不确定性的机械系统鲁棒控制难题，现有深度强化学习方法常导致学习效率低下和策略次优。方法上提出了一种基于课程学习的持续学习框架，将复杂控制问题分解为连续任务，通过逐步扩展动态不确定性来依次学习各不确定性的应对策略，避免灾难性遗忘，并结合基于模型的控制器以残差学习加速收敛。在汽车动力总成振动控制的工业应用中，实验结果表明所得控制器对结构非线性和动态变化具有鲁棒性，成功实现了从仿真到现实的迁移。
GenePlan: Evolving Better Generalized PDDL Plans using Large Language Models
Authors: Andrew Murray, Danial Dervovic, Alberto Pozanco, Michael Cashmore
First: 2026-03-10T10:32:05+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-10T10:32:05+00:00
Comments: 54 pages, 4 figures. Accepted to ICAPS 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We present GenePlan (GENeralized Evolutionary Planner), a novel framework that leverages large language model (LLM) assisted evolutionary algorithms to generate domain-dependent generalized planners for classical planning tasks described in PDDL. By casting generalized planning as an optimization problem, GenePlan iteratively evolves interpretable Python planners that minimize plan length across diverse problem instances. In empirical evaluation across six existing benchmark domains and two new domains, GenePlan achieved an average SAT score of 0.91, closely matching the performance of the state-of-the-art planners (SAT score 0.93), and significantly outperforming other LLM-based baselines such as chain-of-thought (CoT) prompting (average SAT score 0.64). The generated planners solve new instances rapidly (average 0.49 seconds per task) and at low cost (average $1.82 per domain using GPT-4o).
中文标题/摘要
标题：GenePlan：利用大语言模型演化更优的通用PDDL规划器
