Cooperative Game-Theoretic Credit Assignment for Multi-Agent Policy Gradients via the Core
Authors: Mengda Ji, Genjiu Xu, Keke Jia, Zekun Duan, Yong Qiu, Jianjun Ge, Mingqiang Li
First: 2025-06-03T08:04:43+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-10T10:06:56+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
This work focuses on the credit assignment problem in cooperative multi-agent reinforcement learning (MARL). Sharing the global advantage among agents often leads to insufficient policy optimization, as it fails to capture the coalitional contributions of different agents. In this work, we revisit the policy update process from a coalitional perspective and propose CORA, an advantage allocation method guided by a cooperative game-theoretic core allocation. By evaluating the marginal contributions of different coalitions and combining clipped double Q-learning to mitigate overestimation bias, CORA estimates coalition-wise advantages. The core formulation enforces coalition-wise lower bounds on allocated credits, so that coalitions with higher advantages receive stronger total incentives for their participating agents, enabling the global advantage to be attributed to different coalition strategies and promoting coordinated optimal behavior. To reduce computational overhead, we employ random coalition sampling to approximate the core allocation efficiently. Experiments on matrix games, differential games, and multi-agent collaboration benchmarks demonstrate that our method outperforms baselines. These findings highlight the importance of coalition-level credit assignment and cooperative games for advancing multi-agent learning.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于核心解的协作博弈论信用分配方法用于多智能体策略梯度
本研究聚焦于协作式多智能体强化学习中的信用分配问题。传统全局优势共享机制常因无法捕捉不同智能体的联盟贡献而导致策略优化不足。本文从联盟视角重新审视策略更新过程，提出CORA——一种以协作博弈论核心分配为指导的优势分配方法。通过评估不同联盟的边际贡献，并结合截断双Q学习以缓解高估偏差，CORA实现了联盟层面的优势估计。核心解形式为分配信用设定了联盟级下界，使具有更高优势的联盟为其参与智能体获得更强的总体激励，从而将全局优势归因于不同的联盟策略，促进协调最优行为。为降低计算开销，我们采用随机联盟采样高效逼近核心分配。在矩阵博弈、微分博弈及多智能体协作基准测试中的实验表明，本方法优于基线模型。这些发现凸显了联盟级信用分配与协作博弈对推进多智能体学习的重要性。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the credit assignment problem in cooperative multi-agent reinforcement learning, motivated by the limitation that sharing a global advantage often fails to capture the contributions of specific agent coalitions, leading to suboptimal policy optimization. The method introduces CORA, an advantage allocation approach that uses a cooperative game-theoretic core allocation to evaluate marginal contributions of different coalitions, combined with clipped double Q-learning to reduce overestimation bias, thereby estimating coalition-wise advantages and enforcing lower bounds on allocated credits to incentivize coordinated behavior. Experimental results on matrix games, differential games, and multi-agent collaboration benchmarks show that CORA outperforms baseline methods, highlighting the effectiveness of coalition-level credit assignment for advancing multi-agent learning.
本文针对合作多智能体强化学习中的信用分配问题，其动机在于共享全局优势往往无法捕捉不同智能体联盟的贡献，导致策略优化不足。方法上提出了CORA，这是一种基于合作博弈论核心分配的信用分配方法，通过评估不同联盟的边际贡献并结合裁剪双Q学习来减少高估偏差，从而估计联盟层面的优势，并通过对分配信用设置联盟下限来激励协调最优行为。在矩阵游戏、微分游戏和多智能体协作基准上的实验结果表明，该方法优于基线方法，突显了联盟级信用分配和合作博弈对推进多智能体学习的重要性。
ADHint: Adaptive Hints with Difficulty Priors for Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Feng Zhang, Zezhong Tan, Xinhong Ma, Ziqiang Dong, Xi Leng, Jianfei Zhao, Xin Sun, Yang Yang
First: 2025-12-15T08:53:47+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-10T09:51:00+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
To address the limited capability expansion and low sample efficiency of Reinforcement Learning (RL), recent methods have integrated ''hints'' into post-training, which are prefix segments of complete reasoning trajectories, aiming for powerful knowledge expansion and reasoning generalization. However, existing hint-based RL methods often neglect the role of difficulty in the hint-ratio schedule and relative-advantage estimation, resulting in unstable learning and excessive imitation of off-policy hints. To address this, we propose ADHint, which explicitly integrates difficulty into both processes to achieve a better trade-off between exploration and imitation. Specifically, we propose Adaptive Hint with Sample Difficulty Prior, which evaluates the difficulty of each sample under the current policy to schedule an appropriate hint ratio for rollout generation. Furthermore, we introduce Consistency-based Gradient Modulation alongside Selective Masking for Hint Preservation, which jointly modulate token-level gradients within hints to prevent biased and destructive updates. Additionally, we propose Advantage Estimation with Rollout Difficulty Posterior, which leverages the relative difficulty of rollouts with and without hints to compute their respective advantages, yielding more balanced updates. Extensive experiments across diverse modalities, model scales, model families, and domains demonstrate that ADHint achieves superior reasoning capabilities and out-of-distribution generalization. Code and datasets will be made publicly available upon paper acceptance.
中文标题/摘要
标题：ADHint：基于难度先验的自适应提示强化学习
针对强化学习（RL）能力扩展有限和样本效率低的问题，近期研究将“提示”整合至训练后阶段——即完整推理轨迹的前缀片段，旨在实现强大的知识扩展与推理泛化。然而，现有基于提示的RL方法常忽视难度在提示比例调度和相对优势估计中的作用，导致学习不稳定及对离策略提示的过度模仿。为此，我们提出ADHint，将难度显式整合至两个过程中，以在探索与模仿间达成更优平衡。具体而言，我们提出基于样本难度先验的自适应提示，通过评估当前策略下各样本的难度，为推演生成调度合适的提示比例。进一步，我们引入基于一致性的梯度调制与选择性掩码提示保留技术，共同调节提示内的词元级梯度，防止有偏且破坏性的更新。此外，我们提出基于推演难度后验的优势估计，利用含提示与无提示推演的相对难度计算各自优势，实现更均衡的更新。跨多模态、模型规模、模型族及领域的广泛实验表明，ADHint能实现更优的推理能力与分布外泛化性能。代码与数据集将在论文录用后公开。
Summary / 总结
The paper introduces ADHint to address the limitations of existing hint-based reinforcement learning methods, which often overlook difficulty in hint scheduling and advantage estimation, leading to unstable learning and excessive imitation. The method integrates difficulty priors by adaptively scheduling hint ratios based on sample difficulty, modulating token-level gradients to preserve useful hints, and estimating advantages using rollout difficulty to balance exploration and imitation. Experimental results across various modalities, model scales, and domains show that ADHint achieves superior reasoning capabilities and out-of-distribution generalization compared to prior approaches.
本文提出ADHint方法，旨在解决现有基于提示的强化学习方法在提示调度和优势估计中忽视难度因素的问题，这些问题导致学习不稳定和过度模仿。该方法通过基于样本难度自适应调度提示比例、调节标记级梯度以保留有用提示，并利用推演难度估计优势来平衡探索与模仿。在多种模态、模型规模和领域的实验中，ADHint展现出更优的推理能力和分布外泛化性能。
Impact of Markov Decision Process Design on Sim-to-Real Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Tatjana Krau, Jorge Mandlmaier, Tobias Damm, Frieder Heieck
First: 2026-03-10T09:41:37+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-10T09:41:37+00:00
Comments: Submitted at the 65th IEEE Conference on Decision and Control
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement Learning (RL) has demonstrated strong potential for industrial process control, yet policies trained in simulation often suffer from a significant sim-to-real gap when deployed on physical hardware. This work systematically analyzes how core Markov Decision Process (MDP) design choices -- state composition, target inclusion, reward formulation, termination criteria, and environment dynamics models -- affect this transfer. Using a color mixing task, we evaluate different MDP configurations and mixing dynamics across simulation and real-world experiments. We validate our findings on physical hardware, demonstrating that physics-based dynamics models achieve up to 50% real-world success under strict precision constraints where simplified models fail entirely. Our results provide practical MDP design guidelines for deploying RL in industrial process control.
中文标题/摘要
标题：马尔可夫决策过程设计对仿真到现实强化学习迁移的影响
强化学习在工业过程控制中展现出巨大潜力，但仿真训练的策略部署至物理硬件时常存在显著的仿真与现实差距。本研究系统分析了马尔可夫决策过程的核心设计要素——状态构成、目标设定、奖励函数构建、终止条件及环境动力学模型——如何影响这种迁移效果。通过颜色混合任务，我们在仿真与真实实验中评估了不同MDP配置与混合动力学模型。在物理硬件上的验证表明：在简化模型完全失效的严格精度约束下，基于物理的动力学模型可实现高达50%的现实成功率。本研究为工业过程控制中强化学习的部署提供了实用的MDP设计准则。
Summary / 总结
This work is motivated by the significant sim-to-real performance gap that hinders the deployment of reinforcement learning (RL) for industrial process control. The method involves a systematic analysis of how core Markov Decision Process (MDP) design choices—including state composition, reward formulation, and environment dynamics—affect policy transfer from simulation to reality, evaluated through a color mixing task. The main experimental results, validated on physical hardware, show that using physics-based dynamics models in the MDP can achieve up to a 50% real-world success rate under strict precision constraints, whereas simplified models fail completely, providing practical design guidelines for RL deployment.
本研究旨在解决强化学习在工业过程控制中部署时，因仿真与现实的性能差距而受阻的问题。其方法是通过一个颜色混合任务，系统性地分析马尔可夫决策过程的核心设计选择——包括状态构成、奖励函数和环境动力学——如何影响策略从仿真到现实的迁移。在物理硬件上验证的主要实验结果表明，在严格的精度约束下，在MDP中使用基于物理的动力学模型可实现高达50%的现实成功率，而简化模型则完全失败，从而为强化学习的实际部署提供了实用的设计指导原则。
Amnesia: Adversarial Semantic Layer Specific Activation Steering in Large Language Models
Authors: Ali Raza, Gurang Gupta, Nikolay Matyunin, Jibesh Patra
First: 2026-03-10T09:41:03+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-10T09:41:03+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Warning: This article includes red-teaming experiments, which contain examples of compromised LLM responses that may be offensive or upsetting. Large Language Models (LLMs) have the potential to create harmful content, such as generating sophisticated phishing emails and assisting in writing code of harmful computer viruses. Thus, it is crucial to ensure their safe and responsible response generation. To reduce the risk of generating harmful or irresponsible content, researchers have developed techniques such as reinforcement learning with human feedback to align LLM's outputs with human values and preferences. However, it is still undetermined whether such measures are sufficient to prevent LLMs from generating interesting responses. In this study, we propose Amnesia, a lightweight activation-space adversarial attack that manipulates internal transformer states to bypass existing safety mechanisms in open-weight LLMs. Through experimental analysis on state-of-the-art, open-weight LLMs, we demonstrate that our attack effectively circumvents existing safeguards, enabling the generation of harmful content without the need for any fine-tuning or additional training. Our experiments on benchmark datasets show that the proposed attack can induce various antisocial behaviors in LLMs. These findings highlight the urgent need for more robust security measures in open-weight LLMs and underscore the importance of continued research to prevent their potential misuse.
中文标题/摘要
标题：遗忘症：大语言模型中的对抗性语义层特定激活引导
警告：本文包含红队测试实验，其中包含可能具有冒犯性或令人不安的受损大语言模型响应示例。大语言模型（LLMs）具有生成有害内容的潜力，例如制作复杂的钓鱼邮件和协助编写有害计算机病毒代码。因此，确保其生成安全、负责任的响应至关重要。为降低生成有害或不负责内容的风险，研究人员已开发出如基于人类反馈的强化学习等技术，以使LLM输出与人类价值观和偏好保持一致。然而，此类措施是否足以防止LLM生成有害响应仍不确定。本研究提出“遗忘症”——一种轻量级的激活空间对抗攻击方法，通过操纵内部Transformer状态来绕过开源权重LLMs中的现有安全机制。通过对先进开源权重LLMs的实验分析，我们证明该攻击能有效规避现有防护机制，无需微调或额外训练即可生成有害内容。在基准数据集上的实验表明，所提攻击可诱发LLMs产生多种反社会行为。这些发现凸显了开源权重LLMs亟需更强大的安全措施，并强调了持续开展研究以防止其潜在滥用的重要性。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by concerns that existing safety alignments like reinforcement learning from human feedback may be insufficient to prevent large language models (LLMs) from generating harmful content, this paper introduces Amnesia, a lightweight adversarial attack method that manipulates specific internal transformer layer activations to bypass safety mechanisms. The method requires no fine-tuning or additional training and operates by steering semantic representations in the model's activation space. Experimental results on state-of-the-art open-weight LLMs demonstrate that the attack effectively circumvents safeguards, inducing various antisocial behaviors and enabling the generation of harmful content, thereby highlighting vulnerabilities in current safety approaches.
本研究针对现有基于人类反馈的强化学习等安全对齐技术可能不足以防止大语言模型生成有害内容的问题，提出了Amnesia——一种轻量级的对抗性攻击方法，通过操纵模型内部Transformer层的特定激活状态来绕过安全机制。该方法无需微调或额外训练，直接在模型的激活空间中引导语义表示。在先进的开源权重大语言模型上的实验结果表明，该攻击能有效规避现有安全防护，诱导模型产生多种反社会行为并生成有害内容，从而揭示了当前安全措施的脆弱性，强调了加强模型安全研究的紧迫性。
SATURN: SAT-based Reinforcement Learning to Unleash LLMs Reasoning
Authors: Huanyu Liu, Ge Li, Jia Li, Hao Zhu, Kechi Zhang, Yihong Dong
Venue: NeurIPS Spotlight
First: 2025-05-22T08:23:10+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-10T08:35:19+00:00
Comments: Camera-ready version for Neural Information Processing Systems (NeurIPS) 2025, Spotlight Paper
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
How to design reinforcement learning (RL) tasks that effectively unleash the reasoning capability of large language models (LLMs) remains an open question. Existing RL tasks (e.g., math, programming, and constructing reasoning tasks) suffer from three key limitations: (1) Scalability. They rely heavily on human annotation or expensive LLM synthesis to generate sufficient training data. (2) Verifiability. LLMs' outputs are hard to verify automatically and reliably. (3) Controllable Difficulty. Most tasks lack fine-grained difficulty control, making it hard to train LLMs to develop reasoning ability from easy to hard. To address these limitations, we propose Saturn, a SAT-based RL framework that uses Boolean Satisfiability (SAT) problems to train and evaluate LLMs reasoning. Saturn enables scalable task construction, rule-based verification, and precise difficulty control. Saturn designs a curriculum learning pipeline that continuously improves LLMs' reasoning capability by constructing SAT tasks of increasing difficulty and training LLMs from easy to hard. To ensure stable training, we design a principled mechanism to control difficulty transitions. We introduce Saturn-2.6k, a dataset of 2,660 SAT problems with varying difficulty. It supports the evaluation of how LLM reasoning changes with problem difficulty. We apply Saturn to DeepSeek-R1-Distill-Qwen and obtain Saturn-1.5B and Saturn-7B. We achieve several notable results: (1) On SAT problems, Saturn-1.5B and Saturn-7B achieve average pass@3 improvements of +14.0 and +28.1, respectively. (2) On math and programming tasks, Saturn-1.5B and Saturn-7B improve average scores by +4.9 and +1.8 on benchmarks (e.g., AIME, LiveCodeBench). (3) Compared to the state-of-the-art (SOTA) approach in constructing RL tasks, Saturn achieves further improvements of +8.8%. We release the source code, data, and models to support future research.
中文标题/摘要
标题：SATURN：基于SAT的强化学习框架释放大语言模型推理能力
如何设计能有效释放大语言模型（LLM）推理能力的强化学习（RL）任务仍是一个开放性问题。现有RL任务（如数学、编程和推理构建任务）存在三个关键局限：（1）可扩展性：严重依赖人工标注或昂贵的LLM合成来生成足够训练数据。（2）可验证性：LLM输出难以自动可靠地验证。（3）难度可控性：多数任务缺乏细粒度难度控制，难以让LLM实现从易到难的推理能力训练。 为突破这些局限，我们提出SATURN——基于布尔可满足性问题（SAT）的强化学习框架，通过SAT问题训练和评估LLM推理能力。该框架支持可扩展的任务构建、基于规则的验证和精确难度控制。SATURN设计了课程学习流程，通过构建难度递增的SAT任务，使LLM实现从易到难的推理能力持续提升。为确保训练稳定性，我们设计了控制难度跃迁的原则性机制。 我们构建了SATURN-2.6k数据集，包含2,660个不同难度的SAT问题，支持评估LLM推理能力随问题难度的变化规律。将SATURN应用于DeepSeek-R1-Distill-Qwen后，我们得到SATURN-1.5B和SATURN-7B模型，取得以下显著成果：（1）在SAT问题上，两个模型平均pass@3指标分别提升+14.0和+28.1。（2）在数学和编程任务中，在AIME、LiveCodeBench等基准测试上平均得分分别提升+4.9和+1.8。（3）相比当前最先进的RL任务构建方法，SATURN进一步实现+8.8%的性能提升。我们已开源代码、数据和模型以支持后续研究。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the challenge of designing scalable and verifiable reinforcement learning (RL) tasks to enhance the reasoning capabilities of large language models (LLMs), overcoming limitations in existing methods such as reliance on costly data generation and lack of fine-grained difficulty control. It introduces Saturn, a framework that uses Boolean Satisfiability (SAT) problems to create RL tasks, enabling scalable construction, rule-based verification, and precise difficulty control through a curriculum learning pipeline that progressively increases problem complexity. Experimental results show that models trained with Saturn, including Saturn-1.5B and Saturn-7B, achieve significant improvements: on SAT problems, they yield average pass@3 gains of +14.0 and +28.1 respectively; on math and programming benchmarks like AIME and LiveCodeBench, scores improve by +4.9 and +1.8; and compared to state-of-the-art RL task construction methods, Saturn provides an additional +8.8% improvement.
本文针对如何设计可扩展且可验证的强化学习任务以提升大语言模型的推理能力这一挑战，解决了现有方法依赖昂贵数据生成和缺乏细粒度难度控制等局限性。提出了Saturn框架，利用布尔可满足性问题构建强化学习任务，通过课程学习流程实现可扩展的任务生成、基于规则的验证和精确的难度控制，逐步增加问题复杂度。实验结果表明，使用Saturn训练的模型（如Saturn-1.5B和Saturn-7B）取得了显著提升：在SAT问题上，平均pass@3分别提高了+14.0和+28.1；在数学和编程基准测试（如AIME和LiveCodeBench）中，分数分别提升了+4.9和+1.8；与最先进的强化学习任务构建方法相比，Saturn进一步实现了+8.8%的改进。
Robust Regularized Policy Iteration under Transition Uncertainty
Authors: Hongqiang Lin, Zhenghui Fu, Weihao Tang, Pengfei Wang, Yiding Sun, Qixian Huang, Dongxu Zhang
First: 2026-03-10T08:18:27+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-10T08:18:27+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Offline reinforcement learning (RL) enables data-efficient and safe policy learning without online exploration, but its performance often degrades under distribution shift. The learned policy may visit out-of-distribution state-action pairs where value estimates and learned dynamics are unreliable. To address policy-induced extrapolation and transition uncertainty in a unified framework, we formulate offline RL as robust policy optimization, treating the transition kernel as a decision variable within an uncertainty set and optimizing the policy against the worst-case dynamics. We propose Robust Regularized Policy Iteration (RRPI), which replaces the intractable max-min bilevel objective with a tractable KL-regularized surrogate and derives an efficient policy iteration procedure based on a robust regularized Bellman operator. We provide theoretical guarantees by showing that the proposed operator is a $γ$-contraction and that iteratively updating the surrogate yields monotonic improvement of the original robust objective with convergence. Experiments on D4RL benchmarks demonstrate that RRPI achieves strong average performance, outperforming recent baselines including percentile-based methods such as PMDB on the majority of environments while remaining competitive on the rest. Moreover, RRPI exhibits robust behavior. The learned $Q$-values decrease in regions with higher epistemic uncertainty, suggesting that the resulting policy avoids unreliable out-of-distribution actions under transition uncertainty.
中文标题/摘要
标题：转移不确定性下的鲁棒正则化策略迭代
离线强化学习（RL）无需在线探索即可实现数据高效且安全的策略学习，但其性能在分布偏移下常会下降。习得策略可能访问价值估计与学习动态均不可靠的分布外状态-动作对。为在统一框架下解决策略诱导的外推与转移不确定性，我们将离线RL表述为鲁棒策略优化，将转移核视为不确定性集合内的决策变量，并针对最坏情况动态优化策略。我们提出鲁棒正则化策略迭代（RRPI），该方法将难解的最大-最小双层目标替换为可处理的KL正则化代理目标，并基于鲁棒正则化贝尔曼算子推导出高效的策略迭代流程。通过证明所提算子是γ-收缩且迭代更新代理目标能单调改进原始鲁棒目标并收敛，我们提供了理论保证。在D4RL基准测试上的实验表明，RRPI在多数环境中实现了强劲的平均性能，优于包括PMDB等百分位数方法在内的近期基线，同时在其余环境中保持竞争力。此外，RRPI展现出鲁棒行为：习得的Q值在认知不确定性较高区域会下降，表明所得策略在转移不确定性下能规避不可靠的分布外动作。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses performance degradation in offline reinforcement learning due to distribution shift, where policies may visit out-of-distribution state-action pairs with unreliable value estimates and dynamics. To unify handling of policy-induced extrapolation and transition uncertainty, the authors formulate offline RL as a robust policy optimization problem, treating the transition kernel as a decision variable within an uncertainty set and optimizing against worst-case dynamics. They propose Robust Regularized Policy Iteration (RRPI), which replaces the intractable max-min objective with a tractable KL-regularized surrogate and derives an efficient policy iteration procedure based on a robust regularized Bellman operator, supported by theoretical guarantees of contraction and monotonic improvement. Experiments on D4RL benchmarks show that RRPI achieves strong average performance, outperforming recent baselines like PMDB in most environments while remaining competitive, with learned Q-values decreasing in high epistemic uncertainty regions, indicating the policy avoids unreliable out-of-distribution actions under transition uncertainty.
该论文针对离线强化学习中因分布偏移导致的性能下降问题，即策略可能访问分布外的状态-动作对，其中价值估计和动态模型不可靠。为统一处理策略引起的推断和转移不确定性，作者将离线强化学习表述为鲁棒策略优化问题，将转移核视为不确定性集合内的决策变量，并针对最坏情况动态进行优化。他们提出了鲁棒正则化策略迭代（RRPI），用可处理的KL正则化替代目标替换了难以求解的最大-最小双层目标，并基于鲁棒正则化贝尔曼算子推导出高效的策略迭代过程，理论分析保证了算子的收缩性和原始鲁棒目标的单调改进收敛性。在D4RL基准测试上的实验表明，RRPI实现了强大的平均性能，在大多数环境中优于包括PMDB在内的近期基线方法，同时在其余环境中保持竞争力，且学习到的Q值在认知不确定性较高区域下降，表明该策略在转移不确定性下避免了不可靠的分布外动作。
Reward-Zero: Language Embedding Driven Implicit Reward Mechanisms for Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Heng Zhang, Haddy Alchaer, Arash Ajoudani, Yu She
First: 2026-03-10T08:07:49+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-10T08:07:49+00:00
Comments: under review
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We introduce Reward-Zero, a general-purpose implicit reward mechanism that transforms natural-language task descriptions into dense, semantically grounded progress signals for reinforcement learning (RL). Reward-Zero serves as a simple yet sophisticated universal reward function that leverages language embeddings for efficient RL training. By comparing the embedding of a task specification with embeddings derived from an agent's interaction experience, Reward-Zero produces a continuous, semantically aligned sense-of-completion signal. This reward supplements sparse or delayed environmental feedback without requiring task-specific engineering. When integrated into standard RL frameworks, it accelerates exploration, stabilizes training, and enhances generalization across diverse tasks. Empirically, agents trained with Reward-Zero converge faster and achieve higher final success rates than conventional methods such as PPO with common reward-shaping baselines, successfully solving tasks that hand-designed rewards could not in some complex tasks. In addition, we develop a mini benchmark for the evaluation of completion sense during task execution via language embeddings. These results highlight the promise of language-driven implicit reward functions as a practical path toward more sample-efficient, generalizable, and scalable RL for embodied agents. Code will be released after peer review.
中文标题/摘要
标题：Reward-Zero：基于语言嵌入驱动的强化学习隐式奖励机制
本文提出Reward-Zero，一种通用隐式奖励机制，可将自然语言任务描述转化为密集、语义接地的进度信号，用于强化学习（RL）。Reward-Zero作为一种简洁而精密的通用奖励函数，利用语言嵌入提升RL训练效率。通过对比任务规范嵌入与智能体交互经验生成的嵌入，Reward-Zero产生连续且语义对齐的任务完成度信号。该奖励机制无需任务特定工程即可补充稀疏或延迟的环境反馈。集成至标准RL框架后，能加速探索、稳定训练并增强跨任务泛化能力。实验表明，使用Reward-Zero训练的智能体比PPO等传统奖励塑形基线方法收敛更快、最终成功率更高，在部分复杂任务中成功解决了手工设计奖励无法应对的难题。此外，我们开发了基于语言嵌入的任务执行完成度评估微型基准。这些成果彰显了语言驱动隐式奖励函数在实现更高样本效率、更强泛化能力和可扩展性具身智能体RL方面的实用潜力。代码将在同行评审后发布。
Summary / 总结
The paper introduces Reward-Zero, a method motivated by the need for efficient reinforcement learning (RL) without task-specific reward engineering. It transforms natural-language task descriptions into dense, semantically grounded progress signals by comparing language embeddings of task specifications with embeddings from agent interactions, creating an implicit reward function that supplements sparse environmental feedback. Experimental results show that agents using Reward-Zero converge faster, achieve higher success rates than methods like PPO with reward-shaping baselines, and solve tasks where hand-designed rewards fail, demonstrating improved exploration, training stability, and generalization across diverse tasks.
本文提出了Reward-Zero方法，其动机在于无需针对特定任务设计奖励机制即可实现高效的强化学习。该方法通过比较任务描述的语言嵌入与智能体交互产生的嵌入，将自然语言任务描述转化为密集的、基于语义的进度信号，从而形成一个隐式奖励函数来补充稀疏的环境反馈。实验结果表明，使用Reward-Zero的智能体比采用PPO等传统奖励塑造基线的方法收敛更快、最终成功率更高，并能解决一些复杂任务中手工设计奖励无法完成的问题，展现了在多样化任务中更好的探索能力、训练稳定性和泛化性能。
Reinforcing Numerical Reasoning in LLMs for Tabular Prediction via Structural Priors
Authors: Pengxiang Cai, Zihao Gao, Wanchen Lian, Jintai Chen
First: 2025-10-20T10:22:01+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-10T08:07:43+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Tabular prediction traditionally relies on gradient-boosted decision trees and deep learning models, which excel in specific tasks but lack interpretability and transferability. Reasoning large language models (LLMs) promise cross-task adaptability with transparent reasoning traces, yet their potential for tabular data remains unrealized. To bridge this gap, we propose a reasoning framework centered on Permutation Relative Policy Optimization (PRPO), a reinforcement learning method that encodes column-permutation invariance as a structural prior. By estimating advantages across label-preserving permutations, PRPO transforms sparse rewards into dense signals, activating latent numerical reasoning capabilities of LLMs with limited supervision. Extensive experiments show that our method matches fully supervised baselines and dominates in zero-shot settings, performing on par with 32-shot strong baselines. Remarkably, our 8B model significantly outperforms much larger LLMs, achieving up to a 53.17% improvement over DeepSeek-R1 (685B).
中文标题/摘要
标题：通过结构先验增强大语言模型在表格预测中的数值推理能力
表格预测传统上依赖梯度提升决策树和深度学习模型，这些模型在特定任务中表现出色但缺乏可解释性和可迁移性。推理型大语言模型（LLMs）凭借透明的推理轨迹展现出跨任务适应潜力，但其在表格数据中的应用尚未充分实现。为填补这一空白，我们提出了以置换相对策略优化（PRPO）为核心的推理框架——这是一种强化学习方法，将列置换不变性编码为结构先验。通过评估标签保持置换下的优势函数，PRPO将稀疏奖励转化为密集信号，以有限监督激活LLMs潜在的数值推理能力。大量实验表明，我们的方法在完全监督基准上表现相当，并在零样本场景中占据主导地位，其性能与32样本强基线持平。值得注意的是，我们的80亿参数模型显著超越规模更大的LLMs，较DeepSeek-R1（6850亿参数）最高提升达53.17%。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need for interpretable and transferable models in tabular prediction, this paper introduces a reinforcement learning framework that enhances numerical reasoning in large language models (LLMs) by incorporating structural priors. The method, Permutation Relative Policy Optimization (PRPO), encodes column-permutation invariance to transform sparse rewards into dense signals, thereby activating latent reasoning capabilities with minimal supervision. Experimental results demonstrate that the approach matches fully supervised baselines and excels in zero-shot settings, with an 8B model notably outperforming much larger LLMs, achieving up to a 53.17% improvement over DeepSeek-R1 (685B).
本文针对表格预测任务中模型可解释性和可迁移性的需求，提出了一种强化学习框架，通过引入结构先验来增强大语言模型的数值推理能力。该方法采用置换相对策略优化，将列置换不变性作为先验知识，将稀疏奖励转化为密集信号，从而在有限监督下激活模型的潜在推理能力。实验结果表明，该方法在完全监督基准上表现相当，并在零样本设置中占据优势，其8B模型显著优于更大的大语言模型，相比DeepSeek-R1实现了高达53.17%的性能提升。
EgoCross: Benchmarking Multimodal Large Language Models for Cross-Domain Egocentric Video Question Answering
Authors: Yanjun Li, Yuqian Fu, Tianwen Qian, Qi'ao Xu, Silong Dai, Danda Pani Paudel, Luc Van Gool, Xiaoling Wang
First: 2025-08-14T15:11:20+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-10T08:04:01+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Recent advances in Multimodal Large Language Models (MLLMs) have significantly pushed the frontier of egocentric video question answering (EgocentricQA). However, existing benchmarks and studies are mainly limited to common daily activities such as cooking and cleaning. In contrast, real-world deployment inevitably encounters domain shifts, where target domains differ substantially in both visual style and semantic content. To bridge this gap, we introduce \textbf{EgoCross}, a comprehensive benchmark designed to evaluate the cross-domain generalization of MLLMs in EgocentricQA. EgoCross covers four diverse and challenging domains, including surgery, industry, extreme sports, and animal perspective, representing realistic and high-impact application scenarios. It comprises approximately 1,000 QA pairs across 798 video clips, spanning four key QA tasks: prediction, recognition, localization, and counting. Each QA pair provides both OpenQA and CloseQA formats to support fine-grained evaluation. Extensive experiments show that most existing MLLMs, whether general-purpose or egocentric-specialized, struggle to generalize to domains beyond daily life, highlighting the limitations of current models. Furthermore, we conduct several pilot studies, e.g., fine-tuning and reinforcement learning, to explore potential improvements. We hope EgoCross and our accompanying analysis will serve as a foundation for advancing domain-adaptive, robust egocentric video understanding.
中文标题/摘要
标题：EgoCross：面向跨领域第一人称视频问答的多模态大语言模型基准评测
多模态大语言模型（MLLMs）的最新进展显著推动了第一人称视频问答（EgocentricQA）的前沿研究。然而，现有基准与研究主要局限于烹饪、清洁等常见日常活动。而实际部署中不可避免地会遇到领域偏移问题，即目标领域在视觉风格与语义内容上均存在显著差异。为填补这一空白，我们提出了**EgoCross**——一个旨在评估MLLMs在第一人称视频问答中跨领域泛化能力的综合性基准。EgoCross涵盖手术、工业、极限运动和动物视角四个多样且富有挑战性的领域，代表了现实且高影响力的应用场景。该基准包含798个视频片段中的约1000个问答对，覆盖预测、识别、定位和计数四项核心问答任务。每个问答对均提供开放式与封闭式两种格式以支持细粒度评估。大量实验表明，现有大多数MLLMs（无论是通用型还是第一人称专用型）均难以泛化至日常生活之外的领域，凸显了当前模型的局限性。此外，我们通过微调与强化学习等试点研究探索了可能的改进方向。我们希望EgoCross及配套分析能为推进领域自适应、鲁棒的第一人称视频理解研究奠定基础。
Summary / 总结
The motivation behind this work is to address the limited cross-domain generalization of Multimodal Large Language Models (MLLMs) in egocentric video question answering (EgocentricQA), as existing benchmarks primarily focus on common daily activities, whereas real-world applications involve diverse domains with distinct visual and semantic characteristics. To bridge this gap, the authors introduce EgoCross, a comprehensive benchmark covering four challenging domains—surgery, industry, extreme sports, and animal perspective—with approximately 1,000 QA pairs across 798 video clips, supporting tasks like prediction, recognition, localization, and counting in both open and closed formats. Experimental results reveal that most current MLLMs, including general-purpose and egocentric-specialized models, struggle to generalize beyond daily-life domains, underscoring their limitations; pilot studies on fine-tuning and reinforcement learning are conducted to explore potential improvements, aiming to advance robust, domain-adaptive egocentric video understanding.
本研究的动机在于解决多模态大语言模型在自我中心视频问答中的跨领域泛化能力不足问题，因为现有基准主要关注日常活动，而实际应用涉及视觉风格和语义内容差异显著的多样领域。为此，作者提出了EgoCross基准，涵盖手术、工业、极限运动和动物视角四个挑战性领域，包含798个视频片段中的约1000个问答对，支持预测、识别、定位和计数等任务，并提供开放和封闭两种问答格式。实验结果表明，当前大多数多模态大语言模型，无论是通用型还是自我中心专用型，都难以泛化到日常生活之外的领域，突显了其局限性；研究还通过微调和强化学习等试点探索了改进潜力，旨在推动鲁棒、领域自适应的自我中心视频理解发展。
On Regret Bounds of Thompson Sampling for Bayesian Optimization
Authors: Shion Takeno, Shogo Iwazaki
First: 2026-03-10T07:02:20+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-10T07:02:20+00:00
Comments: 42 pages
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We study a widely used Bayesian optimization method, Gaussian process Thompson sampling (GP-TS), under the assumption that the objective function is a sample path from a GP. Compared with the GP upper confidence bound (GP-UCB) with established high-probability and expected regret bounds, most analyses of GP-TS have been limited to expected regret. Moreover, whether the recent analyses of GP-UCB for the lenient regret and the improved cumulative regret upper bound can be applied to GP-TS remains unclear. To fill these gaps, this paper shows several regret bounds: (i) a regret lower bound for GP-TS, which implies that GP-TS suffers from a polynomial dependence on $1/δ$ with probability $δ$, (ii) an upper bound of the second moment of cumulative regret, which directly suggests an improved regret upper bound on $δ$, (iii) expected lenient regret upper bounds, and (iv) an improved cumulative regret upper bound on the time horizon $T$. Along the way, we provide several useful lemmas, including a relaxation of the necessary condition from recent analysis to obtain improved regret upper bounds on $T$.
中文标题/摘要
标题：贝叶斯优化中汤普森采样的遗憾界分析
本文研究广泛应用的贝叶斯优化方法——高斯过程汤普森采样（GP-TS），假设目标函数为高斯过程的样本路径。相较于已建立高概率与期望遗憾界的GP上置信界（GP-UCB）方法，现有对GP-TS的分析多局限于期望遗憾。此外，近期针对GP-UCB的宽松遗憾分析与改进累积遗憾上界能否适用于GP-TS尚不明确。为填补这些空白，本文证明了几类遗憾界：（i）GP-TS的遗憾下界，表明其以概率δ存在对1/δ的多项式依赖；（ii）累积遗憾二阶矩的上界，可直接推导出关于δ的改进遗憾上界；（iii）期望宽松遗憾上界；（iv）关于时间范围T的改进累积遗憾上界。研究过程中提出了若干有用引理，包括对近期分析中获取改进T遗憾上界必要条件的松弛化处理。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses gaps in the theoretical understanding of Gaussian process Thompson sampling (GP-TS) for Bayesian optimization, motivated by the need to establish regret bounds comparable to those of GP-UCB, which has well-documented high-probability and expected regret guarantees. The method involves a rigorous theoretical analysis of GP-TS under the assumption that the objective function is a Gaussian process sample path, deriving several key results: a regret lower bound showing polynomial dependence on 1/δ with probability δ, an upper bound on the second moment of cumulative regret leading to improved δ-dependent bounds, expected lenient regret upper bounds, and an enhanced cumulative regret bound dependent on the time horizon T. The main experimental results are theoretical, demonstrating that GP-TS can achieve improved regret guarantees, supported by useful lemmas including a relaxation of conditions from prior analyses to obtain tighter bounds on T.
本文针对贝叶斯优化中高斯过程汤普森采样（GP-TS）的理论理解空白，旨在建立与GP-UCB可比拟的遗憾界，后者已有完善的高概率和期望遗憾保证。方法是在目标函数为高斯过程样本路径的假设下，对GP-TS进行严格理论分析，得出多项关键结果：一个显示以概率δ时对1/δ具有多项式依赖的遗憾下界、一个累积遗憾二阶矩的上界从而改进δ相关界、期望宽松遗憾上界，以及一个依赖于时间范围T的改进累积遗憾上界。主要实验结果为理论性证明，表明GP-TS能够实现改进的遗憾保证，并辅以有用引理，包括放宽先前分析的条件以获得更紧的T相关界。
Multi-Agent Reinforcement Learning with Communication-Constrained Priors
Authors: Guang Yang, Tianpei Yang, Jingwen Qiao, Yanqing Wu, Jing Huo, Xingguo Chen, Yang Gao
First: 2025-12-03T07:35:07+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-10T06:39:54+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Communication is one of the effective means to improve the learning of cooperative policy in multi-agent systems. However, in most real-world scenarios, lossy communication is a prevalent issue. Existing multi-agent reinforcement learning with communication, due to their limited scalability and robustness, struggles to apply to complex and dynamic real-world environments. To address these challenges, we propose a generalized communication-constrained model to uniformly characterize communication conditions across different scenarios. Based on this, we utilize it as a learning prior to distinguish between lossy and lossless messages for specific scenarios. Additionally, we decouple the impact of lossy and lossless messages on distributed decision-making, drawing on a dual mutual information estimatior, and introduce a communication-constrained multi-agent reinforcement learning framework, quantifying the impact of communication messages into the global reward. Finally, we validate the effectiveness of our approach across several communication-constrained benchmarks.
中文标题/摘要
标题：通信约束先验下的多智能体强化学习
通信是提升多智能体系统中协作策略学习的有效手段之一。然而，在多数现实场景中，有损通信是一个普遍存在的问题。现有的带通信的多智能体强化学习方法，由于可扩展性和鲁棒性有限，难以应用于复杂动态的现实环境。为应对这些挑战，我们提出了一种广义通信约束模型，以统一刻画不同场景下的通信条件。在此基础上，我们将其作为学习先验，用于区分特定场景下的有损与无损消息。此外，借鉴双互信息估计器，我们解耦了有损与无损消息对分布式决策的影响，并引入了一个通信约束的多智能体强化学习框架，将通信消息的影响量化为全局奖励。最后，我们在多个通信约束基准测试中验证了所提方法的有效性。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the prevalence of lossy communication in real-world multi-agent systems and the limitations of existing methods in scalability and robustness, this paper proposes a generalized communication-constrained model to characterize various communication conditions as a learning prior. The method decouples the impact of lossy and lossless messages on decision-making using a dual mutual information estimator and integrates communication effects into a reinforcement learning framework via global reward quantification. Experimental validation across several benchmarks demonstrates the approach's effectiveness in handling communication-constrained environments.
针对现实多智能体系统中普遍存在的通信损耗问题，以及现有方法在可扩展性和鲁棒性上的不足，本文提出了一种广义通信约束模型，将不同场景的通信条件统一表征为学习先验。该方法利用双重互信息估计器解耦损耗与无损消息对分布式决策的影响，并通过全局奖励量化将通信影响引入强化学习框架。在多个通信约束基准测试上的实验验证了该方法的有效性。
Enhancing Heterogeneous Multi-Agent Cooperation in Decentralized MARL via GNN-driven Intrinsic Rewards
Authors: Jahir Sadik Monon, Deeparghya Dutta Barua, Md. Mosaddek Khan
Venue: Proceedings of the 24th International Conference on Autonomous Agents and Multiagent Systems (AAMAS 2025), pages 2681-2683, 2025
First: 2024-08-12T21:38:40+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-10T06:34:04+00:00
Comments: Full paper version for AAMAS 2025, 9 pages, 5 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Multi-agent Reinforcement Learning (MARL) is emerging as a key framework for various sequential decision-making and control tasks. Unlike their single-agent counterparts, multi-agent systems necessitate successful cooperation among the agents. The deployment of these systems in real-world scenarios often requires decentralized training, a diverse set of agents, and learning from infrequent environmental reward signals. These challenges become more pronounced under partial observability and the lack of prior knowledge about agent heterogeneity. While notable studies use intrinsic motivation (IM) to address reward sparsity or cooperation in decentralized settings, those dealing with heterogeneity typically assume centralized training, parameter sharing, and agent indexing. To overcome these limitations, we propose the CoHet algorithm, which utilizes a novel Graph Neural Network (GNN) based intrinsic motivation to facilitate the learning of heterogeneous agent policies in decentralized settings, under the challenges of partial observability and reward sparsity. Evaluation of CoHet in the Multi-agent Particle Environment (MPE) and Vectorized Multi-Agent Simulator (VMAS) benchmarks demonstrates superior performance compared to the state-of-the-art in a range of cooperative multi-agent scenarios. Our research is supplemented by an analysis of the impact of the agent dynamics model on the intrinsic motivation module, insights into the performance of different CoHet variants, and its robustness to an increasing number of heterogeneous agents.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于图神经网络内在奖励增强去中心化多智能体强化学习中的异构协作
多智能体强化学习（MARL）正成为各类序贯决策与控制任务的关键框架。与单智能体系统不同，多智能体系统需要实现智能体间的有效协作。在实际场景中部署这类系统通常需要去中心化训练、多样化的智能体配置，以及从稀疏环境奖励信号中学习的能力。在部分可观测且缺乏智能体异构先验知识的条件下，这些挑战尤为突出。现有研究虽利用内在动机（IM）解决去中心化场景中的奖励稀疏或协作问题，但涉及异构性的研究多假设集中式训练、参数共享和智能体索引。为突破这些限制，我们提出CoHet算法，该算法采用基于图神经网络（GNN）的新型内在激励机制，在部分可观测和奖励稀疏的挑战下，促进去中心化环境中异构智能体策略的学习。在多智能体粒子环境（MPE）和向量化多智能体模拟器（VMAS）基准测试中，CoHet在一系列协作多智能体场景中展现出优于现有技术的性能。本研究进一步分析了智能体动力学模型对内在激励模块的影响，探讨了不同CoHet变体的性能表现，并验证了其对异构智能体数量增加的鲁棒性。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the challenge of fostering cooperation among heterogeneous agents in decentralized multi-agent reinforcement learning (MARL) under conditions of partial observability and sparse environmental rewards. The proposed method, CoHet, introduces a novel intrinsic motivation mechanism driven by a Graph Neural Network (GNN) to guide the learning of distinct agent policies without relying on centralized training, parameter sharing, or agent indexing. Experimental results on MPE and VMAS benchmarks show that CoHet outperforms state-of-the-art methods across various cooperative scenarios, with additional analyses demonstrating its robustness to an increasing number of heterogeneous agents and providing insights into the role of the agent dynamics model.
本文旨在解决在部分可观测性和稀疏环境奖励条件下，去中心化多智能体强化学习中异构智能体间的协作难题。所提出的CoHet方法引入了一种由图神经网络驱动的新型内在激励机制，以指导不同智能体策略的学习，且无需依赖集中式训练、参数共享或智能体索引。在MPE和VMAS基准测试上的实验结果表明，CoHet在各种合作场景中优于现有先进方法；进一步分析还证明了其对异构智能体数量增加的鲁棒性，并揭示了智能体动力学模型对内在激励模块的影响。
Social-R1: Towards Human-like Social Reasoning in LLMs
Authors: Jincenzi Wu, Yuxuan Lei, Jianxun Lian, Yitian Huang, Lexin Zhou, Haotian Li, Xing Xie, Helen Meng
First: 2026-03-10T06:26:24+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-10T06:26:24+00:00
Comments: 27 pages. Code and dataset will be released upon acceptance
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
While large language models demonstrate remarkable capabilities across numerous domains, social intelligence - the capacity to perceive social cues, infer mental states, and generate appropriate responses - remains a critical challenge, particularly for enabling effective human-AI collaboration and developing AI that truly serves human needs. Current models often rely on superficial patterns rather than genuine social reasoning. We argue that cultivating human-like social intelligence requires training with challenging cases that resist shortcut solutions. To this end, we introduce ToMBench-Hard, an adversarial benchmark designed to provide hard training examples for social reasoning. Building on this, we propose Social-R1, a reinforcement learning framework that aligns model reasoning with human cognition through multi-dimensional rewards. Unlike outcome-based RL, Social-R1 supervises the entire reasoning process, enforcing structural alignment, logical integrity, and information density. Results show that our approach enables a 4B parameter model to surpass much larger counterparts and generalize robustly across eight diverse benchmarks. These findings demonstrate that challenging training cases with trajectory-level alignment offer a path toward efficient and reliable social intelligence.
中文标题/摘要
标题：Social-R1：迈向大语言模型中类人化的社会推理能力
尽管大语言模型在众多领域展现出卓越能力，但社会智能——即感知社交线索、推断心理状态并生成恰当回应的能力——仍是关键挑战，尤其对于实现有效人机协作和开发真正服务人类需求的AI而言。当前模型常依赖表层模式而非真正的社会推理。我们认为，培养类人化的社会智能需要通过抵抗捷径解决方案的挑战性案例进行训练。为此，我们推出ToMBench-Hard对抗性基准，旨在为社会推理提供高难度训练样本。在此基础上，我们提出Social-R1强化学习框架，通过多维奖励使模型推理与人类认知对齐。区别于基于结果的强化学习，Social-R1监督整个推理过程，强化结构对齐、逻辑完整性与信息密度。实验表明，该方法使40亿参数模型超越规模更大的模型，并在八个多样化基准测试中实现稳健泛化。这些发现证明，结合轨迹级对齐的挑战性训练案例，为构建高效可靠的社会智能提供了可行路径。

Motivated by the need to enhance social intelligence in large language models for better human-AI collaboration, this paper addresses the limitation of models relying on superficial patterns rather than genuine social reasoning. The method introduces ToMBench-Hard, an adversarial benchmark for hard training examples, and Social-R1, a reinforcement learning framework that aligns model reasoning with human cognition through multi-dimensional rewards supervising the entire reasoning process. Experimental results show that a 4B parameter model trained with this approach surpasses larger counterparts and generalizes robustly across eight diverse benchmarks, demonstrating efficient and reliable social intelligence.
本文旨在提升大语言模型的社会智能以促进人机协作，针对当前模型依赖表面模式而非真正社会推理的问题。方法上，提出了用于困难训练样本的对抗性基准ToMBench-Hard，以及Social-R1强化学习框架，该框架通过多维奖励监督整个推理过程，使模型推理与人类认知对齐。实验结果表明，采用此方法训练的40亿参数模型超越了更大规模的模型，并在八个多样化基准上展现出鲁棒的泛化能力，证明了通过挑战性训练案例和轨迹级对齐可实现高效可靠的社会智能。
From Self-Evolving Synthetic Data to Verifiable-Reward RL: Post-Training Multi-turn Interactive Tool-Using Agents
Authors: Jiaxuan Gao, Jiaao Chen, Chuyi He, Shusheng Xu, Di Jin, Yi Wu
Venue: ICML 2026
First: 2026-01-30T06:01:23+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-10T06:07:37+00:00
Comments: Submitted to ICML 2026
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Interactive tool-using agents must solve real-world tasks via multi-turn interaction with both humans and external environments, requiring dialogue state tracking, multi-step tool execution, while following complex instructions. Post-training such agents is challenging because synthesis for high-quality multi-turn tool-use data is difficult to scale, and reinforcement learning (RL) could face noisy signals caused by user simulation, leading to degraded training efficiency. We propose a unified framework that combines a self-evolving data agent with verifier-based RL. Our system, EigenData, is a hierarchical multi-agent engine that synthesizes tool-grounded dialogues together with executable per-instance checkers, and improves generation reliability via closed-loop self-evolving process that updates prompts and workflow. Building on the synthetic data, we develop an RL recipe that first fine-tunes the user model and then applies GRPO-style training with trajectory-level group-relative advantages and dynamic filtering, yielding consistent improvements beyond SFT. Evaluated on tau^2-bench, our best model reaches 73.0% pass^1 on Airline and 98.3% pass^1 on Telecom, matching or exceeding frontier models. Overall, our results suggest a scalable pathway for bootstrapping complex tool-using behaviors without expensive human annotation.
中文标题/摘要
标题：从自演进合成数据到可验证奖励强化学习：后训练多轮交互式工具使用智能体
交互式工具使用智能体需通过与人及外部环境的多轮交互解决现实任务，要求具备对话状态追踪、多步骤工具执行及复杂指令遵循能力。此类智能体的后训练面临挑战：高质量多轮工具使用数据的合成难以规模化，强化学习可能因用户模拟产生的噪声信号而降低训练效率。本文提出融合自演进数据智能体与验证器强化学习的统一框架。我们的EigenData系统采用分层多智能体引擎，可合成工具锚定对话及可执行的实例级检查器，并通过更新提示词与工作流的闭环自演进过程提升生成可靠性。基于合成数据，我们开发了一种强化学习方案：先微调用户模型，再采用基于轨迹级组间相对优势与动态筛选的GRPO式训练，实现了超越监督微调的持续改进。在tau^2-bench评估中，最佳模型在Airline任务达到73.0% pass^1，Telecom任务达到98.3% pass^1，匹配或超越前沿模型。总体而言，本研究为无需昂贵人工标注即可引导复杂工具使用行为提供了可扩展路径。

The paper addresses the challenge of post-training multi-turn interactive tool-using agents, where scaling high-quality synthetic dialogue data and mitigating noisy reinforcement learning signals from user simulations are key obstacles. The authors propose a unified framework called EigenData, which combines a self-evolving hierarchical multi-agent system to synthesize tool-grounded dialogues with executable per-instance checkers, improving reliability through closed-loop prompt and workflow updates, and a verifier-based RL method that fine-tunes the user model before applying GRPO-style training with trajectory-level advantages and dynamic filtering. Experimental results on the tau^2-bench show that the best model achieves 73.0% pass^1 on Airline and 98.3% pass^1 on Telecom, matching or surpassing frontier models, indicating a scalable approach to bootstrapping complex tool-using behaviors without costly human annotation.
本文针对多轮交互式工具使用智能体的后训练挑战，其核心困难在于难以扩展高质量合成对话数据，且强化学习易受用户模拟产生的噪声信号影响导致训练效率下降。作者提出一个统一框架EigenData，结合了自演化的分层多智能体系统来合成工具接地的对话及可执行的实例检查器，通过闭环自演化过程更新提示和工作流以提高生成可靠性，以及一种基于验证器的强化学习方法，先微调用户模型再采用GRPO风格训练，利用轨迹级组相对优势和动态过滤。在tau^2-bench上的实验结果表明，最佳模型在Airline任务上达到73.0% pass^1，在Telecom任务上达到98.3% pass^1，匹配或超越了前沿模型，这为无需昂贵人工标注即可引导复杂工具使用行为提供了一条可扩展的路径。
Beyond Test-Time Training: Learning to Reason via Hardware-Efficient Optimal Control
Authors: Peihao Wang, Shan Yang, Xijun Wang, Tesi Xiao, Xin Liu, Changlong Yu, Yu Lou, Pan Li, Zhangyang Wang, Ming Lin, René Vidal
First: 2026-03-10T05:42:13+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-10T05:42:13+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Associative memory has long underpinned the design of sequential models. Beyond recall, humans reason by projecting future states and selecting goal-directed actions, a capability that modern language models increasingly require but do not natively encode. While prior work uses reinforcement learning or test-time training, planning remains external to the model architecture. We formulate reasoning as optimal control and introduce the Test-Time Control (TTC) layer, which performs finite-horizon LQR planning over latent states at inference time, represents a value function within neural architectures, and leverages it as the nested objective to enable planning before prediction. To ensure scalability, we derive a hardware-efficient LQR solver based on a symplectic formulation and implement it as a fused CUDA kernel, enabling parallel execution with minimal overhead. Integrated as an adapter into pretrained LLMs, TTC layers improve mathematical reasoning performance by up to +27.8% on MATH-500 and 2-3x Pass@8 improvements on AMC and AIME, demonstrating that embedding optimal control as an architectural component provides an effective and scalable mechanism for reasoning beyond test-time training.

标题：超越测试时训练：通过硬件高效最优控制实现推理学习
关联记忆长期支撑着序列模型的设计。除了记忆回溯，人类通过预测未来状态并选择目标导向的行为进行推理，这种能力对现代语言模型日益重要，却未被原生编码。现有研究虽采用强化学习或测试时训练，但规划仍外置于模型架构。我们将推理形式化为最优控制问题，提出测试时控制层：该层在推理时对隐状态执行有限时域LQR规划，在神经架构内部表征价值函数，并将其作为嵌套目标实现预测前的规划。为确保可扩展性，我们基于辛几何推导硬件高效的LQR求解器，实现为融合CUDA内核，支持并行执行且开销极小。作为适配器集成至预训练大语言模型后，TTC层将MATH-500数学推理性能提升最高27.8%，在AMC和AIME基准上实现2-3倍Pass@8提升，证明将最优控制嵌入架构组件可为超越测试时训练的推理提供高效可扩展机制。
Summary / 总结
Motivated by the need for language models to perform goal-directed reasoning akin to human projection and action selection, which is not natively supported, this paper introduces Test-Time Control (TTC) layers that embed optimal control directly into model architecture. The method formulates reasoning as optimal control, implementing a hardware-efficient LQR solver via a symplectic formulation and a fused CUDA kernel for scalable, low-overhead planning over latent states at inference time. Reinforcement Learning for Self-Improving Agent with Skill Library
Authors: Jiongxiao Wang, Qiaojing Yan, Yawei Wang, Yijun Tian, Soumya Smruti Mishra, Zhichao Xu, Megha Gandhi, Panpan Xu, Lin Lee Cheong
First: 2025-12-18T21:58:19+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-10T05:40:56+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large Language Model (LLM)-based agents have demonstrated remarkable capabilities in complex reasoning and multi-turn interactions but struggle to continuously improve and adapt when deployed in new environments. One promising approach is implementing skill libraries that allow agents to learn, validate, and apply new skills. However, current skill library approaches rely primarily on LLM prompting, making consistent skill library implementation challenging. To overcome these challenges, we propose a Reinforcement Learning (RL)-based approach to enhance agents' self-improvement capabilities with a skill library. Specifically, we introduce Skill Augmented GRPO for self-Evolution (SAGE), a novel RL framework that systematically incorporates skills into learning. The framework's key component, Sequential Rollout, iteratively deploys agents across a chain of similar tasks for each rollout. As agents navigate through the task chain, skills generated from previous tasks accumulate in the library and become available for subsequent tasks. Additionally, the framework enhances skill generation and utilization through a Skill-integrated Reward that complements the original outcome-based rewards. Experimental results on AppWorld demonstrate that SAGE, when applied to supervised-finetuned model with expert experience, achieves 8.9% higher Scenario Goal Completion while requiring 26% fewer interaction steps and generating 59% fewer tokens, substantially outperforming existing approaches in both accuracy and efficiency.

标题：基于技能库的强化学习自进化智能体
基于大语言模型（LLM）的智能体在复杂推理与多轮交互中展现出卓越能力，但在新部署环境中难以持续改进与适应。构建技能库使智能体能够学习、验证并应用新技能是一种前景广阔的方法，但现有技能库方案主要依赖LLM提示，难以实现稳定的技能库构建。为突破这些局限，我们提出一种基于强化学习（RL）的方法，通过技能库增强智能体的自进化能力。具体而言，我们设计了用于自进化的技能增强GRPO框架（SAGE），这是一种将技能系统化融入学习过程的新型RL框架。该框架的核心组件——序列化部署机制——在每次训练迭代中让智能体在相似任务链上连续执行。随着智能体在任务链中推进，先前任务生成的技能将积累至技能库，供后续任务调用。此外，框架通过融合技能奖励机制对原有结果导向型奖励进行补充，从而提升技能生成与利用效率。在AppWorld环境中的实验表明：将SAGE应用于经专家经验监督微调的模型后，场景目标完成率提升8.9%，交互步骤减少26%，生成令牌数降低59%，在准确性与效率上均显著超越现有方法。

The proposed method, SAGE, is a reinforcement learning framework that integrates a skill library through Sequential Rollout, where agents iteratively tackle chains of similar tasks to accumulate and reuse skills, and employs a Skill-integrated Reward to enhance skill generation and utilization. Experimental results on AppWorld show that SAGE applied to a supervised-finetuned model with expert experience achieves 8.9% higher Scenario Goal Completion, requires 26% fewer interaction steps, and generates 59% fewer tokens, outperforming existing methods in both accuracy and efficiency.

Embodied Human Simulation for Quantitative Design and Analysis of Interactive Robotics
Authors: Chenhui Zuo, Jinhao Xu, Michael Qian Vergnolle, Yanan Sui
First: 2026-03-10T05:39:31+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-10T05:39:31+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Physical interactive robotics, ranging from wearable devices to collaborative humanoid robots, require close coordination between mechanical design and control. However, evaluating interactive dynamics is challenging due to complex human biomechanics and motor responses. Traditional experiments rely on indirect metrics without measuring human internal states, such as muscle forces or joint loads. To address this issue, we develop a scalable simulation-based framework for the quantitative analysis of physical human-robot interaction. At its core is a full-body musculoskeletal model serving as a predictive surrogate for the human dynamical system. Driven by a reinforcement learning controller, it generates adaptive, physiologically grounded motor behaviors. We employ a sequential training pipeline where the pre-trained human motion control policy acts as a consistent evaluator, making large-scale design space exploration computationally tractable. By simulating the coupled human-robot system, the framework provides access to internal biomechanical metrics, offering a systematic way to concurrently co-optimize a robot's structural parameters and control policy. We demonstrate its capability in optimizing human-exoskeleton interactions, showing improved joint alignment and reduced contact forces. This work establishes embodied human simulation as a scalable paradigm for interactive robotics design.

标题：具身化人体仿真用于交互式机器人定量设计与分析

Multimodal LLM-assisted Evolutionary Search for Programmatic Control Policies
Authors: Qinglong Hu, Xialiang Tong, Mingxuan Yuan, Fei Liu, Zhichao Lu, Qingfu Zhang
First: 2025-08-07T14:24:03+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-10T05:39:00+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Deep reinforcement learning has achieved impressive success in control tasks. However, its policies, represented as opaque neural networks, are often difficult for humans to understand, verify, and debug, which undermines trust and hinders real-world deployment. This work addresses this challenge by introducing a novel approach for programmatic control policy discovery, called Multimodal Large Language Model-assisted Evolutionary Search (MLES). MLES utilizes multimodal large language models as programmatic policy generators, combining them with evolutionary search to automate policy generation. It integrates visual feedback-driven behavior analysis within the policy generation process to identify failure patterns and guide targeted improvements, thereby enhancing policy discovery efficiency and producing adaptable, human-aligned policies. Experimental results demonstrate that MLES achieves performance comparable to Proximal Policy Optimization (PPO) across two standard control tasks while providing transparent control logic and traceable design processes. This approach also overcomes the limitations of predefined domain-specific languages, facilitates knowledge transfer and reuse, and is scalable across various tasks, showing promise as a new paradigm for developing transparent and verifiable control policies. Code is publicly available at https://github.com/QingL2000/MLES.

标题：多模态大语言模型辅助的进化搜索用于程序化控制策略

Strategically Robust Multi-Agent Reinforcement Learning with Linear Function Approximation
Authors: Jake Gonzales, Max Horwitz, Eric Mazumdar, Lillian J. Ratliff
First: 2026-03-10T05:24:10+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-10T05:24:10+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Provably efficient and robust equilibrium computation in general-sum Markov games remains a core challenge in multi-agent reinforcement learning. Nash equilibrium is computationally intractable in general and brittle due to equilibrium multiplicity and sensitivity to approximation error. We study Risk-Sensitive Quantal Response Equilibrium (RQRE), which yields a unique, smooth solution under bounded rationality and risk sensitivity. We propose \texttt{RQRE-OVI}, an optimistic value iteration algorithm for computing RQRE with linear function approximation in large or continuous state spaces. Through finite-sample regret analysis, we establish convergence and explicitly characterize how sample complexity scales with rationality and risk-sensitivity parameters. The regret bounds reveal a quantitative tradeoff: increasing rationality tightens regret, while risk sensitivity induces regularization that enhances stability and robustness. This exposes a Pareto frontier between expected performance and robustness, with Nash recovered in the limit of perfect rationality and risk neutrality. We further show that the RQRE policy map is Lipschitz continuous in estimated payoffs, unlike Nash, and RQRE admits a distributionally robust optimization interpretation. Empirically, we demonstrate that \texttt{RQRE-OVI} achieves competitive performance under self-play while producing substantially more robust behavior under cross-play compared to Nash-based approaches. These results suggest \texttt{RQRE-OVI} offers a principled, scalable, and tunable path for equilibrium learning with improved robustness and generalization.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于线性函数逼近的策略鲁棒多智能体强化学习
在一般和马尔可夫博弈中实现可证明高效且鲁棒的均衡计算，仍是多智能体强化学习的核心挑战。纳什均衡在计算上通常难以处理，且因均衡多重性及对近似误差的敏感性而显得脆弱。本研究探讨风险敏感量化响应均衡（RQRE），该均衡在有限理性和风险敏感性条件下可产生唯一平滑解。我们提出\texttt{RQRE-OVI}算法——一种采用线性函数逼近、适用于大规模或连续状态空间的乐观值迭代算法，用于计算RQRE。通过有限样本遗憾分析，我们证明了算法的收敛性，并明确刻画了样本复杂度随理性度与风险敏感度参数的缩放规律。遗憾界揭示了一种定量权衡：提高理性度可收紧遗憾界，而风险敏感性则产生正则化效应，增强稳定性和鲁棒性。这展现了期望性能与鲁棒性之间的帕累托前沿，且在完全理性与风险中性的极限情况下可恢复纳什均衡。我们进一步证明，与纳什均衡不同，RQRE策略映射在估计收益上具有利普希茨连续性，且RQRE可解释为分布鲁棒优化问题。实证结果表明，\texttt{RQRE-OVI}在自对弈中取得竞争性性能，且在交叉对弈中相比基于纳什均衡的方法产生显著更鲁棒的行为。这些发现表明，\texttt{RQRE-OVI}为均衡学习提供了一条具有原则性、可扩展性及可调性的路径，在鲁棒性与泛化能力方面均获得提升。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the computational intractability and brittleness of Nash equilibrium in general-sum Markov games by proposing a novel equilibrium concept, Risk-Sensitive Quantal Response Equilibrium (RQRE), which ensures uniqueness and smoothness through bounded rationality and risk sensitivity. The authors introduce RQRE-OVI, an optimistic value iteration algorithm with linear function approximation for large-scale settings, and provide finite-sample regret bounds that quantify a tradeoff: higher rationality reduces regret, while risk sensitivity acts as a regularizer to enhance stability and robustness, recovering Nash equilibrium as a limiting case. Empirical results show that RQRE-OVI achieves competitive performance in self-play and significantly greater robustness in cross-play compared to Nash-based methods, offering a scalable and tunable approach for robust multi-agent reinforcement learning.
本文针对一般和马尔可夫博弈中纳什均衡计算难解性和脆弱性问题，提出了一种新的均衡概念——风险敏感量化响应均衡（RQRE），它通过有限理性和风险敏感性保证了唯一性和平滑性。作者设计了RQRE-OVI算法，这是一种采用线性函数近似的乐观值迭代方法，适用于大规模或连续状态空间，并通过有限样本遗憾分析建立了收敛性，明确了样本复杂度与理性和风险敏感参数的关系。实验结果表明，RQRE-OVI在自对弈中表现优异，且在交叉对弈中比基于纳什的方法具有显著更强的鲁棒性，为多智能体强化学习提供了一条可扩展、可调节的鲁棒均衡学习路径。
Evaluate-as-Action: Self-Evaluated Process Rewards for Retrieval-Augmented Agents
Authors: Jiangming Shu, Yuxiang Zhang, Ye Ma, Xueyuan Lin, Jitao Sang
First: 2026-03-10T05:22:40+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-10T05:22:40+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Retrieval-augmented agents can query external evidence, yet their reliability in multi-step reasoning remains limited: noisy retrieval may derail multi-hop question answering, while outcome-only reinforcement learning provides credit signals that are too coarse to optimize intermediate steps. We propose \textsc{EvalAct} (Evaluate-as-Action), which converts implicit retrieval quality assessment into an explicit action and enforces a coupled Search-to-Evaluate protocol so that each retrieval is immediately followed by a structured evaluation score, yielding process signals aligned with the interaction trajectory. To leverage these signals, we introduce Process-Calibrated Advantage Rescaling (PCAR), a GRPO-based optimization method that rescales advantages at the segment level according to evaluation scores, emphasizing reliable segments while updating uncertain ones conservatively. Experiments on seven open-domain QA benchmarks show that \textsc{EvalAct} achieves the best average accuracy, with the largest gains on multi-hop tasks, and ablations verify that the explicit evaluation loop drives the primary improvements while PCAR provides consistent additional benefits.
中文标题/摘要
标题：评估即行动：检索增强智能体的自评估过程奖励机制
检索增强智能体虽能查询外部证据，但其在多步推理中的可靠性仍受限：噪声检索可能干扰多跳问答，而仅基于结果的强化学习提供的奖励信号过于粗略，难以优化中间步骤。我们提出EvalAct（评估即行动）方法，将隐式的检索质量评估转化为显式动作，并强制执行耦合的“检索-评估”协议，使每次检索后立即生成结构化评估分数，从而产生与交互轨迹对齐的过程信号。为利用这些信号，我们提出过程校准优势重缩放（PCAR）——一种基于GRPO的优化方法，根据评估分数在片段层级重缩放优势值，强调可靠片段的同时保守更新不确定片段。在七个开放域QA基准测试中，EvalAct取得了最佳平均准确率，其中多跳任务提升最为显著。消融实验验证：显式评估循环是主要改进来源，而PCAR能持续提供额外增益。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the challenge of improving the reliability of retrieval-augmented agents in multi-step reasoning, where noisy retrieval can disrupt multi-hop question answering and outcome-only reinforcement learning offers overly coarse credit signals. The proposed method, EvalAct, transforms implicit retrieval quality assessment into an explicit action by enforcing a Search-to-Evaluate protocol, where each retrieval is immediately followed by a structured evaluation score to provide process signals aligned with the interaction trajectory. To utilize these signals, the authors introduce Process-Calibrated Advantage Rescaling (PCAR), a GRPO-based optimization technique that rescales advantages at the segment level based on evaluation scores, emphasizing reliable segments while updating uncertain ones conservatively. Experimental results on seven open-domain QA benchmarks demonstrate that EvalAct achieves the highest average accuracy, with the most significant gains on multi-hop tasks, and ablations confirm that the explicit evaluation loop drives primary improvements while PCAR consistently adds further benefits.
本文旨在解决检索增强代理在多步推理中可靠性不足的问题，其中噪声检索可能干扰多跳问答，而仅基于结果的强化学习提供的奖励信号过于粗糙。提出的方法EvalAct将隐式的检索质量评估转化为显式动作，通过强制实施搜索到评估协议，使每次检索后立即生成结构化评估分数，从而提供与交互轨迹对齐的过程信号。为利用这些信号，作者引入了过程校准优势重缩放（PCAR），这是一种基于GRPO的优化方法，根据评估分数在片段级别重缩放优势，强调可靠片段同时保守更新不确定部分。在七个开放域问答基准上的实验表明，EvalAct实现了最佳平均准确率，在多跳任务上提升最大，消融研究验证了显式评估循环是主要改进来源，而PCAR则持续提供额外增益。
Non-Rectangular Average-Reward Robust MDPs: Optimal Policies and Their Transient Values
Authors: Shengbo Wang, Nian Si
First: 2026-03-01T06:29:34+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-10T05:02:02+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We study non-rectangular robust Markov decision processes under the average-reward criterion, where the ambiguity set couples transition probabilities across states and the adversary commits to a stationary kernel for the entire horizon. We show that any history-dependent policy achieving sublinear expected regret uniformly over the ambiguity set is robust-optimal, and that the robust value admits a minimax representation as the infimum over the ambiguity set of the classical optimal gains, without requiring any form of rectangularity or robust dynamic programming principle. Under the weak communication assumption, we establish the existence of such policies by converting high-probability regret bounds from the average-reward reinforcement learning literature into the expected-regret criterion. We then introduce a transient-value framework to evaluate finite-time performance of robust optimal policies, proving that average-reward optimality alone can mask arbitrarily poor transients and deriving regret-based lower bounds on transient values. Finally, we construct an epoch-based policy that combines an optimal stationary policy for the worst-case model with an anytime-valid sequential test and an online learning fallback, achieving a constant-order transient value.
中文标题/摘要
标题：非矩形平均奖励鲁棒马尔可夫决策过程：最优策略及其瞬态值
我们研究了平均奖励准则下的非矩形鲁棒马尔可夫决策过程，其中模糊集耦合了状态间的转移概率，且对手在整个时域内承诺使用固定核。我们证明，任何在模糊集上一致实现次线性期望遗憾的历史依赖策略都是鲁棒最优的，且鲁棒值可表示为经典最优增益在模糊集上的极小极大表示，无需任何形式的矩形性或鲁棒动态规划原理。在弱通信假设下，通过将平均奖励强化学习文献中的高概率遗憾界转化为期望遗憾准则，我们证明了此类策略的存在性。随后，我们引入瞬态值框架来评估鲁棒最优策略的有限时间性能，证明仅平均奖励最优性可能掩盖任意差的瞬态表现，并基于遗憾推导瞬态值的下界。最后，我们构建了一种基于周期的策略，该策略结合了最坏情况模型的最优固定策略、任意时间有效的序贯检验以及在线学习回退机制，实现了常数阶瞬态值。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses non-rectangular robust Markov decision processes under average-reward criteria, motivated by the need to handle ambiguity sets that couple transition probabilities across states without relying on rectangularity assumptions. The method establishes that any history-dependent policy achieving sublinear expected regret uniformly over the ambiguity set is robust-optimal, and it proves the robust value can be represented as a minimax infimum over classical optimal gains. Experimental results show that under weak communication assumptions, such policies exist via conversion from high-probability regret bounds, and a transient-value framework reveals average-reward optimality can mask poor finite-time performance; an epoch-based policy combining worst-case stationary policies with sequential tests and online learning fallbacks achieves constant-order transient values.
本文研究了平均奖励准则下的非矩形鲁棒马尔可夫决策过程，其动机在于处理跨状态耦合转移概率的模糊集，而无需依赖矩形性假设。方法上证明了任何在模糊集上一致实现次线性期望后悔的历史依赖策略都是鲁棒最优的，且鲁棒值可表示为经典最优增益的极小极大下确界。实验结果表明，在弱通信假设下，通过将高概率后悔界转换为期望后悔准则，此类策略存在；瞬态值框架揭示了平均奖励最优性可能掩盖较差的有限时间性能，而一种结合最坏情形平稳策略、随时有效序列检验和在线学习回退机制的基于周期的策略实现了常数阶瞬态值。
Improving Search Agent with One Line of Code
Authors: Jian Li, Dongsheng Chen, Zhenhua Xu, Yizhang Jin, Jiafu Wu, Chengjie Wang, Xiaotong Yuan, Yabiao Wang
First: 2026-03-10T04:07:39+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-10T04:07:39+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Tool-based Agentic Reinforcement Learning (TARL) has emerged as a promising paradigm for training search agents to interact with external tools for a multi-turn information-seeking process autonomously. However, we identify a critical training instability that leads to catastrophic model collapse: Importance Sampling Distribution Drift(ISDD). In Group Relative Policy Optimization(GRPO), a widely adopted TARL algorithm, ISDD manifests as a precipitous decline in the importance sampling ratios, which nullifies gradient updates and triggers irreversible training failure. To address this, we propose \textbf{S}earch \textbf{A}gent \textbf{P}olicy \textbf{O}ptimization (\textbf{SAPO}), which stabilizes training via a conditional token-level KL constraint. Unlike hard clipping, which ignores distributional divergence, SAPO selectively penalizes the KL divergence between the current and old policies. Crucially, this penalty is applied only to positive tokens with low probabilities where the policy has shifted excessively, thereby preventing distribution drift while preserving gradient flow. Remarkably, SAPO requires only one-line code modification to standard GRPO, ensuring immediate deployability. Extensive experiments across seven QA benchmarks demonstrate that SAPO achieves \textbf{+10.6\% absolute improvement} (+31.5\% relative) over Search-R1, yielding consistent gains across varying model scales (1.5B, 14B) and families (Qwen, LLaMA).
中文标题/摘要
标题：一行代码改进搜索智能体
基于工具的智能体强化学习（TARL）已成为训练搜索智能体自主进行多轮信息检索过程的有前景范式。然而，我们发现一种导致灾难性模型崩溃的关键训练不稳定性：重要性采样分布漂移（ISDD）。在广泛采用的TARL算法——组相对策略优化（GRPO）中，ISDD表现为重要性采样比率急剧下降，导致梯度更新失效并引发不可逆的训练失败。为此，我们提出搜索智能体策略优化（SAPO），通过条件化词元级KL约束来稳定训练。与忽略分布差异的硬截断不同，SAPO选择性地惩罚当前策略与旧策略之间的KL散度。关键在于，该惩罚仅应用于概率较低且策略偏移过度的正向词元，从而在保持梯度流动的同时防止分布漂移。值得注意的是，SAPO仅需对标准GRPO进行单行代码修改，确保即时可部署性。在七个问答基准上的大量实验表明，SAPO相比Search-R1实现了绝对提升10.6%（相对提升31.5%），在不同模型规模（1.5B、14B）和架构系列（Qwen、LLaMA）上均获得稳定增益。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses a critical training instability called Importance Sampling Distribution Drift (ISDD) in Tool-based Agentic Reinforcement Learning (TARL), which causes catastrophic model collapse in search agents by nullifying gradient updates. To stabilize training, the authors propose Search Agent Policy Optimization (SAPO), a method that introduces a conditional token-level KL constraint to selectively penalize excessive policy shifts on low-probability positive tokens, preventing distribution drift while maintaining gradient flow. Experimental results across seven QA benchmarks show that SAPO achieves a +10.6% absolute improvement over baseline methods, with consistent gains across different model scales and families, requiring only a one-line code modification to the standard GRPO algorithm for easy deployment.
本文针对基于工具的智能体强化学习（TARL）中存在的关键训练不稳定性问题，即重要性采样分布漂移（ISDD），该问题会导致搜索智能体因梯度更新失效而发生灾难性模型崩溃。为解决此问题，作者提出了搜索智能体策略优化（SAPO）方法，通过引入条件令牌级KL约束，选择性地对概率较低的正向令牌上策略的过度偏移进行惩罚，从而防止分布漂移同时保持梯度流动。在七个问答基准上的广泛实验表明，SAPO相比基线方法实现了+10.6%的绝对性能提升，且在不同模型规模和系列上均取得一致增益，该方法仅需对标准GRPO算法进行一行代码修改即可部署。
RubiCap: Rubric-Guided Reinforcement Learning for Dense Image Captioning
Authors: Tzu-Heng Huang, Sirajul Salekin, Javier Movellan, Frederic Sala, Manjot Bilkhu
First: 2026-03-10T03:51:27+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-10T03:51:27+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Dense image captioning is critical for cross-modal alignment in vision-language pretraining and text-to-image generation, but scaling expert-quality annotations is prohibitively expensive. While synthetic captioning via strong vision-language models (VLMs) is a practical alternative, supervised distillation often yields limited output diversity and weak generalization. Reinforcement learning (RL) could overcome these limitations, but its successes have so far been concentrated in verifiable domains that rely on deterministic checkers -- a luxury not available in open-ended captioning. We address this bottleneck with RubiCap, a novel RL framework that derives fine-grained, sample-specific reward signals from LLM-written rubrics. RubiCap first assembles a diverse committee of candidate captions, then employs an LLM rubric writer to extract consensus strengths and diagnose deficiencies in the current policy. These insights are converted into explicit evaluation criteria, enabling an LLM judge to decompose holistic quality assessment and replace coarse scalar rewards with structured, multi-faceted evaluations. Across extensive benchmarks, RubiCap achieves the highest win rates on CapArena, outperforming supervised distillation, prior RL methods, human-expert annotations, and GPT-4V-augmented outputs. On CaptionQA, it demonstrates superior word efficiency: our 7B model matches Qwen2.5-VL-32B-Instruct, and our 3B model surpasses its 7B counterpart. Remarkably, using the compact RubiCap-3B as a captioner produces stronger pretrained VLMs than those trained on captions from proprietary models.
中文标题/摘要
标题：RubiCap：基于量规引导的强化学习用于密集图像描述
密集图像描述在视觉-语言预训练与文生图任务中对跨模态对齐至关重要，但规模化获取专家级标注成本极高。虽然通过强视觉-语言模型生成合成描述是可行替代方案，但监督式蒸馏常导致输出多样性受限、泛化能力薄弱。强化学习本可突破这些限制，但其成功目前多集中于依赖确定性验证器的可检验领域——开放式描述任务缺乏此类条件。为此，我们提出RubiCap这一新颖强化学习框架，通过大语言模型编写的评估量规生成细粒度、样本特定的奖励信号。RubiCap首先组建多样化候选描述委员会，随后调用大语言模型量规撰写器提取共识优势并诊断当前策略缺陷，进而转化为显式评估标准，使大语言模型裁判能解构整体质量评估，以结构化多维度评价替代粗糙标量奖励。在广泛基准测试中，RubiCap在CapArena平台取得最高胜率，超越监督蒸馏、先前的强化学习方法、人类专家标注及GPT-4V增强输出。在CaptionQA任务中展现出卓越的词汇效率：我们的70亿参数模型与Qwen2.5-VL-320亿参数指令模型表现相当，而30亿参数模型更超越其70亿参数版本。值得注意的是，使用轻量级RubiCap-3B作为描述生成器训练出的视觉-语言预训练模型，其性能优于基于专有模型描述训练的模型。
Summary / 总结
The paper addresses the challenge of scaling high-quality annotations for dense image captioning, which is crucial for vision-language tasks, by proposing RubiCap, a reinforcement learning framework that overcomes the lack of deterministic reward signals in open-ended captioning. The method employs an LLM to generate fine-grained rubrics that diagnose strengths and weaknesses in candidate captions, converting these insights into structured multi-faceted rewards for policy optimization. Experimental results show that RubiCap achieves the highest win rates on the CapArena benchmark, surpassing supervised distillation, prior RL methods, and human annotations, while also demonstrating superior word efficiency on CaptionQA, with smaller models matching or exceeding larger counterparts, and its captions leading to stronger pretrained vision-language models.
本文针对密集图像描述任务中高质量标注难以扩展的问题，提出了RubiCap框架，该框架通过强化学习解决开放域描述缺乏确定性奖励信号的瓶颈。方法利用大语言模型生成细粒度评分标准，诊断候选描述的优缺点，并将其转化为结构化多维度奖励以优化策略。实验结果表明，RubiCap在CapArena基准上取得了最高的胜率，优于监督蒸馏、先前的强化学习方法及人工标注，同时在CaptionQA上展现出更高的词汇效率，其较小模型能匹配或超越更大模型，且生成的描述能训练出更强大的视觉语言预训练模型。
RL-100: Performant Robotic Manipulation with Real-World Reinforcement Learning
Authors: Kun Lei, Huanyu Li, Dongjie Yu, Zhenyu Wei, Lingxiao Guo, Zhennan Jiang, Ziyu Wang, Shiyu Liang, Huazhe Xu
First: 2025-10-16T16:07:50+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-10T03:25:53+00:00
Comments: https://lei-kun.github.io/RL-100/
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Project1
Abstract
Real-world robotic manipulation in homes and factories demands reliability, efficiency, and robustness that approach or surpass those of skilled human operators. We present RL-100, a real-world reinforcement learning framework built on diffusion visuomotor policies. RL-100 unifies imitation and reinforcement learning under a single clipped PPO surrogate objective applied within the denoising process, yielding conservative and stable improvements across offline and online stages. To meet deployment latency requirements, a lightweight consistency distillation method compresses multi-step diffusion into a one-step controller for high-frequency control. The framework is task-, embodiment-, and representation-agnostic, and supports both single-action and action-chunking control. We evaluate RL-100 on eight diverse real-robot tasks, from dynamic pushing and agile bowling to pouring, cloth folding, unscrewing, multi-stage juicing, and long-horizon box folding. RL-100 attains 100 percent success across evaluated trials, for a total of 1000 out of 1000 episodes, including up to 250 out of 250 consecutive trials on one task. It matches or surpasses expert teleoperators in time to completion. Without retraining, a single policy attains approximately 90 percent zero-shot success under environmental and dynamics shifts, adapts in a few-shot regime to significant task variations (86.7 percent), and remains robust to aggressive human perturbations (about 96 percent). Notably, our juicing robot served random customers continuously for about seven hours without failure when deployed zero-shot in a shopping mall. These results suggest a practical path to deployment-ready robot learning by starting from human priors, aligning training objectives with human-grounded metrics, and reliably extending performance beyond human demonstrations.
中文标题/摘要

家庭与工厂环境中的真实世界机器人操控需要接近或超越熟练人类操作者的可靠性、效率与鲁棒性。我们提出RL-100——一个基于扩散视觉运动策略的真实世界强化学习框架。该框架通过去噪过程中应用的单一截断PPO代理目标，将模仿学习与强化学习统一起来，在离线与在线阶段均实现稳健稳定的性能提升。为满足部署延迟要求，采用轻量级一致性蒸馏方法将多步扩散压缩为单步控制器以实现高频控制。本框架与任务形态、机器人本体及表征方式无关，支持单动作与动作分块控制。我们在八项真实机器人任务中评估RL-100，涵盖动态推物、敏捷保龄球、倾倒液体、布料折叠、拧瓶盖、多步骤榨汁、长时域纸箱折叠等场景。RL-100在全部1000次试验中达成100%成功率，其中单项任务连续250次试验全部成功，完成时间达到或超越专家远程操作员水平。未经重新训练，单一策略在环境与动力学变化下实现约90%零样本成功率，在少量样本条件下适应重大任务变体（86.7%成功率），并对剧烈人为干扰保持强鲁棒性（约96%成功率）。值得注意的是，我们的榨汁机器人在商场零样本部署时，连续为随机顾客服务约七小时无故障。这些结果表明：从人类先验知识出发，使训练目标与人类基准指标对齐，并可靠扩展人类示范之外的性能，可为机器人学习提供切实可行的部署路径。

GameVerse: Can Vision-Language Models Learn from Video-based Reflection?
Authors: Kuan Zhang, Dongchen Liu, Qiyue Zhao, Jinkun Hou, Xinran Zhang, Qinlei Xie, Miao Liu, Yiming Li
First: 2026-03-01T14:29:39+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-10T03:20:19+00:00
Comments: https://gameverse-bench.github.io/
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3 · Project1
Abstract
Human gameplay is a visually grounded interaction loop in which players act, reflect on failures, and watch tutorials to refine strategies. Can Vision-Language Models (VLMs) also learn from video-based reflection? We present GameVerse, a comprehensive video game benchmark that enables a reflective visual interaction loop. Moving beyond traditional fire-and-forget evaluations, it uses a novel reflect-and-retry paradigm to assess how VLMs internalize visual experience and improve policies. To facilitate systematic and scalable evaluation, we also introduce a cognitive hierarchical taxonomy spanning 15 globally popular games, dual action space for both semantic and GUI control, and milestone evaluation using advanced VLMs to quantify progress. Our experiments show that VLMs benefit from video-based reflection in varied settings, and perform best by combining failure trajectories and expert tutorials-a training-free analogue to reinforcement learning (RL) plus supervised fine-tuning (SFT).Our project page is available at https://gameverse-bench.github.io/ . Our code is available at https://github.com/THUSI-Lab/GameVerse .
中文标题/摘要

Experimental results demonstrate that VLMs benefit from reflective loops, with the best performance achieved by combining failure trajectories and expert tutorials, mirroring a training-free analogue to reinforcement learning plus supervised fine-tuning.
