Decoupling Reasoning and Confidence: Resurrecting Calibration in Reinforcement Learning from Verifiable Rewards
Authors: Zhengzhao Ma, Xueru Wen, Boxi Cao, Yaojie Lu, Hongyu Lin, Jinglin Yang, Min He, Xianpei Han, Le Sun
First: 2026-03-10T02:47:59+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-10T02:47:59+00:00
Comments: 9 pages, 8 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Reinforcement Learning from Verifiable Rewards (RLVR) significantly enhances large language models (LLMs) reasoning but severely suffers from calibration degeneration, where models become excessively over-confident in incorrect answers. Previous studies devote to directly incorporating calibration objective into existing optimization target. However, our theoretical analysis demonstrates that there exists a fundamental gradient conflict between the optimization for maximizing policy accuracy and minimizing calibration error. Building on this insight, we propose DCPO, a simple yet effective framework that systematically decouples reasoning and calibration objectives. Extensive experiments demonstrate that our DCPO not only preserves accuracy on par with GRPO but also achieves the best calibration performance and substantially mitigates the over-confidence issue. Our study provides valuable insights and practical solution for more reliable LLM deployment.
中文标题/摘要
标题：解耦推理与置信度：基于可验证奖励的强化学习中校准机制的重建
基于可验证奖励的强化学习（RLVR）显著提升了大语言模型（LLMs）的推理能力，但存在严重的校准退化问题，即模型对错误答案表现出过度自信。先前研究致力于将校准目标直接纳入现有优化框架，然而我们的理论分析表明，最大化策略准确性与最小化校准误差之间存在根本性的梯度冲突。基于这一发现，我们提出了DCPO框架——一种简单而有效的系统性解耦推理与校准目标的方案。大量实验表明，DCPO不仅保持了与GRPO相当的准确率，同时实现了最优的校准性能，并显著缓解了过度自信问题。本研究为构建更可靠的大语言模型部署提供了重要洞见与实践方案。
Summary / 总结
This paper addresses the calibration degeneration problem in Reinforcement Learning from Verifiable Rewards (RLVR), where large language models become overconfident in incorrect answers. The authors identify a fundamental gradient conflict between optimizing for policy accuracy and minimizing calibration error. To resolve this, they propose DCPO, a framework that decouples the reasoning and confidence calibration objectives. Experimental results show that DCPO maintains accuracy comparable to methods like GRPO while achieving superior calibration performance and significantly reducing overconfidence, offering a practical solution for more reliable LLM deployment.
本文针对可验证奖励强化学习中大语言模型对错误答案过度自信的校准退化问题展开研究。作者通过理论分析发现，优化策略准确性与最小化校准误差之间存在根本的梯度冲突。基于此，他们提出了DCPO框架，系统性地解耦了推理与置信度校准目标。大量实验表明，DCPO在保持与GRPO相当准确性的同时，实现了最佳的校准性能，显著缓解了过度自信问题，为更可靠的大语言模型部署提供了有价值的见解和实用解决方案。
AlphaApollo: A System for Deep Agentic Reasoning
Authors: Zhanke Zhou, Chentao Cao, Xiao Feng, Xuan Li, Zongze Li, Xiangyu Lu, Jiangchao Yao, Weikai Huang, Tian Cheng, Jianghangfan Zhang, Tangyu Jiang, Linrui Xu, Yiming Zheng, Brando Miranda, Tongliang Liu, Sanmi Koyejo, Masashi Sugiyama, Bo Han
First: 2025-10-05T15:42:24+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-10T02:38:23+00:00
Comments: Ongoing project
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
We present AlphaApollo, an agentic reasoning system that targets two bottlenecks in foundation-model reasoning: (1) limited reasoning capacity for complex, long-horizon problem solving and (2) unreliable test-time evolution without trustworthy verification. AlphaApollo orchestrates models and tools via three components: (i) multi-turn agentic reasoning, which formalizes model-environment interaction with structured tool calls and responses; (ii) multi-turn agentic learning, which applies turn-level reinforcement learning to optimize tool-use reasoning while decoupling actions from tool responses for stable training; and (iii) multi-round agentic evolution, which refines solutions through a propose-judge-update loop with tool-assisted verifications and long-horizon memory. Across seven math reasoning benchmarks and multiple model scales, AlphaApollo improves performance through reliable tool use (> 85% tool-call success), substantial gains from multi-turn RL (Avg@32: Qwen2.5-1.5B-Instruct 1.07% -> 9.64%, Qwen2.5-7B-Instruct 8.77% -> 20.35%), and improvements from evolution (e.g., Qwen2.5-3B-Instruct 5.27% -> 7.70%, Qwen2.5-14B-Instruct 16.53% -> 21.08%). This project is still ongoing. We welcome feedback from the community and will frequently update the source code and technical report.
中文标题/摘要
标题：AlphaApollo：深度智能体推理系统
本文提出AlphaApollo——一种针对基础模型推理中两大瓶颈的智能体推理系统：（1）复杂长程问题求解的有限推理能力；（2）缺乏可信验证的不可靠测试时演化。该系统通过三大组件协调模型与工具：（i）多轮智能体推理，通过结构化工具调用与响应形式化模型-环境交互；（ii）多轮智能体学习，采用轮次级强化学习优化工具使用推理，同时将动作与工具响应解耦以实现稳定训练；（iii）多轮智能体演化，通过工具辅助验证与长程记忆构成的“提议-评判-更新”循环精化解决方案。在七项数学推理基准及多种模型规模上的实验表明：AlphaApollo通过可靠工具使用（工具调用成功率>85%）、多轮强化学习的显著增益（Avg@32：Qwen2.5-1.5B-Instruct从1.07%提升至9.64%，Qwen2.5-7B-Instruct从8.77%提升至20.35%）以及演化机制改进（如Qwen2.5-3B-Instruct从5.27%提升至7.70%，Qwen2.5-14B-Instruct从16.53%提升至21.08%）有效提升性能。本项目持续进行中，诚邀社区反馈，并将持续更新源代码与技术报告。
Summary / 总结
The paper introduces AlphaApollo, a system designed to overcome two key limitations in foundation-model reasoning: insufficient capacity for complex, long-horizon problem-solving and unreliable test-time evolution lacking trustworthy verification. The method employs a three-component framework: multi-turn agentic reasoning for structured model-environment interaction via tool calls, multi-turn agentic learning using turn-level reinforcement learning to optimize tool-use reasoning while ensuring stable training, and multi-round agentic evolution that refines solutions through a propose-judge-update loop with tool-assisted verification and long-term memory. Experimental results across seven math reasoning benchmarks show significant improvements, including high tool-call success rates over 85%, substantial performance gains from multi-turn RL (e.g., Qwen2.5-7B-Instruct increasing from 8.77% to 20.35%), and further enhancements from the evolution process (e.g., Qwen2.5-14B-Instruct improving from 16.53% to 21.08%).
本文提出了AlphaApollo系统，旨在解决基础模型推理中的两个关键瓶颈：处理复杂、长视野问题的能力有限，以及缺乏可信验证的不可靠测试时演化。该方法采用三组件框架：通过多轮智能体推理实现结构化模型-环境交互与工具调用，利用多轮智能体学习进行轮级强化学习以优化工具使用推理并确保训练稳定性，以及通过多轮智能体演化，借助工具辅助验证和长时记忆的提议-判断-更新循环来精化解决方案。在七个数学推理基准上的实验结果表明，系统取得了显著提升，包括超过85%的高工具调用成功率，多轮强化学习带来的大幅性能增益（例如Qwen2.5-7B-Instruct从8.77%提升至20.35%），以及演化过程的进一步改进（例如Qwen2.5-14B-Instruct从16.53%提升至21.08%）。
Overcoming Valid Action Suppression in Unmasked Policy Gradient Algorithms
Authors: Renos Zabounidis, Roy Siegelmann, Mohamad Qadri, Woojun Kim, Simon Stepputtis, Katia P. Sycara
First: 2026-03-10T02:07:37+00:00 · Latest: 2026-03-10T02:07:37+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
In reinforcement learning environments with state-dependent action validity, action masking consistently outperforms penalty-based handling of invalid actions, yet existing theory only shows that masking preserves the policy gradient theorem. We identify a distinct failure mode of unmasked training: it systematically suppresses valid actions at states the agent has not yet visited. This occurs because gradients pushing down invalid actions at visited states propagate through shared network parameters to unvisited states where those actions are valid. We prove that for softmax policies with shared features, when an action is invalid at visited states but valid at an unvisited state $s^*$, the probability $π(a \mid s^*)$ is bounded by exponential decay due to parameter sharing and the zero-sum identity of softmax logits. This bound reveals that entropy regularization trades off between protecting valid actions and sample efficiency, a tradeoff that masking eliminates. We validate empirically that deep networks exhibit the feature alignment condition required for suppression, and experiments on Craftax, Craftax-Classic, and MiniHack confirm the predicted exponential suppression and demonstrate that feasibility classification enables deployment without oracle masks.
中文标题/摘要
标题：无掩码策略梯度算法中的有效动作抑制问题及其克服
在状态依赖动作有效性的强化学习环境中，动作掩码处理始终优于基于惩罚的无效动作处理方法，但现有理论仅证明掩码保持了策略梯度定理的成立。我们发现无掩码训练存在一种独特的失效模式：它会系统性地抑制智能体尚未访问状态下的有效动作。这是因为在已访问状态中抑制无效动作的梯度会通过共享网络参数传播到未访问状态，而在这些未访问状态中该动作却是有效的。我们证明，对于具有共享特征的softmax策略，当某个动作在已访问状态中无效但在未访问状态$s^*$中有效时，由于参数共享和softmax对数几率的零和特性，其概率$π(a \mid s^*)$会受指数衰减约束。这一界限揭示了熵正则化在保护有效动作与样本效率之间存在权衡，而掩码处理则能消除这种权衡。我们通过实证验证深度网络表现出抑制所需的特征对齐条件，并在Craftax、Craftax-Classic和MiniHack环境中的实验证实了预测的指数抑制现象，同时证明可行性分类技术可实现无需先知掩码的部署。
Summary / 总结
The paper is motivated by the observation that in reinforcement learning with state-dependent action validity, action masking empirically outperforms penalty-based methods, but existing theory only explains that masking preserves the policy gradient theorem. To address this gap, the authors identify a failure mode in unmasked training where valid actions at unvisited states are systematically suppressed due to gradient propagation from visited states where those actions are invalid. The method involves proving that for softmax policies with shared features, the probability of a valid action at an unvisited state decays exponentially under certain conditions, revealing a trade-off between protecting valid actions and sample efficiency with entropy regularization. Experimental results validate that deep networks exhibit the feature alignment required for suppression, and tests on Craftax, Craftax-Classic, and MiniHack confirm exponential suppression while showing that feasibility classification enables deployment without relying on oracle masks.
本文的动机是观察到在具有状态依赖动作有效性的强化学习中，动作掩码在经验上优于基于惩罚的方法，但现有理论仅解释了掩码保持了策略梯度定理。为填补这一空白，作者发现了未掩码训练中的一个失效模式：由于梯度从已访问状态（其中某些动作无效）通过共享网络参数传播，导致在未访问状态中有效的动作被系统性抑制。方法上，作者证明了对于具有共享特征的softmax策略，在特定条件下，未访问状态中有效动作的概率会呈指数衰减，揭示了使用熵正则化时在保护有效动作和样本效率之间的权衡。实验结果验证了深度网络表现出抑制所需的特征对齐条件，并在Craftax、Craftax-Classic和MiniHack上的测试证实了指数抑制，同时表明可行性分类能够实现无需依赖预言掩码的部署。
